Severio Pelagia's House

**Severio Pelagia's House** is a small residence in the Plains District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), between [the Drunken Huntsman](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Drunken_Huntsman "Skyrim:The Drunken Huntsman") and the market stalls.

It is the home of [Severio Pelagia](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia"), the owner of [Pelagia Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagia_Farm "Skyrim:Pelagia Farm").

It contains only one zone, *[Severio Pelagia's House](#Walkthrough)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Severio Pelagia](/wiki/Skyrim:Severio_Pelagia "Skyrim:Severio Pelagia") |

## Walkthrough

Severio Pelagia's House interior

Severio Pelagia's House in ruins

The house is merely used by Severio Pelagia for sleeping, as he tends his farm all day long and spends the evenings at the neighboring tavern. The front door opens to a lit fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), above which hang four bunches of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and a [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"). To the right, a lower wall shelf holds two non-respawning sacks while a higher wall shelf holds another non-respawning sack. To the left, a small table holds a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"). A wall shelf above holds a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") and a bowl containing five [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple").

A few steps lead up to the dinner table which is dressed for four and has an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), an [Eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Left of the dinner table are a set of shelves with a piece of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") and three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of alto wine, and a non-respawning large sack. Next to the shelves are two hanging [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). Across from the shelves is a non-respawning dresser and another bottle of alto wine on top.

A door to the northwest leads into the small bedroom with Severio's owned bed and a non-respawning wardrobe. The room to the northeast has a non-respawning wardrobe, a bowl with a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and a small study with a few books: *[Mysterious Akavir](/wiki/Skyrim:Mysterious_Akavir "Skyrim:Mysterious Akavir")*, *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*, *[The Cabin in the Woods](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cabin_in_the_Woods "Skyrim:The Cabin in the Woods")*, *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")*, and *[Biography of Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v3")*. On the table sits a bottle of Nord mead and a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat").

## Notes

- The front door has a novice lock, the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Severio_Pelagia%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Severio Pelagia's House") to which is carried by Severio Pelagia.
- There is a "Loot" [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") on the top right of the door, marked for very minor loot.
- The house is damaged during the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") and becomes inaccessible afterward.

| # of [Ovens](/wiki/Skyrim:Baking "Skyrim:Baking")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

Shadowfoot Sanctum interior

**Shadowfoot Sanctum** is a small player home located in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). The map marker for the exterior entrance is called **Riften Docks**.

You will be directed to buy the house from [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") for 7,500 gold during the related quest.

The house consists of one area, *[Shadowfoot Sanctum](#Shadowfoot_Sanctum)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.

## Exterior

The Riften Docks entrance

This house possesses two entrances, allowing for easy access to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)") without having to enter Riften itself. The main entrance is located behind a gate in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"), in the room with the executioner's block just across from [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). The second, hidden entrance is an underwater trap door located in the murky pool in the forge area of the sanctum, which leads to a flowing sewer grate outside the walls of Riften. This entrance can be found in the water just south of the western city gates. This Creation adds a new map marker for the Riften Docks which allows for easy access to Shadowfoot Sanctum, as it will place you on the bridge leading to the [Riften Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Warehouse "Skyrim:Riften Warehouse"), conveniently overlooking the sewer grate.

### Shadowfoot Sanctum

Entering from the Ratway, you will find yourself in a narrow sewer passage with running water and the skeletal remains of some poor unfortunate trapped behind a sewer grate. This skeleton possesses some minor treasure. Following this passage, you will come to an open area containing a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a small [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"). This room also possesses a banner with a [Guild Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") as well as a murky pool with a hidden trapdoor leading to Riften Docks.

The next room serves as a well-lit dining area and reading room resembling a typical Riften basement. It contains a [shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh") and a unique painting. Within one of the wardrobes you will find a false back panel leading to a trophy room with nineteen mannequins, a chest surrounded by three [piles of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Pile_of_Gold "Skyrim:Pile of Gold"), a well-stocked [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"), and weapon racks. One of the shield plaques displays a (likely ill-gotten) [Riften Guard's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Riften Guard's Shield"). This room also contains holders for all ten [dragon claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Dragon Claw") from the base game, the five [bugs in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Bugs_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"), the [Right Eye of the Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Right_Eye_of_the_Falmer "Skyrim:Right Eye of the Falmer"), the [Spider Control Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Control_Rod "Skyrim:Spider Control Rod") (the one for [Aicantar's Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar%27s_Spider "Skyrim:Aicantar's Spider"), not the one from [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)")), the five [paragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Unique_Items "Skyrim:Other Unique Items") from the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), [Chillrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillrend "Skyrim:Chillrend"), [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever"), the [Nightingale Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Bow "Skyrim:Nightingale Bow") and [Nightingale Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Blade "Skyrim:Nightingale Blade"), as well as all of the [dragon priest masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Mask "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Mask") in the base game and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Dragon_Priest_Masks "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts"), with the exception of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(item) "Skyrim:Miraak (item)"). In addition, there are shelves for all of the items collected for [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny"). However, these will not activate until after the item has been turned in, so the items will need to be removed from the Thieves Guild afterwards and moved here instead.

Returning to the main dining room, you will find three side rooms behind closed doors. One of these leads to a kitchen, which contains an [oven](/wiki/Skyrim:Baking "Skyrim:Baking") and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking"). Two [Glass Jars](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Jar "Skyrim:Glass Jar"), items unique to this Creation, can be found on a top shelf in here. Another side room contains two child-sized beds and a target dummy for your [adopted children](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption"). Of note in this room is another Glass Jar found on one of the shelves next to some [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), along with a [shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth") on the shelf above. The final side room is the master bedroom, containing a double bed with a [shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") on the shelf above it, next to a [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet") and [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher").

## Notes

- Behind the wall, southeast of the trophy room, is an inaccessible urn containing a copy of all items displayable in the room, presumably for testing purposes. You can retrieve these items by clipping through the wall.

## Bugs

- Mannequin heights can change at random, either sinking into their bases or floating above them.
- Chillrend does not mount onto its named rack correctly, sticks out of the rack, or out of the mannequin to right side of the rack.
  - This can be fixed by walking as close to the rack as possible, looking down, and selecting "Place". You may need to try this multiple times.
- Adopted children will not move to this house if they are living in another player home. Instead, they will continue to live at the house they were in previously.
- Sometimes the False Panel Door will malfunction and an invisible barrier will block you from the leaving the Trophy Room. **?**
- Underwater entry crashes the game occasionally. **?**
- The items contained in the urn mentioned above can be accessed by executing a dual-wield power attack and using [netch jelly](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Jelly "Skyrim:Netch Jelly") or another paralyzing ingredient when the character is clipping through the wall. **?**

## Gallery

- 

  The Ratway entrance
- 

  The forge area
- 

  The trophy room behind the false back panel
- 

  The alchemy station
- 

  A custom painting

Shadowfoot Sanctum interior

**Shadowfoot Sanctum** is a small player home located in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). The map marker for the exterior entrance is called **Riften Docks**.

You will be directed to buy the house from [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") for 7,500 gold during the related quest.

The house consists of one area, *[Shadowfoot Sanctum](#Shadowfoot_Sanctum)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(quest) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum"): Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.

## Exterior

The Riften Docks entrance

This house possesses two entrances, allowing for easy access to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)") without having to enter Riften itself. The main entrance is located behind a gate in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway"), in the room with the executioner's block just across from [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). The second, hidden entrance is an underwater trap door located in the murky pool in the forge area of the sanctum, which leads to a flowing sewer grate outside the walls of Riften. This entrance can be found in the water just south of the western city gates. This Creation adds a new map marker for the Riften Docks which allows for easy access to Shadowfoot Sanctum, as it will place you on the bridge leading to the [Riften Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Warehouse "Skyrim:Riften Warehouse"), conveniently overlooking the sewer grate.

### Shadowfoot Sanctum

Entering from the Ratway, you will find yourself in a narrow sewer passage with running water and the skeletal remains of some poor unfortunate trapped behind a sewer grate. This skeleton possesses some minor treasure. Following this passage, you will come to an open area containing a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a small [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"). This room also possesses a banner with a [Guild Shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") as well as a murky pool with a hidden trapdoor leading to Riften Docks.

The next room serves as a well-lit dining area and reading room resembling a typical Riften basement. It contains a [shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh") and a unique painting. Within one of the wardrobes you will find a false back panel leading to a trophy room with nineteen mannequins, a chest surrounded by three [piles of gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Pile_of_Gold "Skyrim:Pile of Gold"), a well-stocked [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"), and weapon racks. One of the shield plaques displays a (likely ill-gotten) [Riften Guard's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Riften Guard's Shield"). This room also contains holders for all ten [dragon claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Dragon Claw") from the base game, the five [bugs in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Bugs_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"), the [Right Eye of the Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Right_Eye_of_the_Falmer "Skyrim:Right Eye of the Falmer"), the [Spider Control Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Control_Rod "Skyrim:Spider Control Rod") (the one for [Aicantar's Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar%27s_Spider "Skyrim:Aicantar's Spider"), not the one from [Forgotten Seasons](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Seasons_(quest) "Skyrim:Forgotten Seasons (quest)")), the five [paragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Unique_Items "Skyrim:Other Unique Items") from the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), [Chillrend](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillrend "Skyrim:Chillrend"), [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever"), the [Nightingale Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Bow "Skyrim:Nightingale Bow") and [Nightingale Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Blade "Skyrim:Nightingale Blade"), as well as all of the [dragon priest masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Mask "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Mask") in the base game and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor_Artifacts#Dragon_Priest_Masks "Skyrim:Armor Artifacts"), with the exception of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(item) "Skyrim:Miraak (item)"). In addition, there are shelves for all of the items collected for [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny"). However, these will not activate until after the item has been turned in, so the items will need to be removed from the Thieves Guild afterwards and moved here instead.

Returning to the main dining room, you will find three side rooms behind closed doors. One of these leads to a kitchen, which contains an [oven](/wiki/Skyrim:Baking "Skyrim:Baking") and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking"). Two [Glass Jars](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Jar "Skyrim:Glass Jar"), items unique to this Creation, can be found on a top shelf in here. Another side room contains two child-sized beds and a target dummy for your [adopted children](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption"). Of note in this room is another Glass Jar found on one of the shelves next to some [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), along with a [shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth") on the shelf above. The final side room is the master bedroom, containing a double bed with a [shrine of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mara "Skyrim:Shrine of Mara") on the shelf above it, next to a [Jeweled Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Goblet "Skyrim:Jeweled Goblet") and [Jeweled Pitcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Jeweled_Pitcher "Skyrim:Jeweled Pitcher").

## Notes

- Behind the wall, southeast of the trophy room, is an inaccessible urn containing a copy of all items displayable in the room, presumably for testing purposes. You can retrieve these items by clipping through the wall.

## Bugs

- Mannequin heights can change at random, either sinking into their bases or floating above them.
- Chillrend does not mount onto its named rack correctly, sticks out of the rack, or out of the mannequin to right side of the rack.
  - This can be fixed by walking as close to the rack as possible, looking down, and selecting "Place". You may need to try this multiple times.
- Adopted children will not move to this house if they are living in another player home. Instead, they will continue to live at the house they were in previously.
- Sometimes the False Panel Door will malfunction and an invisible barrier will block you from the leaving the Trophy Room. **?**
- Underwater entry crashes the game occasionally. **?**
- The items contained in the urn mentioned above can be accessed by executing a dual-wield power attack and using [netch jelly](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Jelly "Skyrim:Netch Jelly") or another paralyzing ingredient when the character is clipping through the wall. **?**

# Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Purchase a cozy sewer home ideal for a thief.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") |
| Location(s): | [The Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") |
| Reward: | [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(place) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (place)") |
| ID: | ccEEJSSE003\_HouseQuest |
| Required Items: | 7,500 gold |
| Added by: | [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum") |

A subterranean home beneath the streets of Riften

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Purchase [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(place) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (place)") from [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") for 7,500 gold.
2. Visit your new property.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This short quest will start when you talk to [Vekel the Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Vekel_the_Man "Skyrim:Vekel the Man") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"), an underground tavern in [the Ratway](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ratway "Skyrim:The Ratway") beneath [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), and purchase [Shadowfoot Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowfoot_Sanctum_(place) "Skyrim:Shadowfoot Sanctum (place)") for 7,500 gold.

You will be given a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Shadowfoot_Sanctum "Skyrim:Key to Shadowfoot Sanctum") to access the sanctum upon purchasing the property, located a short distance from the Flagon's entrance. It is a fully-furnished player home with a hidden entrance and lots of storage, ideal for members of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). It contains many crafting stations and [shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") as well as space for your [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Spouse "Skyrim:Spouse") and [adopted children](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption"). Enter Shadowfoot Sanctum to complete the quest.

## Quest Stages

| Shadowfoot Sanctum (ccEEJSSE003\_HouseQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Not every home in Skyrim is built above ground. If I'm ever in the need of a more discreet hideout, I should head over to Riften and talk to those in the know. *Objective 10:* Purchase a home in the Riften Ratways |
| 20 |  | After meeting with the Thieves Guild in the Ragged Flagon, I purchased a home in the Ratways from Vekel. I should find the location and make myself at home. *Objective 20:* Enter Shadowfoot Sanctum |
| 100 | ☑ | After meeting with the Thieves Guild in the Ragged Flagon, I purchased a home in the Ratways from Vekel. I found the entrance to Shadowfoot Sanctum and can now settle in. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEEJSSE003_HouseQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccEEJSSE003_HouseQuest`.

Shadowgreen Cavern

**Shadowgreen Cavern** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing leveled [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") and [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains only one zone, *[Shadowgreen Cavern](#Shadowgreen_Cavern)*.

Shadowgreen Cavern interior

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

To reach the cave, follow the road from [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") toward the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") and the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"), but stay on the main road as it curves north then west around the mountain. Five [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes grow along either side of the path, which is marked by piles of rocks leading from the road up to the entrance, and three clusters of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungus grow around the entrance.

### Shadowgreen Cavern

A short path inside leads to a large natural cave with a central rock formation filled with vegetation, with a large number of [monarch butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Monarch_Butterfly "Skyrim:Monarch Butterfly") and [blue butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly") during the day and [luna moths](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth "Skyrim:Luna Moth") and [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") at night. There is a stream running from south to north across the cavern feeding into a pool of water, and holes in the ceiling letting in natural light. There are several [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") running around, and various types of fauna in the cavern.

Fishing supplies

The path turns north into the cavern, and on the left is a tree stump with some [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it and a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") beside it. The path turns to the east and passes a dead tree trunk that has fallen across the stream. On the ground at the end of the tree is another bear trap. Just above the bear trap is another growth of mora tapinella, and to the southwest are three [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). To the northeast is another red mountain flower, and just past it a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). Farther along the shore is another red mountain flower and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found next to a dead [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter"), some [Fishing Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Items#Fishing_Boots "Skyrim:Fishing Items"), a [Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod"), and a bucket with three [histcarp](/wiki/Skyrim:Histcarp "Skyrim:Histcarp") inside. Fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here. There are five [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") in the pool, and on the bottom of the pond, around a half-sunken skeleton, is a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). On the shore above the half-submerged mammoth skeleton are two purple mountain flowers and one blue mountain flower.

To the south, and to the left of the tree in that direction, you can find another red mountain flower and another blue mountain flower. Heading west back to the fallen tree, you will find another blue mountain flower. On the other side of the tree is a red mountain flower, and to the south of it is a purple mountain flower. Look to the east now to see a massive stone pillar that has fallen over at a slight angle; the path deeper into the cavern runs underneath this pillar.

As you pass under the arch formed by the fallen pillar, you will see one of a pack of three wolves wandering where the path splits at a T-junction; the others can be found farther along the path to the southeast. Along the eastern edge of the path after the arch there are two red and one purple mountain flowers. To the west, around the back of the pillar, is another red mountain flower, another two between it and the path to the south, and another two behind the tree to the west. To the west is a ledge, and to the south you will find a rotten tree stump with an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") inside. As you head back east to the main path, there is another rotten stump on the right with some mora tapinella growing on it.

As you go down the path, you can find a blue mountain flower and a red mountain flower on the right. Another three red and two purple mountain flowers can be found along the outer right rock wall. There is a dead [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") just to the left of the path forward, as well as another red mountain flower. If you backtrack to the T-junction and turn to face the path down, you can climb the rocks to the left and follow them to a purple mountain flower. You can also climb the rocks on the other side of the junction, near the stump, and carefully make your way along to find three mora tapinella, two red mountain flowers, and one purple mountain flower.

Along the path past the dead elk, you should be able to see another fallen tree. Before that, along the right-hand wall you will find a red mountain flower and a purple mountain flower, and another purple flower on the left. Just past the fallen tree, a [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") will emerge from another tree. The spriggan will call a leveled animal, which lurks just around the corner to the north, to aid it in battle. There is another rabbit running around here, a purple mountain flower to the right just before the spriggan's tree, and a blue mountain flower and another purple mountain flower on either side of the path after it. You can climb the rocks on either side of the fallen tree; climb the ledge on the northern side to find two mora tapinella on either side of a large stump, and a red mountain flower.

Around the corner are another two spriggans, one on the ledge to the north, and the other to the west against a large tree. The one on the northern ledge is trying to blend with a stump, so its upper parts may be visible and vulnerable to a ranged attack. Under the northern ledge is a red mountain flower, and a purple mountain flower is on the ledge. The stump on the ledge has some mora tapinella growing on it. To the west is a fallen tree with more mora tapinella and a red mountain flower growing beside it. If you climb the rocks behind it and head north, you can find another two red mountain flowers. If you climb over the rocks to the east and follow that ledge to the south, you will find another red mountain flower and another blue mountain flower.

As you climb the main path, there is a purple mountain flower on the left, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the right. Before proceeding up the path, go through the bush to the west to a ledge above the pond. One red mountain flower and one blue mountain flower can be found up here, as well as another red mountain flower and another purple mountain flower through the bushes to the north. Now climb the rocks to the northeast to find another purple mountain flower and another red mountain flower.

As you start to climb up the path, there are four [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the rock wall to the right, though only three can be harvested, and a stump to the left with a growth of mora tapinella. Farther up the path, the ground will shake and there will be a small [rockfall](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders"). To avoid damage, retreat and hug the rockface as soon as the ground shakes. From here you can find two red, one blue, and two purple mountain flowers as the path levels out. At the top of the next upward section is another spriggan, normally hidden against the trunk unless you attracted its attention by making too much noise below. There are two more blue mountain flowers and one more purple mountain flower as you reach the area with the spriggan, and another red mountain flower and another purple mountain flower as the path reaches the plateau.

On the plateau is a small pond surrounding a small island with a large tree growing up and out of the cavern, but be careful, as there are two spriggans and two leveled animals up here too. From the top of the path, there is a red mountain flower to the north, another two red mountain flowers and three purple mountain flowers to the east, and if you follow the path until you are facing north, another red mountain flower. There is a fallen tree to the south bridging the gap to the island. On the island is an unlocked boss chest, a leveled weapon, a leveled soul gem, a random potion, and a leveled potion of healing. There are two [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") as well; one by the chest, and one to the north of it. The path down is to the north; on the bridge are a red mountain flower and a blue mountain flower.

While on the plateau, head to the northeast edge and then look down; you should spot a chest (expert-locked) on a ledge with no apparent way to reach it. It can be reached by facing the widest part of the ledge and using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). It can also be reached with some luck by heading to the end of the bridge, facing east, and sprint-jumping off. This can be difficult, as there is a protruding section of the wall to the left, which means you cannot aim along the ledge, and must instead take a few steps toward the middle of the bridge and aim for the smallest edge. If you miss the ledge itself and catch the rocks just below it, you will need to turn back east to jump up. To get down from the ledge, you need to face the plateau and use whirlwind sprint, or jump and hope to hit the path running up the side of it. If you miss the jump, you might still survive the fall to the ground below, but will take heavy damage.

At the end of the bridge off the plateau, drop down to the west to find another red mountain flower and an adept-locked chest. Go through the bush and hug the wall, then make a steep drop to another ledge (it will hurt, but should not kill you). This ledge has a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"), a lootable skeleton of an unfortunate person, a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"). Another red mountain flower and a blue mountain flower can be found here. To leave, jump into the pond, then follow the path back out.

| Plants |
| --- |
| 41 [Red Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  26 [Purple Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  13 [Blue Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  12 [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella")  3 [Glowing Mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom")  2 [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") |

## Notes

- Although the map marker indicates the cave is in the mountains near the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy"), it is actually farther north, close to the coastline. This is an artifact of the map's angle and how far north the cave is, which you can see by moving the map left and right: the cave marker doesn't move at the same rate as the embassy and other nearby markers.
- Shadowgreen Cavern contains the highest number of red mountain flowers in the game, and is tied for the sixth highest number of purple mountain flowers. It also contains the fourth highest amount of mora tapinella.
- This is a good place for collecting [butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing") and [blue butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing") during the day, and [luna moth wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing") and [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") at night. The cave has eleven spawn points for luna moths and torchbugs, giving it the seventh highest concentration of these sites in the game.
- The dungeon is cleared by killing all of the spriggans. There is no "boss".

## Bugs

- One of the four glowing mushrooms cannot be harvested.

# Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [JR](/wiki/User:JR "User:JR"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [75.106.138.23](/wiki/Special:Contributions/75.106.138.23 "Special:Contributions/75.106.138.23"), *not checked* |

| **Discover the writings of Shalidor and benefit from his wisdom.** | |

|  |  |

| Quest Giver: | [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") |
| Location(s): | [The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"), various dungeons |

| ID: | MGR21 |

Shalidor's Insights

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
2. Travel to the indicated location and retrieve [Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights_(book) "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights (book)").
3. Return to Urag gro-Shub.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Talk to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") and ask him if there are any special books he's looking for. He will tell you that he's looking for a book Arch-Mage Shalidor wrote so he can translate his writings. The book can be located in the boss-level chest of any [dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") in the game including ones added in [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), meaning that your destination is randomly selected from over 140 possible dungeons. For specific details about the target location, see its place page; details about any possible conflicts with other quests are also provided there.

The book is in the dungeon's boss chest, normally located at the end of the dungeon. Return to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") and return the book. He will say that it will take about a day to translate the writings.

The quest will complete at this point and clear from your journal, although you will have written that you still need to return to Urag after the book has been translated.

Wait for at least 24 hours, and when you return Urag will tell you he's finished translating the text. He will give you three identical copies of one of several possible ["Shalidor's Insights" scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights:_Alteration "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights: Alteration"), or will pass on any knowledge gained from the writings in the form of a one-point skill increase to any magic skill other than Enchanting.

## Notes

- Which scrolls or skill boost you earn is decided when you hand over [Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights_(book) "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights (book)") to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"). It is possible to obtain the reward you prefer by saving before giving him the book and reloading the save until the desired reward is obtained.
- If the quest marker points to [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt"), it is possible to complete this quest very easily by doing the Forsworn chain in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), as this is where Madanach has his base of operations. All of the Forsworn in this area are friendly if you completed [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine"), as long as you sided with the Forsworn in the mine.
- The quest may point to a number of locations which cannot be accessed without completing certain other actions. You may wish to avoid clashes by reloading the game and getting another location. Following is a list of locations and the actions needed to be undertaken to complete this quest:
  - [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn"): partial completion of [Find Red Eagle's Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Find_Red_Eagle%27s_sword "Skyrim:Find Red Eagle's sword") / [Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)").
  - [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum"): complete [Speaking With Silence](/wiki/Skyrim:Speaking_With_Silence "Skyrim:Speaking With Silence"). The quest marker may also point to the back door, but you still must complete Speaking with Silence.
  - [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah"): complete [Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!") This location is the most common reason why the quest marker does not appear. (This is addressed by version 1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"); the Katariah can no longer be chosen as a target location for this quest.)
  - [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb"): complete [Glory of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Glory_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:Glory of the Dead").
- If [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed, some radiant locations may be on [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"). If you are in Skyrim, you will not receive a quest marker pointing you to the quest location, but must travel to Solstheim first (at which point any quest markers you have to quests in Skyrim will disappear).
  - One of these locations can be [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak"), which means you would need to do [The Path of Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Path_of_Knowledge "Skyrim:The Path of Knowledge") to complete this side quest.

## Bugs

- If the quest marker points to [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins") and you have previously defeated Vokun, the book will be in an inaccessible area in the back of Vokun's Throne Room.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, fixes this bug.
  - Vokun's Throne Room may be accessed by utilizing a follower to open the gate blocking the player from the antechamber exit above the first room. This is accomplished by bringing a follower after clearing out the entire dungeon (clearing out the dungeon may be necessary), climbing up the pile the rubble, in the first room, besides Anska, and using Whirlwind Sprint to access the walkway leading to the exit from the antechamber. The follower will run through the dungeon and eventually appear on the other side of the gate. The follower can then be instructed to pull the chain, thereby opening the gate and permitting the player into Vokun's Throne Room. Unconfirmed on PC.
  -  This can be made reachable using [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands, either to resurrect Vokun and kill him again (select the body, not his ashes) or to simply pass through one of the closed gates (use 'tcl' to turn clipping on and off).
- If the quest [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") is active when this quest sends you to [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep"), the "insights" may be missing.
  - To fix this you can type in console `sqv mgr21`, look for a line REF 'Book'->"(x), x is id you need, then jump and open console again midair so the book won't fall under ground, type in console `prid x` where x is id you got previously, and last type `moveto player`. Look for a book on ground.
- When you return to ask Urag if he has translated the writings, he may not give you any reward.
- If you have started [Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") and cannot find the quest marker for Shalidor's insights on either Skyrim or Solstheim the questline is permanently broken without console commands (because the book is on the nonexistent ship Katariah).
  -  Type `sqv mgr21` into the console. Search for Ref 'Book'-> (x) where x is the Book Ref ID code. Type `Prid x` and press enter. Then type `moveto player`. The book should fall on the floor in front of you. Remember to do this in a private location because picking up the book will be classified as stealing.
- Urag repeats the lengthy introduction to this quest every time it starts because the tracker variable resets each time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Shalidor's Insights (MGR21) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Urag gro-Shub is looking for writings by the Arch-Mage Shalidor, so that he can translate them into something useful for the College. He's asked that I attempt to find another copy for him. *Objective 10:* Find Shalidor's writings |
| 20 |  | I've managed to find the writings of the Arch-Mage Shalidor that Urag gro-Shub was looking for. I should take them to him at the Arcanaeum so that he can translate them. *Objective 20:* Talk to Urag |
| 200 | ☑ | Urag gro-Shub asked me to bring him more of the writings of the Arch-Mage Shalidor. I was able to find another copy, and have brought it to him. He will translate it as soon as he's able, and then we'll see what we can learn from it. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MGR21 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MGR21`.

Shalidor's Maze

**Shalidor's Maze** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") containing [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") and a [dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora"). It contains only one zone, *[Shalidor's Maze](#Shalidor.27s_Maze)*.

### Exterior

Entrance

The entrance is at ground level on the east side of Labyrinthian's outdoor ruin, just east of the mound-like structure containing the ruined dragon priest monument. Despite the location's name, it is not actually a maze, as there are no intersections where you must decide which way to turn.

There is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") just outside the entrance. See [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") for full details of the surrounding ruin.

### Shalidor's Maze

Courtyard

You enter into a corridor descending a flight of stairs to the north. After a couple turns, the corridor opens into an open-air courtyard with a large stone wall ahead. There is an arch through the middle of the wall, and stairways up to the top on either side of the courtyard. In front of the arch, there is a large flower bed and a tree growing on either side. This flower bed, along with more around the courtyard and hanging from the walls and arches outside the maze, contains plants that are listed in the table below. Taking either stairway leads to the top of the wall and provides a good view of the maze beyond the arch, also giving you access via [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to the top of the walls surrounding the maze and courtyard. These walls can also be reached by jumping around the obstructing rock face on the western side. On the western wall, near the northwest corner of the area in an easily missed alcove, is an unlocked chest. To easily locate this chest, after you pass the sloped part of the wall, walk under the first square arch then stop just before the next one; the alcove will be on your left. On the eastern wall, there is another alcove with a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), a leveled [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") (up to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") in quality), and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). The easiest way to reaching this alcove is to continue around from the west wall, climb the peaked roof over the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), and keep going. The two (western and eastern) alcoves are almost directly opposite each other.

| Plants |
| --- |
| 5 [Blue Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  9 [Deathbells](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell")  14 [Dragon's Tongues](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue")  11 [Hanging Mosses](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss")  10 [Purple Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  4 [Red Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") |

Staff projections

Beyond the arch near the entrance is another courtyard with a raised circle. Atop the circle is a burnt corpse holding a filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") and a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Tattered_Note "Skyrim:Tattered Note"). By the corpse are four smaller circles, each projecting a staff, namely, staves of [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fear "Skyrim:Staff of Fear"), [Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"), [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magelight "Skyrim:Staff of Magelight"), and [Repulsion](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Repulsion "Skyrim:Staff of Repulsion"). The staves represent spells from the schools of [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"), [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), and [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), respectively. On either side of this area are two more flower beds, each containing a tree and plants. Behind the staves is an archway to the start of the maze. You can walk all the way around the outside of the maze to reach the word wall at the other end of the maze, which teaches part of the [Dismay](/wiki/Skyrim:Dismay "Skyrim:Dismay") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

Sigil of Alteration

Sigil of Destruction

Entering the maze from the beginning, you pass two shutters that contain four loose gold [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a random filled soul gem. The path heads north to a turning to the east; here, it is barred. To the right of the bars is a shutter that contains a [scroll of Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Magelight "Skyrim:Scroll of Magelight"). There is a Sigil of Alteration on the north wall, which requires you to cast [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight") on the sigil to lower the bars. You can use a scroll, staff, or spell to cast Magelight; all will work. Follow the linear path through this part of the maze, opening the shutters as you go. Some of them hold items including a flute, two pieces of charcoal, or a loose gold coin, but most hold nothing. You will encounter a couple [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") in this part of the maze. When you reach the end of the path, you will find the Sigil of Destruction, which requires you to cast [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") or another targeted Destruction spell. When you do, the floor will open and allow you to drop and continue onward.

Rising staircase

Waterfall

The shaft has three beams across it to help break your fall. Growing from these beams are hanging moss plants. Once you reach the bottom, the path continues to the south and enters a typical catacomb-style area. At the crossroads, the path to the east is a dead end. The southern path ends in a shaft similar to the one you dropped down earlier, with beams across it and a trap in the ceiling. Heading west leads toward a stone wall that rises as you approach to reveal a spiral staircase leading up and out of the maze on the west side, opposite a waterfall. Take the stairs and head north to the word wall and the second entrance.

Sigil of Illusion

Sigil of Restoration

This end is blocked by bars, similar to the southern end; this time, the nearby wall is marked with the Sigil of Illusion, which requires the use of any targeted Illusion spell to open the way, such as Fear. In this section of the maze, you will find the following items in the shutters: a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), [bloody rags](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloody_Rags "Skyrim:Bloody Rags"), a piece of [bent Dwemer scrap metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bent_Dwemer_Scrap_Metal "Skyrim:Bent Dwemer Scrap Metal"), an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet") together, a [centurion dynamo core](/wiki/Skyrim:Centurion_Dynamo_Core "Skyrim:Centurion Dynamo Core"), and a *[Spell Tome: Heal Other](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Heal_Other "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Heal Other")*. You will encounter an [ice wraith](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") and two skeevers. The skeevers might be found already dead, killed by the ice wraith. You will also pass a dead skeleton that can be looted, and a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Liminal Bridges](/wiki/Skyrim:Liminal_Bridges "Skyrim:Liminal Bridges")* next to it. At the end of the path, the wall bears the Sigil of Restoration, which requires the use of a targeted Restoration spell or use of the Staff of Repulsion. The drop beyond this barrier is to the shaft opposite where you landed last time. Directly ahead will be a sphere of magical energy blocking the way. This sphere will only appear if all four sigils have been activated.

Dremora

As you approach the sphere, you will be teleported to a circular platform with a leveled dremora who will summon a [flame atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Flame Atronach") and shoot firebolts at you. Once the dremora loses a certain amount of health, you will be teleported back to the entrance to Shalidor's Maze. Two leveled atronachs will appear beyond the arch and immediately attack; the dremora will also appear in front of you if you did not kill him in the magical sphere. If the dremora appears outside the sphere, killing him will enable you to loot a [Diadem of the Savant](/wiki/Skyrim:Diadem_of_the_Savant "Skyrim:Diadem of the Savant") from his corpse along with a [Daedra heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") and a random weapon. The diadem reduces the magicka cost of all spells by 5%. To obtain this item, it is recommended to let the dremora survive the earlier fight in the magical sphere. Alternatively, if you kill him quickly during the Trial of Conjuration, you may loot the diadem from his corpse there, though killing him in one hit may cause you to become stuck in the sphere (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Notes

- This location cannot be independently [cleared](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons"). It is only shown as cleared when the boss draugr of Labyrinthian has been killed, as the maze is considered to be part of Labyrinthian. The maze never adds to your count of cleared locations, and therefore does not contribute to the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement.
- [Fast travel](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Travel "Skyrim:Fast Travel") is not available in Shalidor's Maze, nor will the [Call Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Call_Dragon "Skyrim:Call Dragon") shout summon [Odahviing](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing").
- This maze is a unicursal maze, which means there is only one path for you to take. Its type is also known as a labyrinth, which gave the ruin its name.
- You don't need to finish the maze to progress through the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") questline, nor do you need to join the College to gain access to the latter.
- Even though the maze was built as a test for Archmages, you don't need any previous magical abilities or knowledge to solve it, as the staves serve as substitutes for the spells.
- If you do not wish to use the staves, it is possible to jump into the maze from the side parapets. Alternatively, casting the corresponding spells will suffice; for the Sigil of Alteration, a useful scroll is also available nearby.
- From an aerial view, this maze appears to be shaped like an hourglass. Interestingly enough, there is an "hourglass riddle" during the [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Arena:Labyrinthian "Arena:Labyrinthian") quest in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*, and during [The Rosethorn Cache](/wiki/Oblivion:The_Rosethorn_Cache "Oblivion:The Rosethorn Cache") quest in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*.
- You may be able to open the Restoration sigil with Destruction spells.
- If you enter the maze during snowy weather, it will snow inside as well.
- The music will fluctuate between environmental music and dungeon music.
- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") can get trapped in here. It is safer to tell them to wait outside.
- If you are interested only in the word wall, you can access it by going around the maze (either left or right).
- If you get caught on the peak while climbing the roof over the word wall, jump toward the north (rear) and you'll be freed.
- For a more in-depth guide on Shalidor's Maze, read the book [A Minor Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Minor_Maze "Skyrim:A Minor Maze").

## Bugs

- In the French, Italian, Spanish, German, Dutch, Russian, Polish, and Japanese versions of the game, a bug prevents you from finishing the maze. Even if you cast the right spell on the right sigil, nothing happens.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
  - Change the game's language to English to bypass the bug.
- In the French, German, Spanish, and Italian versions of the game, traps in the area may not work properly.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- If the dremora is killed by your first hit (as may occur if you have the Devastating Blow perk), the dremora won't teleport back to the maze entrance, and you will get stuck in the Trial of Conjuration zone.
  - Try attacking the dremora corpse with a melee weapon. This can sometimes allow you to progress through the trial.
  -  if that fails use console command (`coc MazeEntrance`) to return to the entrance.
- Sometimes a sigil will not activate, or the Trial of Conjuration zone may not trigger.
  - If this happens, try walking the maze again.
  - Also try a variety of spells and staves if the first one fails. The Restoration sigil, for example, may not activate with Healing Hands, but instead with Repel Lesser Undead.
- Your follower may refuse to leave the area after completing the maze. If you dismiss them, they may not return home.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - Try fast traveling to a nearby location, and your follower should reappear when the game loads.
  -  You may move outside the labyrinth and use the console to move your follower to you (`prid [follower's refID]` followed by `moveto player`). They should then follow you as normal.
  - Dismissing and rehiring your follower may fix this.
- Followers may also remain stuck in the maze before completing it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- A respawning copy of the Diadem of the Savant can also be found on the wood chopping block outside [Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack"). It is possible this was a mistake, as the Creation Kit specifies that the diadem was meant to be a reward for completing Shalidor's Maze.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. It changes the diadem outside Froki's Shack into a leveled circlet with a [Fortify Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_Archery "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") effect.
- It is possible for the Dremora holding the Diadem of the Savant to fail to be teleported back out of Shalidor's Maze when you solve it. If this happens, the Diadem is unobtainable.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.9, addresses this issue. A copy will now be generated should this fail to work as expected.
  - Another copy of the Diadem of the Savant an also be found on the wood chopping block outside [Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack"), provided you don't have Unofficial Skyrim Patch 1.2.5 or later.

## Maps

- 

  Shalidor's Maze

# Skyrim:Shaman's Hut

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Shaman's Hut ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Shaman%27s+Hut)) | | |

| # of [Arcane Enchanters](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") | 1 |

Shaman's Hut

The **Shaman's Hut** is the home of shaman [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") and his daughter [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the southeast side of the village, south of the [Greathall](/wiki/Skyrim:Greathall "Skyrim:Greathall").

It contains only one zone, *[Shaman's Hut](#Shaman.27s_Hut)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Frea](/wiki/Skyrim:Frea "Skyrim:Frea") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider") |

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance is a bench. The entrance is unlocked.

### Shaman's Hut

Shaman's Hut interior

The entrance leads into a room with a well-dressed dinner table to the left and three respawning barrels and a non-respawning sack to the right, all of them with food. Next to the barrels are a set of shelves with two bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), an [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam") and one bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") along with a respawning food sack. The dinner table holds three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") in a bowl, a [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), two pieces of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a piece of bread, a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). On a shelf above are two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on a plate and a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute").

Opposite the table is the entrance to the room with an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters"). A non-respawning dresser holds various clothing and a bowl with a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") sits on top, next to a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes"). To the left of the enchanter is a copy of the book *[Children of the All-Maker](/wiki/Skyrim:Children_of_the_All-Maker "Skyrim:Children of the All-Maker")* and in a wooden bowl are a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), a [pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl"), and a rare [small pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl"). Also on the table there's a filled [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), a salt pile, and a plate with another Nordic barnacle and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). Above the enchanter are two non-respawning food sacks, some [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), and a bit of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") on a shelf. On the floor to the left of the table is an open box containing a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato").

A huge fireplace covers most of the floor in the central room with two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and two ash yams on the side. On the roof supports above is a single bottle of ale. There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") in the southwestern corner, with a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") in a bowl and a freshly caught [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and some [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam") hanging above. The non-respawning cupboard to the left contains clutter and the respawning barrel contains food. The shelves above the cupboard hold a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a fillet of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), and another salt pile. A bottle of alto wine and a bottle of ale can be found on the top shelves along with a respawning [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") containing uncommon ingredients.

Another respawning apothecary's satchel on a ledge, this time containing rare ingredients, can be found beneath the mudcrab trophy on the wall, along with some wheat and a bucket containing a sample of [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw"), a sample of [trama root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root"), and a [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin"). Some shelves near the bedroom door hold a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"), and two non-respawning food sacks. The bedroom contains two owned beds and a set of shelves with three pearls and a horker tusk.

# Skyrim:Sharpslope Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Sharpslope Cave | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Chaurus Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Shellbug](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1zFalmerValley02 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") | |

Sharpslope Cave

**Sharpslope Cave** is a small cave in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") containing [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and one of the rare [shellbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug"). It contains only one zone, *[Sharpslope Cave](#Sharpslope_Cave)*.

### Exterior

The exterior of this cave is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). There are two entrances. The upper entrance is reached by heading north from the Wayshrine of Resolution to a small [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") settlement containing two tents, then following the path to the right up and across several bridges and past several more Falmer settlements. The lower entrance is reached from the same small settlement, by continuing along the river heading southwest. You will pass a group of five [chaurus cocoons](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon"), two of which are occupied, with two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") among them. A short distance farther is the entrance. There are three more occupied chaurus cocoons, two more empty cocoons, and four more orichalcum ore veins along the river, with the first vein immediately south of the lower entrance, and the last vein in the corner on the opposite bank.

### Sharpslope Cave

The upper entrance leads into a dimly lit passage heading west, south, and west again as it descends. At the bottom, a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") is on the wall by a turn to the north. The ramp then enters a chamber, where it descends in a spiral around the outer wall. There are many [Falmer hives](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") in the chamber, but most are empty. Two Falmer, one a magic-user, patrol the upper part of the ramp. Between the first and second Falmer hives, a narrow opening on the outer wall leads to another chamber containing one of the rare [shellbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug"). In order to obtain their [chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug_Chitin "Skyrim:Shellbug Chitin"), these creatures must be [mined](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"); the material cannot be obtained through killing the creatures by conventional means. Shellbugs are also not detected by the [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") spell.

The ramp continues to descend past an empty alcove and around a central column of rock surrounded by scaffolding. At the bottom, the path passes south into a second chamber. Beyond more scaffolding to the left, a [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter") and a [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") roam, while a high-level Falmer is in a tent above. A Falmer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") is against a thin rock pillar at ground level. There are two upper ledges along the sides of the chamber, but both are empty. An earthen ramp and a walkway from the tent lead to the passage in the east with the lower entrance.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to mine the shellbug after it respawns. Leaving and reentering the cave will enable the shellbug, allowing you to mine it normally.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.
- You may not be able to interact with some of the glowing mushrooms.

## Maps

Sharpslope Cave

# Skyrim:Shearpoint

## Overview

Shearpoint

**Shearpoint** is a mountaintop [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches all three words of the [Throw Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Throw_Voice "Skyrim:Throw Voice") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Dragon "Skyrim:Bounty: Dragon")**: Kill a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") in its [lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dragon Seekers](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Seekers "Skyrim:Dragon Seekers")**: Go to a [dragon lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Lairs "Skyrim:Dragon Lairs") with [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas") or [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") and kill the dragon. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The summit is visible behind [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep"). A rough path to the word wall can be followed by heading northwest past the keep and circling around to the northeast. Alternatively, you may head south from [Tumble Arch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumble_Arch_Pass "Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass") before heading east once the slope becomes easier to climb.

Before the [dragons' return](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"), the word wall will be guarded by [Krosis](/wiki/Skyrim:Krosis_(creature) "Skyrim:Krosis (creature)"), an undead [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest").

After the dragons' return, the word wall will be guarded by a leveled [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon"). If Krosis had not previously been defeated, he will also be present.

Regardless of whether [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has been completed, the boss chest is against the word wall.

## Notes

- When the location [respawns](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn"), Krosis' sarcophagus will be resealed, but no dragon priest will respawn. The dragon respawns as usual.
- A [Shearpoint Dragon](/wiki/Legends:Shearpoint Dragon) card appears in [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends").

## Bugs

- The location might not be marked as cleared even after you kill the dragon and Krosis and learn the word from the wall.
  - Reloading a previous save may fix this.
  -  The [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `SetLocationCleared 0x0001916c 1` will force the area to be marked as cleared.
- The word wall will occasionally only teach you one of the three words of Throw Voice.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
  - Reloading a previous save may fix this.
- The dragon may rest on the word wall and not move, and will be invincible.
  - Reloading a previous save may fix this.
  - Fast traveling and returning later may fix this.
- If you learn of this location from gossip, such as a city guard, you'll be able to fast travel to the location, even though you have never been there before. This will cause your "Locations Discovered" statistic to forever be off by one.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- You may still hear the word wall music when you return to this location, even if you previously killed the dragon and Krosis, learned the shout, and cleared the location.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.7, fixes this bug.
  -  The console command `"f09f6".disable` will stop the music, while the command `"f09f2".disable` will stop the sizzling sound effect.

# Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Shimmermist Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shimmermist+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
