| Northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") East of [Whitewatch Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Whitewatch_Tower "Skyrim:Whitewatch Tower") | |

Shimmermist Cave

**Shimmermist Cave** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains two zones: *[Shimmermist Cave](#Shimmermist_Cave)* and *[Shimmermist Grotto](#Shimmermist_Grotto)*.

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Outside the cave are several menacing Falmer totems that should be a sign to stay away. There is also a patch of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus just to the right of the entrance. This cave system can be very difficult for low-level players to clear.

### Shimmermist Cave

Entering the cave, it is strikingly unique with a plethora of bioluminescent flora and natural lighting. There are many [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") to be harvested throughout the cave system and [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") found throughout the second zone. The ambiance is beautiful with shimmering opalescent ceilings, green glows, and flowing mist. Having a [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Light "Skyrim:Light") source or [Night Eye](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Eye_(power) "Skyrim:Night Eye (power)") is recommended after this room as [traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps "Skyrim:Traps") are hard to see and areas where the Falmer dwell are the darkest portions of the cave.

The entrance leads into a passage that descends to the north before turning east and continuing to descend. On your right you will pass an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus, and ahead you will be able to see an earthen bridge crossing a pool of water fed by two waterfalls pouring down the walls. There are ramps leading down into the water, where you can catch a [direfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Direfish "Skyrim:Direfish") and five [tripod spiderfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripod_Spiderfish "Skyrim:Tripod Spiderfish"). Above you on the north wall is a ledge that is used as a short-cut back to the exit. On the far side of the bridge is a leveled creature (from a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") up to at least a chaurus). The path enters another narrow passage that continues to the east before turning south and opening out into a chamber with a ledge above you. There is a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") growing in the darkened passage, and right by the exit into the next chamber is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap from above. There is a Falmer standing on the ledge keeping watch, and on the right is a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") containing a concealed Falmer. To the left of the hive are the bodies of three [dead bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead) "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") with several [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") on the ground among them. To the east is a Falmer tent with a closed gate blocking access to the interior. There is an unlocked Falmer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the left, and inside the tent is a small fire and a patch of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus. The path continues past the tent and curves around to the west as it climbs a ramp up. There is another fly amanita and a bleeding crown fungi along this path. At the top there is an opening heading west that leads into another chamber, where the Falmer previously seen was standing on the edge of the ledge. Following the ledge west along the edge you come to a rock with two [Falmer helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Helmet "Skyrim:Falmer Helmet"), a [Falmer bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow") and quiver of [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Arrow "Skyrim:Falmer Arrow"), a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe"), and two loose chaurus eggs on top. Farther to the rear against the west wall are four more patches of fly amanita fungus. To the south is another narrow passage that after a few turns and passing a patch of bleeding crown fungus opens out into yet another chamber with several rock pillars around the chamber and a leveled Falmer standing beside an unlocked Falmer chest, with three white cap fungus beside them at the rear. To the right of the chest is a passage descending to the south. The passage leads to the entrance to *Shimmermist Grotto*.

### Shimmermist Grotto

The grotto is the deepest portion of the cave system and by far the deadlier one. Falmer are found in larger numbers and, descending deeper, many chaurus egg sacs begin to appear. The passage leads out on to a ledge with two leveled Falmer opposite, next to a Falmer tent with gates on the entrance. In front of the tent is a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), and inside are several chaurus egg sacs and an unlocked Falmer chest. There is an earthen ramp leading down to the southwest. At the bottom a narrow passage heads west and leads to a chamber guarded by a chaurus. There is a skeleton in the middle of the floor. The exit is to the south; after a short passage it turns and opens into another chamber with two leveled chaurus in a feeding pit below. There is a ramp down on your right and a bridge that crosses the pit ahead. In the bottom of the pit there are three more skeletons. Another ramp leads back up on the far side, east of the bridge. To the west is an unlocked Falmer chest, to the right of a narrow passage. This continues to the west before turning south and entering a wider passage guarded by a leveled Falmer. There are a couple more fly amanita and white cap fungi growing in the passage (see [bugs](#Bugs)). The architecture changes to that found in Dwemer ruins, with a pair of metal doors at the end.

Beyond the doors is a room containing a leveled Falmer and a [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") standing in a docking station. Both enemies are formidable foes, and separating them is key (see [notes](#Notes) for tactics that may help to defeat them). Low-level players will likely die in one or two hits from either one, even from being near the Dwarven centurion as its steam vents can be fatal. Dwarven centurions have difficulty maneuvering corners and can't fit into small spaces, which can be exploited to destroy it with ranged attacks. In front of this is a stone table with two loose chaurus eggs, three [Dwemer cogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"), a [Falmer sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Falmer Sword"), a Falmer war axe, and various pieces of Dwemer metal. To the right of the docking station is an unlocked Falmer chest and a Falmer tent. To the east under a ledge is a partially buried dresser containing various Dwemer metal items. In the eastern corner is a ramp leading up to the ledge and the passage back to the first zone. The passage returns you to the chamber containing the pool, on the north side on a ledge above the water. From here retrace your steps to the exit.

## Notes

- It is possible to bypass the initial Falmer cave area and go straight to the grotto. In the first room with the bridge and waterfalls, cross the bridge then immediately bear left and jump up the rocks to the tunnel that leads to the grotto. You will emerge on a stone shelf directly across from the Falmer; the Falmer will be able to access your position, but the centurion will not if you back up slightly. It is also possible to reach this ledge by climbing the rock in the center of the bridge and using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").
- If the centurion is lured to the preceding hallway, it will become stuck, as the corridor is too short for its tall frame. You may then attack the centurion from range, but beware its steam venting. Another effortless method to defeat the centurion is to hide inside the small hut in the centurion's room. It cannot enter the hut through the small entrance, and will be vulnerable to attack.
- Two [quicksilver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") are outside. The first is in front of a large rock west-southwest of the cave entrance, and the second is south of the rock.

## Bugs

- The fungi in the final passages and ruins don't seem to ever respawn. **?**

# Skyrim:Ships

## Overview

Wreck of the Winter War

 This page lists all the **ships** and **shipwrecks** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload")** — A ship docked north of Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dainty+Sload)
:   **[Dead Man's Dread](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread_(place) "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread (place)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread") — An ancient ship located within the Grotto on Blackbone Isle. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dead+Man%27s+Dread)
:    **[Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly")** — A shipwreck northeast of Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hela%27s+Folly)
:    **[The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah")** — The personal transport vessel of the Emperor, Titus Mede II. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Katariah)
:   **[The North Wind](/wiki/Skyrim:The_North_Wind "Skyrim:The North Wind")** — A ship docked at the Windhelm docks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+North+Wind)
:   **[Northern Maiden](/wiki/Skyrim:Northern_Maiden "Skyrim:Northern Maiden")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A ship initially docked at the Windhelm docks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=141040&y=34208&zoom=15)
:    **[Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear")** — A shipwreck west of Ravenscar Hollow on the northern coast. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan%27s+Tear)
:    **[Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench")** — A deep underwater ravine northwest of Winterhold consisting of four submerged shipwrecks. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pilgrim%27s+Trench)
:   **[Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave")** — A pirate ship docked at Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Wave)
:   **[The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall")** — A ship docked in Dawnstar's Northstar Port. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Sea+Squall)
:    **[Wreck Of The Brinehammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_Of_The_Brinehammer "Skyrim:Wreck Of The Brinehammer")** — A shipwreck northwest of Dawnstar along the shore of the Sea of Ghosts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+Of+The+Brinehammer)
:    **[Wreck of the Icerunner](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Icerunner "Skyrim:Wreck of the Icerunner")** — An Imperial ship which will run aground east of Solitude containing Blackblood Marauders and the assassin Deeja. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Icerunner)
:    **[Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_The_Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Wreck of The Pride of Tel Vos")** — A shipwreck on a small island east of Winterhold. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+The+Pride+of+Tel+Vos)
:    **[Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A shipwreck south-southeast of Raven Rock containing reavers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Strident+Squall)
:    **[Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War")** — A shipwreck east-southeast of Snow Veil Sanctum and far northeast of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wreck+of+the+Winter+War)

# Skyrim:Shiv

## Overview

*"Ah, you want protection? I can get you what you need."*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to your fellow inmates.
2. Ask [Grisvar the Unlucky](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky") for his spare [shiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv_(item) "Skyrim:Shiv (item)").
3. Obtain a bottle of [Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma").
4. Swap the Skooma for Grisvar's spare shiv.

### So what are you in for?

Before throwing you into [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), the guards were careful enough to remove all of your equipment, leaving weapon-based characters at a distinct disadvantage. If you chat to your fellow inmates, however, you will learn that [Grisvar the Unlucky](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky") has a spare weapon, and might be willing to let you have it.

### If you want to get ahead, get a shiv

Grisvar admits to having an extra [shiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv_(item) "Skyrim:Shiv (item)") but isn't keen to part with it. He is something of a [Skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") addict, and has heard that [Duach](/wiki/Skyrim:Duach "Skyrim:Duach") has got a bottle of the good stuff. Grisvar claims to be "shaking just thinking about it", and wants you to obtain the bottle for him.

### Distilled Pleasure

Grisvar isn't as discerning as his request makes him seem, and will accept any bottle of Skooma. Several of the mine's inmates possess bottles of Skooma but Duach is often to be found on his own, making it easier to pick his pockets or kill him quietly. You can also try to pass a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") check with Duach or beat him in a brawl to make him hand over his bottle. However you obtain the Skooma, take it back to Grisvar.

### Forlorn hope

The Skooma is warmly received, and Grisvar gladly hands over his spare shiv. He asks you to promise you won't ever use it on him - and it's perhaps just as well that no option to accept the promise is offered.

## Quest Stages

| Shiv (FreeformCidhnaMineA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Talk to Grisvar about getting a shiv |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Get a bottle of Skooma for Grisvar |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Bring Grisvar the Skooma |
| 35 |  | *Objective 30:* Bring Grisvar the Skooma |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 40, 50, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformCidhnaMineA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformCidhnaMineA`.

Shor's Stone

**Shor's Stone** is a mining [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in the northern [Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift").

It is north-northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") in the pass between the Rift and [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). The town's name is taken from the [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") god [Shor](/wiki/Lore:Shor "Lore:Shor"). The residents are having trouble with [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") that have infested the local [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") mine, [Redbelly Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Redbelly_Mine "Skyrim:Redbelly Mine").

## Notes

- An [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") are due north of [Sylgja's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Sylgja%27s_House "Skyrim:Sylgja's House").
- Shor's Stone is the only town besides [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") that operates with its own [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone_Guard "Skyrim:Shor's Stone Guard").
- Animals spawn very close to Shor's Stone, which may occasionally cause fights to break out between the villagers and animals.
- Music tends to play irregularly in the area, as you can hear one song fade and another replace it.
- Shor's Stone also [appears](/wiki/Online:Shor%27s_Stone "Online:Shor's Stone") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

# Skyrim:Shor's Watchtower

## Overview

| North-northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") South of [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") | |

Shor's Watchtower

**Shor's Watchtower** is a small [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") north-northeast of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone").

## Walkthrough

The watchtower is just north of Shor's Stone along the main road in the pass between [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") and [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). Depending on the faction that currently controls the Rift, the watchtower contains either the corpses of [Riften guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Guard "Skyrim:Riften Guard") or [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier"). The view to the north from the top of the tower includes [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and the northern coast of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") beyond.

Outside the entrance to the watchtower is a campfire with the bodies of two guards nearby. Through the doorway into the tower is a small room with wooden supports at regular intervals. Against the east wall is the start of several flights of stairs that spiral up to the top of the tower. Against the west wall, immediately on your left as you enter, are four weapon racks holding a selection of predominately [iron weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons"). Farther to the right is a long wooden table holding two pieces of cheese, two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a letter (of which there is both an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Letter "Skyrim:Imperial Letter") and a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Watchtower_Guard%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Watchtower Guard's Letter") version) promising reinforcements and warning of an impending attack. There are no signs of either the reinforcements or the attacking forces. On the ground under the stairs is a healing potion along with several crates and sacks containing [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). As you climb the stairs, you will pass a barrel with a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on top and see several patches of blood splattered against the walls and stairs. At the top are the bodies of two more unfortunate guards, a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot, and more sacks of food. All of the guards have all their belongings still on them and can be looted.

## Bugs

- At times, the letter cannot be activated.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  - If the letter cannot be activated, sometimes looking at the ground below the table still makes it possible to interact.
- The dead Riften guards are called "Riften Guards" even though they aren't actually in Riften.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. They will now be called "Rift Guards".
  - This won't be an issue if the Rift is under Imperial control, as the dead Imperial soldiers will properly be called "Imperial Soldiers".

A word wall

### Radiant Dungeons

This quest can send you to *almost* any dungeon or dragon lair that contains a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). The list of possible values of `Dungeon` is:

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") | [Ancient's Ascent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient%27s_Ascent "Skyrim:Ancient's Ascent") [Shriekwind Bastion](/wiki/Skyrim:Shriekwind_Bastion "Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion") [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge") | [Kilkreath Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") [Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge") | [Dead Men's Respite](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Men%27s_Respite "Skyrim:Dead Men's Respite") [Eldersblood The list of word walls you will *not* be sent to includes the following, most of which have an associated quest. In addition to those listed here, no Dawnguard or Dragonborn word walls will ever be targeted by this quest except Arcwind Point.

## Walkthrough

After you use a [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") in a settlement, a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") will find you and give you a *[Letter from a Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_a_Friend "Skyrim:Letter from a Friend")*, which provides the location of a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") when you read it. Traveling to the location and learning the Word of Power from the wall completes the quest.

This quest can be repeated multiple times, and can also be active simultaneously with the other quest to locate word walls, [The Words of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power"). Both quests can even point you to the same word wall as the other.

## Notes

- This quest can be triggered while shouting in a dungeon, not only in a settlement. Oddly, it can possibly even direct you to the same dungeon where you used the shout. The bug below may occur if the shout is used in the dungeon before finding the word wall in that same dungeon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. The quest will no longer be triggered by shouting in uninhabited locations; and specifically, only habitations/dwellings/military encampments will trigger it.

## Bugs

- This quest may point you to a word wall that you have already visited, in which case your quest marker will lead you to a word wall with chanting and sound effects as though there were a word to learn on it, however none of the words will be highlighted. This prevents you from completing the quest and from obtaining another quest to find a word wall.
  -  Use the console code `SetStage WICastMagic04 200` to complete the quest.
- The shouts added with the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") and [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-ons were never inserted into the formlist used by the "letter from a friend" event trigger. There is no reason for them to be absent from the formlist.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, fixes this bug.
- This quest can be triggered by shouting inside empty buildings, abandoned houses, dungeons, and other locations where you are unlikely to have been seen shouting by a "friend."
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. You must now be seen shouting somewhere in a city, town, inn, military camp, or the like.
- Sometimes when going to the word wall, the word will not even appear even though you don't have it yet. This can be fixed by reloading a previous save.

## Quest Stages

| Shout - learn about word wall (WICastMagic04) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Find the source of power in <Alias=Dungeon> |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WICastMagic04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WICastMagic04`.

# Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion

## Overview

Shriekwind Bastion

**Shriekwind Bastion** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Shriekwind Bastion](#Shriekwind_Bastion)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Although the interior of the ruin is named "Shriekwind Bastion", the map markers for the two entrances are named "North Shriekwind Bastion" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=North+Shriekwind+Bastion&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "South Shriekwind Bastion" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=South+Shriekwind+Bastion&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. The northern entrance is south of [Lake Ilinatla](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), and the southern entrance is northeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: North Shriekwind Bastion

North Shriekwind Bastion

There is no path leading from the nearby road that runs along the southern shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"); however, the covered entrance can be seen from the road. You may encounter two skeletons who guard a nearby unmarked burial site. A large stone arch forms an open antechamber in front of the entrance, which consists of an unlocked metal gate and an iron door leading into the bastion at the bottom of a short flight of stairs. To the left is a flight of stairs that lead above the antechamber and farther up the mountain. At the top of the first flight of stairs, on a ledge to the left is a birds' nest containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). At this point the path splits, with the main trail going left, while to the right, directly over the entrance are more stairs climbing to a terrace with an unlit brazier at the far end. Inside the brazier is a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and an Ancient Nord weapon. There is a second Ancient Nord weapon and a pair of [ancient Nord boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Boots "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Boots") beside the brazier. The main trail passes under a square arch formed by a stone placed atop two upright stones a few paces apart, before circling around and above the first terrace. Near the top, under a low arch is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Above the chest, climbing another flight of stairs on the left leads to a lookout point, which provides a good view of the lake and northern [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), and to the northeast, parts of [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"). West of the entrance, down the side of the mountain, there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").

### Exterior: South Shriekwind Bastion

South Shriekwind Bastion

Following the road from Falkreath toward [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), turn left just after the last tree on the left, before you reach the bandit's [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap that spans the road a short distance south of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). The path leads up the mountain to the first terrace. Near the start of the terrace is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). Stairs lead up to a terrace with a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") slumbering in a horizontal sarcophagus in an alcove on the right. Past this, stairs lead down, with more opposite leading back up again. To the left of those that lead back up are more stairs that descend to another lower terrace, where a skeleton is patrolling near a stone hut that contains many candles. At the far end is an unlocked chest resting on a fallen section of masonry. Climbing the stairs to the terrace above leads to another draugr standing in front of another sarcophagus, at the top of a short flight of stairs. To the left of these stairs is an iron door leading into the interior. You may exit this door if you cleared the bastion by starting from the north entrance.

### Shriekwind Bastion

The entrance at [North Shriekwind Bastion](#Exterior:_North_Shriekwind_Bastion) leads to a wide brightly lit passage with novice-locked double-iron doors at the far end. There is a leveled vampire either by the doors or sitting in a circular room on the right. In the room, by one of several chairs is a bucket containing twelve loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Against the rear wall is a sideboard holding two [helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") (one [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and one random), a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), with a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") to the right and an unlocked chest to the left. To the right of the doorway in a small alcove at eye level on the wall are two [iron swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), with a kettle full of skulls below them.

Through the doors is a large room containing a few large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), an empty throne to the left, and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") next to a stone altar with two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top. The bandit is on a circular section of floor under a shaft with a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") above and [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that shoot from the sides of the shaft. On the west wall is a chain that triggers the floor to rise and the spears to shoot from the wall. To the south is a doorway into an overgrown hallway containing a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), with a series of flights of stairs leading up to an iron door. This door leads into some catacombs, with two skeletons at the top of some stairs around the corner to the right. There are a number of empty [coffins](/wiki/Skyrim:Coffin "Skyrim:Coffin") found in alcoves along the walls.

At the top of the stairs, a doorway leads out into a large open area with the trap door seen previously in the center. There is a plinth beside it with a handle in the top, which activates the same trap as before. In the corner is a large tree, and against the north wall are stairs leading up to the first of several pathways rising in terraces around the room. There are a couple skeletons found on each of these levels. Depending on your skill with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), you may be able to clear most, if not all, of these skeletons from ground level. Climbing the long flight of stairs leads up to the first level, where two skeletons are on guard. At the far end is an iron door leading into a small area of catacombs with more empty coffins and a couple [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). A doorway leads into a semicircular room with two doorways on the right-hand wall both leading to the same passage, separated by a blood-soaked raised section with several [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") and a random potion of healing on top. Beside this is a basket of skulls and another random potion of healing. On your left as you enter the room is a set of shelves holding an iron dagger. On the left is an unlocked chest and a large urn, and in an alcove opposite the entrance are a large number and variety of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") and boots, including a pair of the rare [Pleated Shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pleated_Shoes "Skyrim:Pleated Shoes").

Three handles

The passage leads to a small wet area with natural light filtering from above, with eight [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing down the walls and from a beam. There is a lowered gate opposite and a chain on the right which raises the gate. The room beyond contains two skeletons and is overgrown with vegetation. In the center on a block of stone are three handles, with two doorways nearby both blocked by gates; a larger doorway is to the north, and a smaller doorway with two more skeletons is up a short flight of stairs to the southeast. The skeletons can be dealt with using a [fire rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Rune "Skyrim:Fire Rune") as close to the gate as possible. There are also concealed doors to the east and southwest. The handle to the east opens the concealed door to the east, revealing a small area with an open upright coffin containing an iron helmet and random gauntlets. The handle to the southwest opens the concealed door on that wall, where another upright, open coffin contains a random cuirass. The final handle to the northwest opens the southeast gate holding back the two skeletons. Through this doorway is a small room containing an apprentice-locked chest with three chains above. The left-hand chain is the chain you want, as it operates the larger gate to the north. The right-hand chain operates the gate between the room with three handles and the wet room (which is useful if you are following this guide in reverse, from the South entrance to the North one, and thus have come from the northern entrance and need to open the western entrance). Finally, the center chain operates the gate between the room with three handles and this room, shutting you in this room until you pull the center chain again.

Continue through the large gate and follow the corridor around to the left, where several more hanging moss are growing from the walls. There is a skeleton ahead, and three dead skeletons lying on the floor beyond. These can be looted, and beside them is an iron dagger, helmet, and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). The passage beyond the skeletons has two [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") down the middle of the floor, both triggering [battering rams](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"), the first from the ceiling behind you, and the second from the ceiling in front. This passage leads out onto the second level of the large area. There are two more skeletons on this level, unless previously dealt with from below. At the far end, another passage heads away from the open area, before a couple turns lead into a narrower passage, where a doorway on the left enters a torture chamber with a [vampire's thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall") sitting on a throne on the right. The floor is awash with blood, which makes finding the two large [rubies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby") and flawless ruby on the floor difficult. There are two torture racks and a small cage hanging from the ceiling, which contains a [burnt corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Burnt Corpse"). To your left is a chain that triggers a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") to shoot up from the floor and continue burning this corpse. Opposite the entrance, a passage continues up a flight of stairs to a corner with a chair in front of a fireplace and another doorway into a wider passage heading west. On the far wall is a doorway into a small alcove with a random enchanted [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a random helmet, and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"). These are all in front of another concealed door, which is opened with a chain just inside the entrance to the alcove, revealing a passage to the entrance at [South Shriekwind Bastion](#Exterior:_South_Shriekwind_Bastion). If you enter from the south, you will approach this passage and secret door from the other side, where there is a rather more obvious chain to open the door; when you then emerge into the main corridor, turning left leads you downward toward the northern entrance - thus following the description of this guide's previous areas in reverse - whereas turning right leads you farther up the tower, toward the upper chambers.

Climbing the stairs to the west brings you to another overgrown area and an open door into a passage heading east. On your right is a cave-in, and to the left is an empty coffin. The passage leads out onto the top walkway of the open area, with another skeleton (unless previously dealt with) and stairs on the left. Follow the walkway to the far end, where you will find a wide passage with a plinth with a handle in the top by the start, several burnt corpses along the length of the passage, and a doorway at the end blocked by a gate. If you pull the handle, the gate will rise; however, [flamethrower statues](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") along the length of the passage will also activate. There is an alternative: look just to the right of this handle to find a chain on the inside of the passage, which only raises the gate without triggering the flamethrowers.

The final battle

Through the doorway is a flight of stairs leading up to double doors. Through these is a boss vampire standing beside stairs leading up to a brazier that appears filled with blood, with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") or poison on the ground beside it and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")* on a piece of fallen masonry. At the top of the room is a circular passage around a central stairwell, with an unlocked chest and three burial urns against the outside wall and a fourth burial urn against the inner wall. There is a wooden spiral staircase rising to a short passage and a large room with a row of large statues on either side and a sarcophagus in front of the word wall at the far end. As soon as you enter this room, the sarcophagus will burst open and a draugr magic-user will emerge. Between the first and second statues on the right is an unlocked chest. In front of both of the last statues are two plinths with random potions or poisons on [weight sensitive plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), but these don't seem to trigger anything adverse. Approach the word wall to learn a word for the Elemental Fury shout.

### Exterior: Shriekwind Overlook

It is possible to reach this balcony by mountain climbing, avoiding the need to completely traverse the interior to reach the word wall or complete any quests here. The balcony is a small lookout point devoid of anything interesting apart from the view. It is on the northwestern side of the mountain, far above both of the entrances.

## Notes

- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") seem to have problems navigating the passages leading to and from the terraces in the large open area, constantly heading back to the lowest level for each subsequent walkway.
- East of the northern entrance is an unmarked shallow cave containing a pack of [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and a chest. East of the unmarked cave, north of Pinewatch, is a dead [wood cutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Cutter "Skyrim:Wood Cutter") and the unique iron battleaxe [The Woodsman's Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodsman%27s_Friend "Skyrim:The Woodsman's Friend").
- Northwest of the northern entrance, across the road, is an unmarked burial site guarded by two skeletons. There are six graves by a central pillar, banner, and some floral offerings (two sprigs of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), one [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and one [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")). Three patches of [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") give the site some dark color.

## Bugs

- After using the handles to pass the gate to the main chamber, your follower may get stuck and will not rejoin you until you leave the ruin.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - If you walk a corridor or two past the plates, then wait one hour, they should respawn next to you. You can also use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to knock them loose, and they will then follow you.
- The draugr here is also flagged as a boss when only the vampire is supposed to be.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Shriekwind Bastion ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shriekwind+Bastion)) | | |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"), [Skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), [Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") | |

| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 1 |

Shriekwind Bastion

**Shriekwind Bastion** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Shriekwind Bastion](#Shriekwind_Bastion)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Although the interior of the ruin is named "Shriekwind Bastion", the map markers for the two entrances are named "North Shriekwind Bastion" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=North+Shriekwind+Bastion&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "South Shriekwind Bastion" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=South+Shriekwind+Bastion&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. The northern entrance is south of [Lake Ilinatla](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), and the southern entrance is northeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: North Shriekwind Bastion

North Shriekwind Bastion

There is no path leading from the nearby road that runs along the southern shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"); however, the covered entrance can be seen from the road. You may encounter two skeletons who guard a nearby unmarked burial site. A large stone arch forms an open antechamber in front of the entrance, which consists of an unlocked metal gate and an iron door leading into the bastion at the bottom of a short flight of stairs. To the left is a flight of stairs that lead above the antechamber and farther up the mountain. At the top of the first flight of stairs, on a ledge to the left is a birds' nest containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). At this point the path splits, with the main trail going left, while to the right, directly over the entrance are more stairs climbing to a terrace with an unlit brazier at the far end. Inside the brazier is a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and an Ancient Nord weapon. There is a second Ancient Nord weapon and a pair of [ancient Nord boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Boots "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Boots") beside the brazier. The main trail passes under a square arch formed by a stone placed atop two upright stones a few paces apart, before circling around and above the first terrace. Near the top, under a low arch is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Above the chest, climbing another flight of stairs on the left leads to a lookout point, which provides a good view of the lake and northern [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), and to the northeast, parts of [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"). West of the entrance, down the side of the mountain, there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").

### Exterior: South Shriekwind Bastion

South Shriekwind Bastion

Following the road from Falkreath toward [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), turn left just after the last tree on the left, before you reach the bandit's [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap that spans the road a short distance south of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). The path leads up the mountain to the first terrace. Near the start of the terrace is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). Stairs lead up to a terrace with a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") slumbering in a horizontal sarcophagus in an alcove on the right. Past this, stairs lead down, with more opposite leading back up again. To the left of those that lead back up are more stairs that descend to another lower terrace, where a skeleton is patrolling near a stone hut that contains many candles. At the far end is an unlocked chest resting on a fallen section of masonry. Climbing the stairs to the terrace above leads to another draugr standing in front of another sarcophagus, at the top of a short flight of stairs. To the left of these stairs is an iron door leading into the interior. You may exit this door if you cleared the bastion by starting from the north entrance.

### Shriekwind Bastion

The entrance at [North Shriekwind Bastion](#Exterior:_North_Shriekwind_Bastion) leads to a wide brightly lit passage with novice-locked double-iron doors at the far end. There is a leveled vampire either by the doors or sitting in a circular room on the right. In the room, by one of several chairs is a bucket containing twelve loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Against the rear wall is a sideboard holding two [helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") (one [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and one random), a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), with a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") to the right and an unlocked chest to the left. To the right of the doorway in a small alcove at eye level on the wall are two [iron swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), with a kettle full of skulls below them.

Through the doors is a large room containing a few large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), an empty throne to the left, and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") next to a stone altar with two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top. The bandit is on a circular section of floor under a shaft with a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") above and [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that shoot from the sides of the shaft. On the west wall is a chain that triggers the floor to rise and the spears to shoot from the wall. To the south is a doorway into an overgrown hallway containing a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), with a series of flights of stairs leading up to an iron door. This door leads into some catacombs, with two skeletons at the top of some stairs around the corner to the right. There are a number of empty [coffins](/wiki/Skyrim:Coffin "Skyrim:Coffin") found in alcoves along the walls.

At the top of the stairs, a doorway leads out into a large open area with the trap door seen previously in the center. There is a plinth beside it with a handle in the top, which activates the same trap as before. In the corner is a large tree, and against the north wall are stairs leading up to the first of several pathways rising in terraces around the room. There are a couple skeletons found on each of these levels. Depending on your skill with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), you may be able to clear most, if not all, of these skeletons from ground level. Climbing the long flight of stairs leads up to the first level, where two skeletons are on guard. At the far end is an iron door leading into a small area of catacombs with more empty coffins and a couple [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). A doorway leads into a semicircular room with two doorways on the right-hand wall both leading to the same passage, separated by a blood-soaked raised section with several [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") and a random potion of healing on top. Beside this is a basket of skulls and another random potion of healing. On your left as you enter the room is a set of shelves holding an iron dagger. On the left is an unlocked chest and a large urn, and in an alcove opposite the entrance are a large number and variety of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") and boots, including a pair of the rare [Pleated Shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pleated_Shoes "Skyrim:Pleated Shoes").

Three handles

The passage leads to a small wet area with natural light filtering from above, with eight [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing down the walls and from a beam. There is a lowered gate opposite and a chain on the right which raises the gate. The room beyond contains two skeletons and is overgrown with vegetation. In the center on a block of stone are three handles, with two doorways nearby both blocked by gates; a larger doorway is to the north, and a smaller doorway with two more skeletons is up a short flight of stairs to the southeast. The skeletons can be dealt with using a [fire rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Rune "Skyrim:Fire Rune") as close to the gate as possible. There are also concealed doors to the east and southwest. The handle to the east opens the concealed door to the east, revealing a small area with an open upright coffin containing an iron helmet and random gauntlets. The handle to the southwest opens the concealed door on that wall, where another upright, open coffin contains a random cuirass. The final handle to the northwest opens the southeast gate holding back the two skeletons. Through this doorway is a small room containing an apprentice-locked chest with three chains above. The left-hand chain is the chain you want, as it operates the larger gate to the north. The right-hand chain operates the gate between the room with three handles and the wet room (which is useful if you are following this guide in reverse, from the South entrance to the North one, and thus have come from the northern entrance and need to open the western entrance). Finally, the center chain operates the gate between the room with three handles and this room, shutting you in this room until you pull the center chain again.

Continue through the large gate and follow the corridor around to the left, where several more hanging moss are growing from the walls. There is a skeleton ahead, and three dead skeletons lying on the floor beyond. These can be looted, and beside them is an iron dagger, helmet, and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). The passage beyond the skeletons has two [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") down the middle of the floor, both triggering [battering rams](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"), the first from the ceiling behind you, and the second from the ceiling in front. This passage leads out onto the second level of the large area. There are two more skeletons on this level, unless previously dealt with from below. At the far end, another passage heads away from the open area, before a couple turns lead into a narrower passage, where a doorway on the left enters a torture chamber with a [vampire's thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall") sitting on a throne on the right. The floor is awash with blood, which makes finding the two large [rubies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby") and flawless ruby on the floor difficult. There are two torture racks and a small cage hanging from the ceiling, which contains a [burnt corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Burnt Corpse"). To your left is a chain that triggers a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") to shoot up from the floor and continue burning this corpse. Opposite the entrance, a passage continues up a flight of stairs to a corner with a chair in front of a fireplace and another doorway into a wider passage heading west. On the far wall is a doorway into a small alcove with a random enchanted [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a random helmet, and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"). These are all in front of another concealed door, which is opened with a chain just inside the entrance to the alcove, revealing a passage to the entrance at [South Shriekwind Bastion](#Exterior:_South_Shriekwind_Bastion). If you enter from the south, you will approach this passage and secret door from the other side, where there is a rather more obvious chain to open the door; when you then emerge into the main corridor, turning left leads you downward toward the northern entrance - thus following the description of this guide's previous areas in reverse - whereas turning right leads you farther up the tower, toward the upper chambers.

Climbing the stairs to the west brings you to another overgrown area and an open door into a passage heading east. On your right is a cave-in, and to the left is an empty coffin. The passage leads out onto the top walkway of the open area, with another skeleton (unless previously dealt with) and stairs on the left. Follow the walkway to the far end, where you will find a wide passage with a plinth with a handle in the top by the start, several burnt corpses along the length of the passage, and a doorway at the end blocked by a gate. If you pull the handle, the gate will rise; however, [flamethrower statues](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") along the length of the passage will also activate. There is an alternative: look just to the right of this handle to find a chain on the inside of the passage, which only raises the gate without triggering the flamethrowers.

The final battle

Through the doorway is a flight of stairs leading up to double doors. Through these is a boss vampire standing beside stairs leading up to a brazier that appears filled with blood, with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") or poison on the ground beside it and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")* on a piece of fallen masonry. At the top of the room is a circular passage around a central stairwell, with an unlocked chest and three burial urns against the outside wall and a fourth burial urn against the inner wall. There is a wooden spiral staircase rising to a short passage and a large room with a row of large statues on either side and a sarcophagus in front of the word wall at the far end. As soon as you enter this room, the sarcophagus will burst open and a draugr magic-user will emerge. Between the first and second statues on the right is an unlocked chest. In front of both of the last statues are two plinths with random potions or poisons on [weight sensitive plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), but these don't seem to trigger anything adverse. Approach the word wall to learn a word for the Elemental Fury shout.

### Exterior: Shriekwind Overlook

It is possible to reach this balcony by mountain climbing, avoiding the need to completely traverse the interior to reach the word wall or complete any quests here. The balcony is a small lookout point devoid of anything interesting apart from the view. It is on the northwestern side of the mountain, far above both of the entrances.

## Notes

- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") seem to have problems navigating the passages leading to and from the terraces in the large open area, constantly heading back to the lowest level for each subsequent walkway.
- East of the northern entrance is an unmarked shallow cave containing a pack of [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and a chest. East of the unmarked cave, north of Pinewatch, is a dead [wood cutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Cutter "Skyrim:Wood Cutter") and the unique iron battleaxe [The Woodsman's Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodsman%27s_Friend "Skyrim:The Woodsman's Friend").
- Northwest of the northern entrance, across the road, is an unmarked burial site guarded by two skeletons. There are six graves by a central pillar, banner, and some floral offerings (two sprigs of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), one [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and one [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")). Three patches of [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") give the site some dark color.

## Bugs

- After using the handles to pass the gate to the main chamber, your follower may get stuck and will not rejoin you until you leave the ruin.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - If you walk a corridor or two past the plates, then wait one hour, they should respawn next to you. You can also use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to knock them loose, and they will then follow you.
- The draugr here is also flagged as a boss when only the vampire is supposed to be.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Shriekwind Bastion

## Overview

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
