| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 1 |

Shriekwind Bastion

**Shriekwind Bastion** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Shriekwind Bastion](#Shriekwind_Bastion)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Elemental Fury](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Fury "Skyrim:Elemental Fury") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Although the interior of the ruin is named "Shriekwind Bastion", the map markers for the two entrances are named "North Shriekwind Bastion" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=North+Shriekwind+Bastion&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "South Shriekwind Bastion" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=South+Shriekwind+Bastion&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. The northern entrance is south of [Lake Ilinatla](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), and the southern entrance is northeast of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").

## Related Quests

- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: North Shriekwind Bastion

North Shriekwind Bastion

There is no path leading from the nearby road that runs along the southern shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"); however, the covered entrance can be seen from the road. You may encounter two skeletons who guard a nearby unmarked burial site. A large stone arch forms an open antechamber in front of the entrance, which consists of an unlocked metal gate and an iron door leading into the bastion at the bottom of a short flight of stairs. To the left is a flight of stairs that lead above the antechamber and farther up the mountain. At the top of the first flight of stairs, on a ledge to the left is a birds' nest containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). At this point the path splits, with the main trail going left, while to the right, directly over the entrance are more stairs climbing to a terrace with an unlit brazier at the far end. Inside the brazier is a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and an Ancient Nord weapon. There is a second Ancient Nord weapon and a pair of [ancient Nord boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Boots "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Boots") beside the brazier. The main trail passes under a square arch formed by a stone placed atop two upright stones a few paces apart, before circling around and above the first terrace. Near the top, under a low arch is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Above the chest, climbing another flight of stairs on the left leads to a lookout point, which provides a good view of the lake and northern [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), and to the northeast, parts of [Bleak Falls Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleak_Falls_Barrow_(place) "Skyrim:Bleak Falls Barrow (place)"). West of the entrance, down the side of the mountain, there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein").

### Exterior: South Shriekwind Bastion

South Shriekwind Bastion

Following the road from Falkreath toward [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"), turn left just after the last tree on the left, before you reach the bandit's [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap that spans the road a short distance south of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"). The path leads up the mountain to the first terrace. Near the start of the terrace is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). Stairs lead up to a terrace with a leveled [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") slumbering in a horizontal sarcophagus in an alcove on the right. Past this, stairs lead down, with more opposite leading back up again. To the left of those that lead back up are more stairs that descend to another lower terrace, where a skeleton is patrolling near a stone hut that contains many candles. At the far end is an unlocked chest resting on a fallen section of masonry. Climbing the stairs to the terrace above leads to another draugr standing in front of another sarcophagus, at the top of a short flight of stairs. To the left of these stairs is an iron door leading into the interior. You may exit this door if you cleared the bastion by starting from the north entrance.

### Shriekwind Bastion

The entrance at [North Shriekwind Bastion](#Exterior:_North_Shriekwind_Bastion) leads to a wide brightly lit passage with novice-locked double-iron doors at the far end. There is a leveled vampire either by the doors or sitting in a circular room on the right. In the room, by one of several chairs is a bucket containing twelve loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Against the rear wall is a sideboard holding two [helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") (one [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and one random), a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), a random pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), with a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") to the right and an unlocked chest to the left. To the right of the doorway in a small alcove at eye level on the wall are two [iron swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), with a kettle full of skulls below them.

Through the doors is a large room containing a few large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), an empty throne to the left, and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") next to a stone altar with two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons") on top. The bandit is on a circular section of floor under a shaft with a [trap door](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") above and [spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that shoot from the sides of the shaft. On the west wall is a chain that triggers the floor to rise and the spears to shoot from the wall. To the south is a doorway into an overgrown hallway containing a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), with a series of flights of stairs leading up to an iron door. This door leads into some catacombs, with two skeletons at the top of some stairs around the corner to the right. There are a number of empty [coffins](/wiki/Skyrim:Coffin "Skyrim:Coffin") found in alcoves along the walls.

At the top of the stairs, a doorway leads out into a large open area with the trap door seen previously in the center. There is a plinth beside it with a handle in the top, which activates the same trap as before. In the corner is a large tree, and against the north wall are stairs leading up to the first of several pathways rising in terraces around the room. There are a couple skeletons found on each of these levels. Depending on your skill with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), you may be able to clear most, if not all, of these skeletons from ground level. Climbing the long flight of stairs leads up to the first level, where two skeletons are on guard. At the far end is an iron door leading into a small area of catacombs with more empty coffins and a couple [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). A doorway leads into a semicircular room with two doorways on the right-hand wall both leading to the same passage, separated by a blood-soaked raised section with several [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") and a random potion of healing on top. Beside this is a basket of skulls and another random potion of healing. On your left as you enter the room is a set of shelves holding an iron dagger. On the left is an unlocked chest and a large urn, and in an alcove opposite the entrance are a large number and variety of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") and boots, including a pair of the rare [Pleated Shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pleated_Shoes "Skyrim:Pleated Shoes").

Three handles

The passage leads to a small wet area with natural light filtering from above, with eight [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing down the walls and from a beam. There is a lowered gate opposite and a chain on the right which raises the gate. The room beyond contains two skeletons and is overgrown with vegetation. In the center on a block of stone are three handles, with two doorways nearby both blocked by gates; a larger doorway is to the north, and a smaller doorway with two more skeletons is up a short flight of stairs to the southeast. The skeletons can be dealt with using a [fire rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Rune "Skyrim:Fire Rune") as close to the gate as possible. There are also concealed doors to the east and southwest. The handle to the east opens the concealed door to the east, revealing a small area with an open upright coffin containing an iron helmet and random gauntlets. The handle to the southwest opens the concealed door on that wall, where another upright, open coffin contains a random cuirass. The final handle to the northwest opens the southeast gate holding back the two skeletons. Through this doorway is a small room containing an apprentice-locked chest with three chains above. The left-hand chain is the chain you want, as it operates the larger gate to the north. The right-hand chain operates the gate between the room with three handles and the wet room (which is useful if you are following this guide in reverse, from the South entrance to the North one, and thus have come from the northern entrance and need to open the western entrance). Finally, the center chain operates the gate between the room with three handles and this room, shutting you in this room until you pull the center chain again.

Continue through the large gate and follow the corridor around to the left, where several more hanging moss are growing from the walls. There is a skeleton ahead, and three dead skeletons lying on the floor beyond. These can be looted, and beside them is an iron dagger, helmet, and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). The passage beyond the skeletons has two [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") down the middle of the floor, both triggering [battering rams](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"), the first from the ceiling behind you, and the second from the ceiling in front. This passage leads out onto the second level of the large area. There are two more skeletons on this level, unless previously dealt with from below. At the far end, another passage heads away from the open area, before a couple turns lead into a narrower passage, where a doorway on the left enters a torture chamber with a [vampire's thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire's Thrall") sitting on a throne on the right. The floor is awash with blood, which makes finding the two large [rubies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby") and flawless ruby on the floor difficult. There are two torture racks and a small cage hanging from the ceiling, which contains a [burnt corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Corpse "Skyrim:Burnt Corpse"). To your left is a chain that triggers a [flame spout trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") to shoot up from the floor and continue burning this corpse. Opposite the entrance, a passage continues up a flight of stairs to a corner with a chair in front of a fireplace and another doorway into a wider passage heading west. On the far wall is a doorway into a small alcove with a random enchanted [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a random helmet, and a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"). These are all in front of another concealed door, which is opened with a chain just inside the entrance to the alcove, revealing a passage to the entrance at [South Shriekwind Bastion](#Exterior:_South_Shriekwind_Bastion). If you enter from the south, you will approach this passage and secret door from the other side, where there is a rather more obvious chain to open the door; when you then emerge into the main corridor, turning left leads you downward toward the northern entrance - thus following the description of this guide's previous areas in reverse - whereas turning right leads you farther up the tower, toward the upper chambers.

Climbing the stairs to the west brings you to another overgrown area and an open door into a passage heading east. On your right is a cave-in, and to the left is an empty coffin. The passage leads out onto the top walkway of the open area, with another skeleton (unless previously dealt with) and stairs on the left. Follow the walkway to the far end, where you will find a wide passage with a plinth with a handle in the top by the start, several burnt corpses along the length of the passage, and a doorway at the end blocked by a gate. If you pull the handle, the gate will rise; however, [flamethrower statues](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") along the length of the passage will also activate. There is an alternative: look just to the right of this handle to find a chain on the inside of the passage, which only raises the gate without triggering the flamethrowers.

The final battle

Through the doorway is a flight of stairs leading up to double doors. Through these is a boss vampire standing beside stairs leading up to a brazier that appears filled with blood, with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") or poison on the ground beside it and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")* on a piece of fallen masonry. At the top of the room is a circular passage around a central stairwell, with an unlocked chest and three burial urns against the outside wall and a fourth burial urn against the inner wall. There is a wooden spiral staircase rising to a short passage and a large room with a row of large statues on either side and a sarcophagus in front of the word wall at the far end. As soon as you enter this room, the sarcophagus will burst open and a draugr magic-user will emerge. Between the first and second statues on the right is an unlocked chest. In front of both of the last statues are two plinths with random potions or poisons on [weight sensitive plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), but these don't seem to trigger anything adverse. Approach the word wall to learn a word for the Elemental Fury shout.

### Exterior: Shriekwind Overlook

It is possible to reach this balcony by mountain climbing, avoiding the need to completely traverse the interior to reach the word wall or complete any quests here. The balcony is a small lookout point devoid of anything interesting apart from the view. It is on the northwestern side of the mountain, far above both of the entrances.

## Notes

- [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") seem to have problems navigating the passages leading to and from the terraces in the large open area, constantly heading back to the lowest level for each subsequent walkway.
- East of the northern entrance is an unmarked shallow cave containing a pack of [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") and a chest. East of the unmarked cave, north of Pinewatch, is a dead [wood cutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Cutter "Skyrim:Wood Cutter") and the unique iron battleaxe [The Woodsman's Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Woodsman%27s_Friend "Skyrim:The Woodsman's Friend").
- Northwest of the northern entrance, across the road, is an unmarked burial site guarded by two skeletons. There are six graves by a central pillar, banner, and some floral offerings (two sprigs of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), one [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and one [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")). Three patches of [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") give the site some dark color.

## Bugs

- After using the handles to pass the gate to the main chamber, your follower may get stuck and will not rejoin you until you leave the ruin.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  - If you walk a corridor or two past the plates, then wait one hour, they should respawn next to you. You can also use the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to knock them loose, and they will then follow you.
- The draugr here is also flagged as a boss when only the vampire is supposed to be.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

Shrine of Azura

The **Shrine of Azura** is the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Azura](/wiki/Lore:Azura "Lore:Azura").

The shrine at night

## Related Quests

- **[The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star")**: Help find and repair [Azura's Star](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star "Skyrim:Azura's Star").

## Walkthrough

The shrine is south of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") on the summit of a tall mountain. The path leading to the shrine is found not far south of [Whistling Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Whistling_Mine "Skyrim:Whistling Mine"), and rises sharply to the west. To reach it, travel southeast along the path from Winterhold in the direction of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). If the weather is clear, or if you use the [Clear Skies](/wiki/Skyrim:Clear_Skies "Skyrim:Clear Skies") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), it is possible to see a long way in all directions from the shrine.

The shrine sits atop a stone fort-like structure that was supposedly built by [Dunmer](/wiki/Lore:Dunmer "Lore:Dunmer"), who revere Azura. There is an altar in front of the massive statue; [Aranea Ienith](/wiki/Skyrim:Aranea_Ienith "Skyrim:Aranea Ienith") spends all her time worshipping before the altar when not [following](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") you. To the right of the altar on a level below is a small camp, which consists of a small tent containing an unowned bedroll and a collection of crates and sacks containing food.

## Notes

- [Faldrus](/wiki/Skyrim:Faldrus "Skyrim:Faldrus") can be seen in a [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions "Skyrim:World Interactions") on a pilgrimage to the shrine. You can ask him where the shrine is, and he'll mark its location on your map. He will join Aranea Ienith in front of the statue if you follow him there and he survives his pilgrimage to the shrine. Otherwise, he will disappear from the game after you leave him.
- Some innkeepers, such as [Orgnar](/wiki/Skyrim:Orgnar "Skyrim:Orgnar"), will also mark the shrine's location on your map if you ask them for rumors.

# Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |

Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

The **Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon** is the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Lore:Mehrunes_Dagon "Lore:Mehrunes Dagon"). It contains only one zone, *[Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](#Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

### Exterior

The easiest way to reach the shrine is to travel southwest from [the Lord Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lord_Stone "Skyrim:The Lord Stone"). Before the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past") is completed, you will only find the stone altar in front of the key-locked door to Dagon's shrine. At the end of the quest, two [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora "Skyrim:Dremora") will attack you. Each carries a copy of the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Mehrunes%27_Shrine "Skyrim:Key to Mehrunes' Shrine") which opens the door to the shrine. After completing the quest, the two Dremora will respawn every 10 days, and will attack on sight.

A [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") is 130 feet west-northwest of the shrine. It may be reached by dropping off the cliff near the boss chest at [Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar") and proceeding north to the ledge with the ore vein. On the south side of the peak with Dagon's statue is a stash of items, including a randomly enchanted helm and war axe, two potions, three gemstones, a burial urn, and a chest. The stash is to the right of a stone cairn and beneath a stylized dragon glyph.

### Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

Princely prizes

Upon entering, you will be in an icy tunnel. Follow it until it opens into the shrine proper, and deal with the two Dremora inside. There is a raised area in front of you with a short flight of stairs leading up, and two other short sets of ascending stairs to the same raised area at both the eastern and western ends of the small cave. The stairs are separated by large stone pillars. Turning to the left as you enter the main cave, you will find a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") against the north wall. Against the east wall is an open chest containing two [ebony ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ingot "Skyrim:Ebony Ingot") and four [gold ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"). There is a fifth gold ingot in front of the chest, which will drop almost fully into the ground making it impossible to obtain unless you pick it up before taking any of the ingots in the open chest (this will happen every time you come here, and once fallen, it will stay that way). Ascend the stairs in front of the open chest to an unlocked chest, also against the east wall. In the southeast corner around a lit brazier is some cheap crockery, a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile").

To the right, against the south wall is a sideboard containing two [refined moonstone ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Moonstone "Skyrim:Refined Moonstone"), three further gold ingots, a random enchanted helmet, a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Soul Gem"), a [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") of [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), and an unlocked strong box. In the center of the south wall is an unlocked boss chest. To the right of the boss chest, leaning against the south wall, is a [staff of banishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Banishing "Skyrim:Staff of Banishing"). Farther to the right is another sideboard containing a second unlocked strong box, a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")*, two bowls of glow dust, three gold ingots, two random soul gems, an ebony ingot, an [elixir of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Strength "Skyrim:Elixir of Strength"), and another random enchanted helmet.

In the southwest corner around another lit brazier is more crockery, a bowl of bone meal, and a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"). Against the west wall is another unlocked chest, and farther to the right down the stairs is another large urn and an open chest containing random boots. There is a final large urn against the right-hand stone pillar as you enter, opposite the second urn.

## Notes

- The shrine is useful when you want to start smithing [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric") armor and weapons, as after killing the four respawning Dremora, you can loot their [hearts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart"); you can also obtain their [fire-enchanted weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage").
- The shrine is not present during the events of [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online"): *[Greymoor](/wiki/Online:Greymoor "Online:Greymoor")*. However, tattered tapestries belonging to the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn") indicate they constructed the shrine sometime between [2E 582](/wiki/Lore:Second_Era#2E_582 "Lore:Second Era") and the [Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion_Crisis "Lore:Oblivion Crisis").
- Anything you drop in the shrine will stay there when the area resets.

## Bugs

- The Dremora may not respawn at the shrine, even after waiting 30 in-game days. However, leveled loot will continue to respawn inside.
  - Wait another 30 game days, and they might respawn, both inside and outside.
- One or more Dremora may spawn without a weapon, and if they aren't a mage, they will resort to attacking with their fists.

# Skyrim:Shrine of Talos

## Overview

This article is about the place in Markarth. For all other shrines, see [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines").

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Shrine: Shrine of Talos ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+of+Talos+%28building%29)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MarkarthShrineofTalos | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | |

Shrine of Talos in Markarth

The **Shrine of Talos** is a small shrine in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") dedicated to the worship of the god [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim").

Inside the Shrine of Talos

It is a small, one-room location that is usually empty. The statue of the forsaken deity is the well-lit center-piece of the otherwise gloomy interior. A [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") can be found directly in front of the statue; activating it gives you the [Blessing of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Talos "Skyrim:Blessing of Talos").

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").

## Notes

- It is unknown why THIS Shrine of Talos exists when Markarth is under Imperial control.

## Bugs

- A basket in the shrine may clip with the stone platform it is placed on.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Shrine to Peryite

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Shrine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Shrine.png) | Daedric Shrine: Shrine to Peryite ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shrine+to+Peryite)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 12 |
| Occupants | |
| [Kesh the Clean](/wiki/Skyrim:Kesh_the_Clean "Skyrim:Kesh the Clean") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DA13PeryiteShrine | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") West of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Shrine to Peryite

The **Shrine to Peryite** is the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite").

## Related Quests

- **[The Only Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure")**: Slay an apostate [worshipper](/wiki/Skyrim:Orchendor "Skyrim:Orchendor") for the Daedra Lord [Peryite](/wiki/Lore:Peryite "Lore:Peryite").

## Walkthrough

The shrine is northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), west of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"). Anyone traveling to the shrine from Markarth would be advised to take the path to the north of [Salvius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Salvius_Farm "Skyrim:Salvius Farm"), then take the right fork near [Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald"), as there is no direct route from Karthwasten to the shrine. A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") is down the hill to the west, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is near the ancient totem to the southeast, just below and east of the nearby [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper "Skyrim:Juniper") tree at the base of the small outcropping. Farther east toward Karthwasten, near the edge of the hill above, is another iron ore vein.

The shrine is relatively humble. There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") next to a large rock, with a long wooden table to the right, and a campfire to the right of the table. A [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") is hanging over the fire, as is an unused cooking pot that contains an [alchemy ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). On the table are a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")*, a [scroll of Heal Other](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Heal_Other "Skyrim:Scroll of Heal Other"), and a metal pot containing a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), an [abecean longfin](/wiki/Skyrim:Abecean_Longfin "Skyrim:Abecean Longfin"), a [silverside perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Silverside Perch"), and a filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). There is also an odd-looking golden cauldron in front of a withered tree to the south; the tree is wrapped in sickly green roots, with three clusters of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus along with several human and animal skulls around the trunk. The cauldron is used in the ceremony to contact Peryite during the related quest.

Whereas most Daedric Princes have a statue, the shrine to Peryite is the tree, which is flanked by three large upright stones. The only worshipper of Peryite at the shrine is a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") named [Kesh the Clean](/wiki/Skyrim:Kesh_the_Clean "Skyrim:Kesh the Clean"). Kesh owns all of the items on the table, and will be displeased if he sees you taking any of the items even after you complete the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Only_Cure "Skyrim:The Only Cure") for his master. Kesh spends all of his time either cooking or working at the alchemy lab. He doesn't seem to sleep, sit, or even eat, as there is no furniture, bedding, or [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") in the area.

The shrine is positioned on the top of a cliff above Karthwasten. At the base of the cliff itself, beneath a withered tree to the southeast, lies a natural recess with an interesting [easter egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Easter_Eggs#William_Shakespeare "Skyrim:Easter Eggs") and some good loot. This is an unmarked location. Two random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a random enchanted [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), and two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") lie at the base of an ancient stone totem. The top of the totem has two carved human faces facing east and west, and two dragons with straightened tails facing north and south. Shackles hang from the tail of the northern dragon. Given its proximity to the shrine and the fact that Peryite's symbol is a dragon, it can be inferred that the ancient totem has something to do with the Daedric Prince. A [Wood Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Elf "Skyrim:Wood Elf") corpse and some bloody human body parts lie beneath the totem. There is also an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") on the south side of the totem containing nice leveled loot, which seems to always include a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book *[Incident at Necrom](/wiki/Skyrim:Incident_at_Necrom "Skyrim:Incident at Necrom")*. Farther south, just up the hill and behind the rocks, lies a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") (easily accessible when descending from the shrine). A few paces westward up the hill from the skeleton in a rocky crevice is another unmarked location, comprising a dead sabre cat on a patch of blood-splattered ground surrounded by a leveled weapon, a leveled enchanted [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), four arrows, and a knapsack containing some loot. A juniper tree lies just east of the totem, toward Karthwasten. A wild animal is prowling nearby, just to the north.

## Notes

- Just southwest of the shrine is a Dwarven ruin guarded by a [wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wispmother "Skyrim:Wispmother"). An unlocked Dwarven chest can be found there. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-149762&y=34720&zoom=17&legacy=true)

Skyrim is dotted with **shrines** dedicated to the [Divines](/wiki/Lore:Divines "Lore:Divines") (including [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Tiber_Septim "Lore:Tiber Septim")), which can be activated to receive a [blessing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessings "Skyrim:Blessings") that will cure all [diseases](/wiki/Skyrim:Disease "Skyrim:Disease") and grant a blessing from the specific deity while removing any existing blessing.

Shrines are often accompanied by a large statue, although the shrines themselves are obelisks or sculptures small enough to fit on tabletops.

They are found in the temples within various cities, inside some dungeons, and in [unmarked locations](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Shrines "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") throughout the wilderness. [Daedric Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") are listed separately. There is a shrine to each of the [Aedra](/wiki/Lore:Aedra "Lore:Aedra") in the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") (except a shrine of Talos, which later becomes available if Solitude is taken by [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") forces).

## Shrine of Akatosh

A shrine of Akatosh grants:

[Blessing of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Blessing of Akatosh"): *Magicka regenerates 10% faster.*

- [Regenerate Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Regenerate_Magicka "Skyrim:Regenerate Magicka"), 10 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Akatosh)

### Rorikstead

This shrine is atop the hill directly north of [Frostfruit Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostfruit_Inn "Skyrim:Frostfruit Inn") in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

**Offerings**:

- [Blue Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing")
- [Dragon Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Scales "Skyrim:Dragon Scales")
- *[Kolb & the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolb_%26_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Kolb & the Dragon")*

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-84223&y=15343)

### Twilight Valley

This shrine is placed inside of a tower atop a hill northeast of [Twilight Sepulcher](/wiki/Skyrim:Twilight_Sepulcher "Skyrim:Twilight Sepulcher") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") Hold.

**Offerings**:

- *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*
- *[Olaf and the Dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_and_the_Dragon "Skyrim:Olaf and the Dragon")*
- [Potion of Enhanced Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina")
- Two [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") samples

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-66608&y=-77872)

### Steamcrag Hillock

This shrine is on a hill northeast of the [Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone") and south and slightly east of [Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp"). The shrine is in the middle of some stone pillars, with several bones and entire skeletons scattered across the area. [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") ore veins are nearby.

**Offerings**:

- *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")*
- [Iron War Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe")
- [Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull")
- [Troll Skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=147317&y=-22145)

### Fort Sungard Shrine

This shrine is within the [Fort Sungard Shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard_Shrine "Skyrim:Fort Sungard Shrine") at [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"), southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Only present if the fort is occupied by the Legion. By default, it is a shrine of Kynareth, and is a shrine of Talos if occupied by Stormcloaks.

### Skyborn Altar

This shrine is next to the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") at [Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar") if [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") has not yet been started. A [Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp") defends this location. The shrine shares its altar with a skeleton and [embalming tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Embalming_Tool "Skyrim:Embalming Tool").

**Offerings**:

- [Iron Warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer")
- Two [Petty Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem")
- [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-5666&y=48380)

## Shrine of Arkay

A shrine of Arkay grants:

[Blessing of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Blessing of Arkay"): *Increases your health by 25 points.*

- [Fortify Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Health "Skyrim:Fortify Health"), 25 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Arkay)

### Wayward Pass

Found at the resting place of an ancient traveler in [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass"), alongside several graves.

**Offerings**:

- [Amulet of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Amulet of Arkay")
- [Iron Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots")
- [Iron Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet")
- Two [Linen Wraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Linen_Wrap "Skyrim:Linen Wrap")
- [Steel Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield")
- [Steel Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword")
- [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=76286&y=63066)

### Windhelm Hills

Found northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), south of [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum"). Disappears if the Empire gains control of Winterhold as the [Winterhold Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Stormcloak Camp") replaces it.

**Offerings**:

- [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- Two [Petty Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem")
- [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")
- [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=145848&y=55973)

### Falkreath Hall of the Dead

_02.jpg)

The [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)") has a total of three Shrines of Arkay, appropriate for Falkreath's focus on the grave. Two are placed in front of the Hall of the Dead, and the final one is inside the Hall. None of the shrines have any offerings.

### Markarth Hall of the Dead

.jpg)

This shrine is in a small rest area inside the catacombs of the [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)"). No offerings are placed next to the shrine.

### Riften Hall of the Dead

_02.jpg)

The [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") Arkay shrine is placed in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)"), beneath the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara"). The shrine itself is placed next to the body preparation area.

**Offerings**:

- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- Two [Blue Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")
- Two [Purple Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")

### Solitude Hall of the Dead

.jpg)

The [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Solitude) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Solitude)") keeps its shrine on its first level on a shelf. An [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") is stored on the shelf beneath the shrine.

### Whiterun Hall of the Dead

_04.jpg)

The [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Whiterun) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Whiterun)") keeps its shrine in a well-decorated room, with both sides leading to the shrine flanked by pews.

**Offerings**:

- Four [Skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull")

### Windhelm Hall of the Dead

[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")'s [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Windhelm) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Windhelm)") keeps a shrine of Arkay in the heart of its crypt. A [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"), and [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") have been placed next to the shrine.

### Druadach Redoubt

[Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") has a shrine to Arkay on a ledge by the ramps, halfway along the northeastern wall. Two lit candles are on either side of the shrine. The shrine can only be activated by clipping out of bounds.

## Shrine of Auriel DG

A shrine of Auriel grants:

[Blessing of Auriel](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Auriel "Skyrim:Blessing of Auriel"): *You are 10% more effective with missile weapons.*

- [Fortify Marksman](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Marksman "Skyrim:Fortify Marksman"), 10 pts for 12 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

### Darkfall Cave

This well-hidden shrine is within [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave"), at [Knight-Paladin Gelebor](/wiki/Skyrim:Knight-Paladin_Gelebor "Skyrim:Knight-Paladin Gelebor")'s camp, and right before traversing to [Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage").

### Inner Sanctum

Found in the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)"), a holy site for the Auriel faithful. It is surrounded by [Frozen Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Falmer "Skyrim:Frozen Falmer").

**Offerings**:

- A [Draught of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health")
- Sixteen [Elven Arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow")
- An [Emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald")
- A [Garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet")
- A [Potion of Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka")
- Two [Red Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")
- Two [Gleamblossoms](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleamblossom "Skyrim:Gleamblossom")
- Three [Yellow Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Yellow Mountain Flower")
- [Scroll of Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fireball "Skyrim:Scroll of Fireball")

## Shrine of Dibella

A shrine of Dibella grants:

[Blessing of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Blessing of Dibella"): *+10 Speechcraft.*

- [Fortify Persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Persuasion "Skyrim:Fortify Persuasion"), 10 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Dibella)

### Bridge at Old Hroldan

This shrine is found in the wilderness south of [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn"), across the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), and directly adjacent to the bridge. This large shrine may have a [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") resting at it.

**Offerings**:

- [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- An [Iron Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger")
- A sample of [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")
- Two [Red Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")
- A [Silver Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-114063&y=-15486)

### Temple of Dibella

The [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") keeps a shrine inside the public portion of the Temple. Although the entire Temple is dedicated to Dibella and filled with possible offerings, there are no offerings placed near the actual shrine itself.

### Broken Tower Redoubt

This shrine is found in the top section of the interior of [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt"). The Forsworn have covered the shrine in bones and blood. It is unclear if this was intended as an act of desecration or worship.

**Offerings**:

- [Bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl")
- [Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet")
- [Jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug")

### Morvunskar

This shrine of Dibella can be found in the tower of [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar"), in a room next to [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked") that is also being used for sleeping. Two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a leveled potion have been placed near the shrine, although it is not clear if any of the occupants of Morvunskar are dedicated worshippers.

### Watching Dawnstar

This shrine of Dibella is found south of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), on a stone platform with a statue depicting the Goddess constructed on top of a cliff east of the road.

**Offerings**:

- A [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")
- *[Incident at Necrom](/wiki/Skyrim:Incident_at_Necrom "Skyrim:Incident at Necrom")*
- Four [Purple Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")
- Two [Red Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=30062&y=85774)

### Lucky Lorenz's Shack

This shrine is within the wreckage of [Lucky Lorenz's](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucky_Lorenz "Skyrim:Lucky Lorenz") shack, across the river from the [Abandoned Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison"). Specifically, it is in the far corner from where the shack was destroyed by a falling tree. It is unclear if any of the remaining objects in the house were intended as an offering.

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=91862&y=-15387)

### Haelga's Bunkhouse

Found in the master bedroom of [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse"), Riften. [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga") considers herself to be a fervent worshipper of Dibella, and practices the Dibellan Arts. Numerous items in her room are related to her method of worshipping Dibella, including copies of *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v1 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1")* and *[v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v2 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2")*, a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), [Falmer Blood Elixir](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Blood_Elixir "Skyrim:Falmer Blood Elixir"), [honey](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey "Skyrim:Honey"), [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower"), a [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"), two [potions of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), and a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor").

## Shrine of Julianos

A shrine of Julianos grants:

[Blessing of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Blessing of Julianos"): *Increases your Magicka by 25 points.*

- [Fortify Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka"), 25 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Julianos)

### Fellglow Keep

The [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") shrine of Julianos is a little southwest of the Fellglow Keep Ritual Chamber, on a dresser with candles. There are no offerings placed next to the shrine.

### Julianos's Fallen

This shrine is north of [Shearpoint](/wiki/Skyrim:Shearpoint "Skyrim:Shearpoint"), after going down some cliffs. It is also southeast of [Tumble Arch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumble_Arch_Pass "Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass"). The shrine has been left on the ground, next to a skeleton that appears to have been transporting it to a different location. As the shrine was seemingly lost in transit, there are no offerings at this location.

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=70163&y=26768)

### Harmugstahl

This shrine is in [Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl"), in Kornalus' room. It has been placed on a dresser with a lantern.

### Fort Amol

This shrine is found in the courtyard of [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"). It will disappear along with the elemental mage occupants should the fort be taken over by either side in the Civil War.

**Offerings**:

- [Amulet of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Amulet of Julianos")
- A [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") sample

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=100885&y=-24055)

## Shrine of Kynareth

A shrine of Kynareth grants:

[Blessing of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Blessing of Kynareth"): *Increases your stamina by 25 points.*

- [Fortify Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Stamina "Skyrim:Fortify Stamina"), 25 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Kynareth)

### Temple of Kynareth

The [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") in the city of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") unsurprisingly also has a shrine dedicated to the Goddess. The shrine has been placed on a simple table, with most of the interior of the temple being dedicated to emergency medical services due to the war.

### Fort Sungard

You can find a shrine in the [Fort Sungard Shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard_Shrine "Skyrim:Fort Sungard Shrine") area, which is in the middle of the southern portion of the fort. The shrine will originally be dedicated to Kynareth while the Forsworn occupy the fort. This shrine will be changed to one dedicated to Akatosh if the Imperials control it, and Talos if the Stormcloaks do.

### Hjaalmarch Hills

Southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), east of the river, between the city and [Crabber's Shanty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crabber%27s_Shanty "Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty"). It is just a few steps northeast of [Brood Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Brood_Cavern "Skyrim:Brood Cavern"). Notably, this is the only shrine of Kynareth that is actually located outside in Skyrim.

**Offerings**:

- Two different pairs of [Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots")
- [Draught of Waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Draught of Waterbreathing")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender")
- A [Silver Ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring")
- [Tundra Cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-49953&y=48824)

### Wreck Of The Brinehammer

This shrine is found inside the [Wreck Of The Brinehammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_Of_The_Brinehammer "Skyrim:Wreck Of The Brinehammer"), midway between the cities Dawnstar and Solitude. The shrine is lying on the floor near bookshelves. It is unclear if any of the nearby objects were intended as offerings to the shrine, due to the wreckage.

### Crystaldrift Cave

This shrine is found in [Crystaldrift Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Crystaldrift_Cave "Skyrim:Crystaldrift Cave"), in the northwest corner of the main chamber. [Wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") populate the cave, and will attack intruders trying to visit the shrine if they are seen.

**Offerings**:

- [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine")
- *[Gadnor's Last Wishes](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadnor%27s_Last_Wishes "Skyrim:Gadnor's Last Wishes")*
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- Leveled Potion

### Wilderness Shrine

On [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"), on a hill north of the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone"). It is on the other side of the cliff behind [Severin Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Severin_Manor "Skyrim:Severin Manor"). An [albino spider pod](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Albino Spider Pod") can be found near the shrine, and [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam") grow next to it.

**Offerings**:

- [Amulet of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Amulet of Kynareth")
- [Flin](/wiki/Skyrim:Flin "Skyrim:Flin")
- Two [Trama Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=23823&y=39381)

## Shrine of Mara

A shrine of Mara grants:

[Blessing of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Mara "Skyrim:Blessing of Mara"): *Healing spells restore 10% more.* [[1]](#intnote_FortifyRestoration)

- [Fortify Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), 10 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Mara)

### Nightcaller Temple

A shrine can be found in [Nightcaller Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightcaller_Temple "Skyrim:Nightcaller Temple"), on a table along the wall to the left as you enter. A copy of *[Trials of St. Alessia](/wiki/Skyrim:Trials_of_St._Alessia "Skyrim:Trials of St. Alessia")* is on same table as the shrine.

### Temple of Mara

The [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") keeps a shrine of Mara in the central altar of the temple, near a statue of the Goddess. This is also the location where [marriages](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") are performed. The priests directly collect donations, so no offerings have been left at the shrine itself.

### Karan and Talvur's Campsite

This shrine can eventually be found northwest of [Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Old Hroldan") and south of [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole"). It is originally a site of a tragedy, the death of [Karan](/wiki/Skyrim:Karan "Skyrim:Karan") and [Talvur](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvur "Skyrim:Talvur") as they were eloping. Some time after discovering the site, it will be replaced with a shrine.

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-117833&y=434)

### Border Corner Shrine

This shrine is placed to mark the rough tri-border between [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), and [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). It is at the foot of the mountain range containing the [Skyborn Altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyborn_Altar "Skyrim:Skyborn Altar") dragon lair, and to the south and slightly to the east of the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"). [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") is physically the closest other landmark to it, and can be found northwest from that ruin. The shrine itself is a large and raised stone platform. [Snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") are present at the shrine.

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=2172&y=34962)

## Shrine of Stendarr

A shrine of Stendarr grants:

[Blessing of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Blessing of Stendarr"): *Block 10% more damage with your shield.*

- [Fortify Blocking](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Blocking "Skyrim:Fortify Blocking"), 10 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Stendarr)

### The Two Pillars

This shrine is near the center of [Whiterun Hold's](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") tundra, south of [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") and northeast of [Broken Fang Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Fang_Cave "Skyrim:Broken Fang Cave"). Close to and within sight of the shrine of Zenithar to the west. This site consists of a slightly raised stone platform, with the shrine in the center of two free-standing pillars and sconces on a stone altar. A strong box sits next to the shrine.

**Offerings**:

- [Flawless Amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Amethyst "Skyrim:Flawless Amethyst")
- [Goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet")
- [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile")
- *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")*

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-44675&y=-5729)

### Fort Greenwall

A shrine of Stendarr can be found in the Captain's Quarter of [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") on a dresser flanked by shelves storing alcohol, mugs, lanterns, and a few books. Besides the lit candles on the dresser, several mugs and lanterns have also been stored on the top of the dresser.

### Stendarr's Beacon

[Stendarr's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Stendarr's Beacon") is an active site of worship held by the [Vigil of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigil_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigil of Stendarr"). The Vigil maintain spartan quarters within the tower, and keep their shrine of Stendarr in a sleeping area. The shrine is placed upon a stone altar with lit candles and sconces flanking it.

### Hall of the Vigilant

This shrine is found inside the [Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant"), appropriate for an organization that venerates this God. The shrine has been place on the center of a long table covered in candles to illuminate it. A *[Letter to Keeper Carcette](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_Keeper_Carcette "Skyrim:Letter to Keeper Carcette")* has been left here. This shrine will disappear after the quest [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)") is started, as the Hall will be destroyed.

**Offerings**:

- Two samples of [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal")
- A [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart")
- Two [Plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") holding the alchemical ingredients
- Leveled Enchanted Mace
- A [Wolf Pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt")

## Shrine of Talos

A shrine of Talos grants:

[Blessing of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Talos "Skyrim:Blessing of Talos"): *Time between shouts is reduced 20%.*

- [Fortify Shouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Shouts "Skyrim:Fortify Shouts"), 0.2 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Talos)

### Windhelm Temple of Talos

The [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") keeps its own shrine of Talos, in front of multiple pews for religious services. The active priests of this temple leave no offerings at the shrine itself.

### Sea of Ghosts

On the island directly west of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") and north of [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"). It is slightly southwest of [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb"). Skeletal remains are present here, along with a satchel. A [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe") and a copy of *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")* is here.

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=89647&y=109961)

### Winterhold Glaciers

In a glacial valley north of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand") and west of [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"). It is also southeast of the [Tower Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Tower_Stone "Skyrim:The Tower Stone"). A stone platform with a statue and shrine dedicated to Talos is here, being consumed by the ice.

**Offerings**:

- [Banded Iron Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Iron Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots")
- [Potion of the Defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Potion of the Defender")
- [Steel Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword")
- *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=80388&y=96837)

### Ilas-Tei's Last Stand

On an island northwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") and just northeast of [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb"). This shrine is on an elevated stone platform also being used for hunting purposes, and recently by the unfortunate [Ilas-Tei](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilas-Tei "Skyrim:Ilas-Tei"). A copy of *[Breathing Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Breathing_Water "Skyrim:Breathing Water")* can be found on a barrel next to cage here, and a [scroll of Calm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Calm "Skyrim:Scroll of Calm") can be found close by.

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=99867&y=128622)

### Watcher of Windhelm

[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), south-southwest of the city, west of [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables") on a high rock outcropping. It can easily be seen from the road to Windhelm, and has a good view of the city itself. A copy of *[The Talos Mistake](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Talos_Mistake "Skyrim:The Talos Mistake")* has been left here by parties unknown.

**Offerings**:

- [Iron Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword")
- random [Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet")
- [Iron Warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- leveled [stamina potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=128799&y=24553)

### Riften

A shrine of Talos can be found in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), behind [Black-Briar Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Manor "Skyrim:Black-Briar Manor"). [Nura Snow-Shod](/wiki/Skyrim:Nura_Snow-Shod "Skyrim:Nura Snow-Shod") tends to the shrine as a priestess. Numerous plants grow around the shrine, including [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). [White cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") can also be found here. This shrine will disappear if Riften is captured by the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").

### Weynon Stones

There is an altar at the [Weynon Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Weynon_Stones "Skyrim:Weynon Stones") with a shrine of Talos with a statue of the God. A broken battleaxe has been left at the shrine.

**Offerings**:

- [Iron Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets")
- Two [Steel Ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=43896&y=47136)

### Whiterun

A shrine of Talos with a priest can be found in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), next to the Gildergreen tree. [Heimskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Heimskr "Skyrim:Heimskr") can be found preaching for fifteen hours of the day.

### Markarth Shrine of Talos

The [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") shrine of Talos still has a shrine to pray at, even though the temple has been closed. Candles are still lit around the statue and shrine at the center altar.

### Fellglow Keep

This shrine is inside [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") among rubble and a broken altar in front of a ruined statue of Talos. Although abandoned by its faithful, this shrine will still work if you pray at it.

### White River Valley

This shrine is east of Whiterun, a short distance southeast of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave"), in a shallow alcove under a rock outcropping. Also see [Elisif's Tribute](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif%27s_Tribute "Skyrim:Elisif's Tribute"). A satchel has been left at the altar, along with embalming tools and a plate.

**Offerings**:

- [Iron Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger")
- [Iron Greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword")
- [Iron Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Petty Soul Gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=52654&y=8111)

### Cradlecrush Pond

You can find this shrine by heading southwest of Windhelm, on a straight line between [Cradlecrush Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock") and [Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond"), at the shores of a small pond, northwest of [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill"). A statue of Talos right next to it is visible from Windhelm's entry bridge.

**Offerings**:

- *[2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6")*
- [Steel Horned Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Horned_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Horned Helmet")
- [Steel Mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace")
- [Steel Plate Gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Plate Gauntlets")
- [Steel Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=98195&y=-1989)

### Froki's Peak

A shrine of Talos can be found southwest of [Froki's Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack"). It can be reached by following a path from Froki's Shack up the mountain. A satchel has been left at the base of a statue also present with the shrine.

**Offerings**:

- *[The Amulet of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Amulet_of_Kings "Skyrim:The Amulet of Kings")*
- [Alto Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Imperial Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet")
- [Imperial Light Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Light Shield")
- [Imperial Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword")
- [Iron Boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots")
- *[King](/wiki/Skyrim:King "Skyrim:King")*

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=92894&y=-106513)

### Ilinalta Foothills

This shrine is northeast of [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch"), east of [Lakeview Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Lakeview_Manor "Skyrim:Lakeview Manor"), and southwest of the [Guardian Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_Stones "Skyrim:The Guardian Stones"). A [Thalmor Justiciar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Justiciar "Skyrim:Thalmor Justiciar") attacked the shrine, and can be found dead among the worshippers he slew. An iron sword is found next to the shrine, but it may have been used in the defense of the worshippers, and was not placed as an offering.

**Offerings**:

- [Bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-2824&y=-68422)

### Fort Sungard

[Fort Sungard Shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard_Shrine "Skyrim:Fort Sungard Shrine") at [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"), southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Only present if the fort is occupied by the Stormcloaks.

## Shrine of Zenithar

A shrine of Zenithar grants:

[Blessing of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Blessing of Zenithar"): *Prices are 10% better.*

- [Fortify Barter](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Barter "Skyrim:Fortify Barter"), 10 pts for 8 hours
- [Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=View+all+on+map&search=Shrine+of+Zenithar)

### Four Skull Lookout

Northeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), a shrine of Zenithar can be found west of [Four Skull Lookout](/wiki/Skyrim:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout") on a rocky promontory overlooking the river valley. It is easily within sight of the western column of Four Skull Lookout.

**Offerings**:

- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe")
- [Roll of Paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?centeron=487)

### Crumbling Bastion

Within ruins in the wilderness between [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") and [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"), immediately east of [Gjukar's Monument](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjukar%27s_Monument "Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument"). Close to and within sight of the shrine of Stendarr to the east. The shrine is sheltered by the stone structure surrounding it, and can be found on a stone altar with candles. A satchel has also been placed on the altar with the shrine. An [Amulet of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Amulet of Zenithar") lies on the ground underneath the broken corner of the altar as if the amulet had been left on the altar as an offering but fell to the ground when the corner of the altar broke off.

**Offerings**:

- *[2920](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")*
- Two [Silver Ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-52807&y=-7972)

### Ring of Boulders

This shrine is west of [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den") set against a large rock. There are other rocks of varying size around the area in a loose circle.

**Offerings**:

- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")
- [Quill](/wiki/Skyrim:Quill "Skyrim:Quill")
- [Roll of Paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-56542&y=1965)

### Fallowstone

A shrine of Zenithar is northeast of [Riften Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Stables "Skyrim:Riften Stables"). Take the road north from the stables then turn east immediately after the guard towers. Look up the hillside for the ruins of an Imperial Fort Tower. A satchel has been left at the altar

**Offerings**:

- [Amulet of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Amulet of Zenithar")
- [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=181239&y=-81960)

### Solstheim Shrine

A shrine of Zenithar can also be found in [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"). It is northeast of [Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag"), reached from [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"). Numerous geodes veins surround the shrine, alongside a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). An East Empire Company Strongbox is also found here.

**Offerings**:

- [Corundum Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore")

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&x=40017&y=58964)

## Furnishing Options HF

With the *[Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire")* add-on installed, you can build each of these shrines in the [cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Cellar "Skyrim:Cellar") of your house. Note that the shrine to Auriel from the *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* add-on is not available as an option.

## Notes

- The description of the Blessing of Mara is misleading; the actual effect is that Restoration spells cost 10% less magicka to cast.
- When [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")'s [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") is active, shrines outside of the player's home will cost gold to remove diseases.
