Shroud Hearth Barrow

**Shroud Hearth Barrow** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains two zones: *[Shroud Hearth Barrow](#Shroud_Hearth_Barrow)* and *[Shroud Hearth Depths](#Shroud_Hearth_Depths)*.

The residents of Ivarstead believe the barrow is haunted. [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm"), the local innkeeper, will provide you with the most information, citing the example of [Wyndelius Gatharian](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian"), an adventurer who tried exploring the barrow a year earlier but never returned.

## Related Quests

- **[Lifting the Shroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Lifting_the_Shroud "Skyrim:Lifting the Shroud")**: Investigate the haunted barrow outside of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").
- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

### Shroud Hearth Barrow

Barrow interior

A typical Nordic stone barrow, the outer ring is lined with coffins holding ancestral remains. The door into the barrow is on the inner wall. The entryway door opens to a winding wooden stairway going down. At the landing is a shelf holding a potion, a petty soul gem, and a small burial urn to loot. The path continues downward, heading southeast with dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") to loot on either side of the passage. A coin purse is tucked into the bottom crypt on the left. The passage ends in an intersection where a ghost may be behind the gate to the right, warning you to leave, and another room is to the left. Go into the room on the left. Once inside, you will notice four levers: two on either side of the door. Activate the levers closest to the door to open the iron gate on the other side of the passage. The lever on the far right activates a [dart](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart "Skyrim:Dart") trap. Before you leave, there is a burial urn stuck in the rubble in the right-hand corner of the room and a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Before the Ages of Man](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Ages_of_Man "Skyrim:Before the Ages of Man")* is on the embalming table.

In the next room, there are doors on either end. One is an apprentice-locked door, and the other an iron portcullis with a pull-chain. Open the locked door first. Directly inside is [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") triggering a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap"). However, the spears are well enough ahead that they do not present an issue if you proceed slowly into the room. Ahead is an unlocked chest rigged with an adept-locked [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") trap. The cable will activate a dart trap if not disarmed before opening the chest. After looting the chest go back out to the portcullis. Pulling the chain will lift the gate and trigger a spear trap. Wait until the spears retract back into the wall and proceed through without incident. At the bottom of the stairs are two more iron doors. The door to the right is tension cable rigged to trigger [flamethrower statues](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") when opened. Wait until the flames extinguish and proceed through. At the other end of this room is a [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps"). In order to operate the door, and continue exploring the barrow, you will need the [Sapphire Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Sapphire Dragon Claw"). This can be obtained by giving [Wilhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Wilhelm "Skyrim:Wilhelm"), the innkeeper in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"), [Wyndelius Gatharian's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Wyndelius's Journal").

In order to find the journal, go back to the last room and open the other door. This leads to adventurer [Wyndelius Gatharian](/wiki/Skyrim:Wyndelius_Gatharian "Skyrim:Wyndelius Gatharian"). The antechamber has a small burial urn on the south wall. The next room is Wyndelius' chambers. He may be sleeping when you arrive. If he is awake he will attack you. In his room, there is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a large table serving as a desk. The journal you need is on the table. Also on the table are a small satchel, the [Philter of the Phantom](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_the_Phantom "Skyrim:Philter of the Phantom"), and two books. Next to the fire are a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), a random potion, and a pair of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on the shelf. Now, backtrack out of the barrow to take the journal to Wilhelm. Initiate a conversation about the barrow and then give him the journal. If you have not initiated the related [Lifting the Shroud](/wiki/Skyrim:Lifting_the_Shroud "Skyrim:Lifting the Shroud") quest, giving Wilhelm the journal will activate and update the quest in your journal.

Once you have the Sapphire Dragon Claw go back to Shroud Hearth Barrow to the puzzle door room. The combination is on the palm of the claw; starting with the outer ring **Moth—Owl—Wolf**. When the door recedes go straight to the end of the hall. Here you will find a broken table beneath a stone etching bearing an empty random soul gem and a random helmet. The passage turns left and descends passing a sideboard with a random mace on top and into a hall containing five sarcophagi: two around the perimeter and three up on a raised dais. On a pedestal in the middle of the dais is the spell tome [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh"). As you move about the room the portcullises on either end will close, trapping you inside. A small illuminated alcove in the eastern corner of the chamber to the right of the dais has a lever which reverses this. Its gate will open automatically as you move about the room. When that happens, [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") will emerge from the coffins and attack. After the draugr are done activate the lever. As you exit a large urn is on the ground to the left just before a winding staircase. Notice the [trap door grate](/wiki/Skyrim:Trap_Door "Skyrim:Trap Door") on the floor with water below at the base of the stairs. Stepping on the grate will cause it to collapse, dumping you into the water. A pull chain directly across the grate locks it into place. At the bottom of the pool are some skeletal remains with a coin purse and a random greatsword. Avoid touching the handle on the nearby wall as it will close the grate above you causing you to drown if you cannot quickly reactivate it.

Barrow interior

The stairs lead to a door on the second level and yet another door on the third. Open the uppermost door first. It is master-locked and inside is an expert-locked chest and a random soul gem is beside it. Go back down a flight to the first door. Just inside is a pressure plate triggering a poison dart trap. At the bottom of the stone stairs is a second pressure plate that triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram"). A [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") is waiting just around the corner. The skeleton is positioned correctly so that if you sneak down the stairs, you can use the pressure plate battering ram to smash him. On the left is a sideboard with a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on top.

The next door opens onto the balcony of a large room. To the left is an urn. Next to the urn are two sarcophagi, each with an activating handle next to it. If you are up to it, pulling each handle will expel a draugr and a skeleton, respectively. To the right is a hole in the stone showing a chest in a well lit room. The doorway is actually a sarcophagus around the corner to the right, opened by a handle on the wall beside it.

Standing in oil

Looking through the wooden bulwark, you will spot five skeletons down below, all conveniently standing in an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick"). Use a flame spell or take advantage of the oil lamps hanging above the skeletons to neatly incinerate them. The chest is unlocked, and the room contains a random potion, a random empty soul gem, a random sword, and a small burial urn. When your plundering is complete, head down the platform stairs.

Cross through the pit and up the stairs to the balcony on the other side. More draugr will awaken to impede you. A small burial urn is in the rubble at the top of the stairs. A random mace can be found on a broken table tucked in the northwest corner of the balcony. The next door opens to a stairway with a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") at the base that triggers a [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") trap. At the top of the stairs, a draugr is waiting. The tripwire can be used to kill the draugr, or simply jump over the wire to avoid the hassle of running through the swinging blades. (Revisiting this area will require you to still have the Shroud Hearth Barrow key to open the door at the top of these stairs.) A chain just inside the room at the top of the stairs will stop the blades. More draugr will awaken as you enter the room. A pressure plate triggering a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap is right at the mouth of the passage heading east. More draugr are in this passage as well. The draugr guarding the door will have a Shroud Hearth Barrow key for you to pick up. On the right before the door is a burial urn.

The key will open up the expert-locked door that leads to a room with an underground stream and a stone bridge. Before going farther into the room, jump into the shallow water to your left and activate the chain, which raises the gate. A coin purse and draugr body to loot are underwater against the back wall. Before going up the stairs, take the stone walkway to the bridge. Cross the bridge to the alcove with a filled random soul gem and a pair of random gauntlets. Farther on, a leveled sword is behind the waterfall at the end of the room. Back across the bridge and up the stairs you will find a pressure plate in the middle of the room that seemingly does nothing and four rotating totem pillars. Ignore the pillars for now and enter the doors ahead. A draugr is waiting in the next room along with a second pressure plate. A medium coin purse is on the table to the left along with a burial urn and a pair of random boots. A small urn is on the shelves to the right.

Step on the pressure plate. Revolving doors will open on four alcoves revealing a totem statue. Note which totem is revealed in each alcove from left to right (**Whale—Eagle—Snake—Whale**). This is the combination for the pillars in the outer room. Back in the outer room, activate each totem pillar, again from left to right, in the combination revealed. Once the totems are correctly aligned, step on the pressure plate to lower the wooden bridge across to the next room, as well as to open the portcullis.

Across the bridge

Across the bridge, a throne is to the left and a random potion of healing and a random war axe are on a table to the right. A draugr is also waiting in the passage ahead. A spike wall pressure plate is just inside the doorway, but a little off-center. Sidle your way past it on the right. Just past the gate, to the right, is an alcove with a large urn on one side and a random filled soul gem and random dagger on a shelf on the other. An apprentice-locked door opens to a room with a [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot") on a pedestal. The pedestal is actually a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), and removing the ingot will trigger another flamethrower trap. If you are quick, stand to the far left of the pedestal, grab the ingot, and quickly move backwards behind the corner to avoid the flames. Alternatively, shoot the ingot off of the pedestal and wait for the flames to stop.

Back in the main passage, a tripwire triggering [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") is across your path. Jump over it, or trigger it, backing up quickly to avoid the damage. In either case, you may be able to kill or injure another wandering draugr (just up ahead) with the trap. At the top of the incline a small burial urn is to the right, and a random potion of magicka and random bow are on the table. The next set of doors leads to Shroud Hearth Depths.

### Shroud Hearth Depths

Coffin room

Ahead of you is a great hall. However, before you descend the stairs to enter, look to your left for a random potion of healing, then proceed. The great hall you enter has a large stone temple in the center and thirteen sarcophagi arranged around it—a bad omen. Stepping into the room causes the gate behind you to close and the enemies to start emerging. There are six skeletons and seven draugr, one of which is boss level. An advantage here is that the enemies do not all emerge at once; they will rise to replace the fallen. Once all have been defeated, both the way back and the way forward will be opened. Take some time to loot the corpses before heading up the wooden plank to a very narrow tunnel.

The tunnel opens to another large room with a boss chest, front and center. The chest has a novice-locked tension cable trap that triggers a dart trap from the ceiling. A large coin purse, a random weapon, and a piece of random armor are also lying by the chest. A random potion of healing is lying in the rocks on the left-hand wall, and more random armor (a chestpiece) and weaponry, as well as a small burial urn with a large coin purse tucked behind is on the table to the right.

Make your way past the chest to hear the telling chanting of a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). The wall holding a part of the [Kyne's Peace](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Peace "Skyrim:Kyne's Peace") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") is directly ahead.

Treasure awaits

After collecting the shout, there is an adept-locked chest in the water. The most direct route to it is to stand on the edge of the wooden platform leading to the word wall (just to the northwest of the bridge), and face northwest. Jump down into the water and turn around to face southeast. In a small alcove, just under a large support beam for the platform, is the submerged chest. To the left of the word wall is a broken bridge. Using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout you can reach the small alcove on the other side to find a random filled soul gem and a quality greatsword, with a large coin purse nestled in between.

The exit is across the intact stone bridge to the right. This leads back to the barrow and into a small, circular room with a pull chain. The chain opens a hidden door leading into a partially collapsed tunnel. The tunnel ends in another pull chain and secret door. There is also a random warhammer in your path as you approach the end of the tunnel as well as a small urn by the secret door. This secret door opens into Wyndelius Gatharian's chambers. Backtrack to the entrance of the barrow.

## Notes

- If you lack Whirlwind Sprint, in third person you can hug the wall between each pillar and jump your way to the alcove in the room with the word wall, or you can try using shouts, spells or arrows to knock these items from the bridge, though either method is difficult.
- If you're stuck in Shroud Hearth Depths coffin room, look for any foe in the area. Sometimes a skeleton flees into the water, it must be killed to progress. The last draugr will not emerge if any previously killed are currently raised to fight for you. Just kill the raised undead to progress.
- A [clay deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Clay "Skyrim:Clay")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") can be found along the shore east of the barrow.
- Shroud Hearth Barrow also [appears](/wiki/Online:Shroud_Hearth_Barrow_(place) "Online:Shroud Hearth Barrow (place)") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- If the dragon claw door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- The word wall may not glow, rendering you unable to learn part of the Kyne's Peace shout.
- The pressure plate for the puzzle may not work at all, regardless of the presence of an object. Reloading to a previous save and attempting again seemed to fix this. **?**
- Sometimes the pressure plate for the puzzle does not work if there is something on or very close to the plate. Moving the item/body away fixes this issue.[*verification needed — Needs testing to determine cause*]
- Once the oil pool is set on fire, the skeletons and their bones will be seen floating above the firepit due to a primitive collision box error.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
- In the room with the Oakflesh spell tome, there are two triggers that will close the gates in the room—one on the raised platform and one on the lower portion. If you trigger one, open the gates, then trigger the other, the escape lever will be blocked off and you will have no way out of the room.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- If you are trapped in the room, try the following: Open the console, click on a gate with mouse, then type  `disable` . This will disable the chosen gate, allowing you to exit.
- Triggering the pressure plate in the room with the puzzle solution using an arrow fired from a Bound Bow will cause the windows to cycle indefinitely. **?**
- Sometimes the draugr holding the Shroud Hearth Barrow key is behind the locked door, making getting to the key to unlock the door impossible. **?**
- If you summon a flame atronach to fight Wyndelius Gatharian, the journal you need to complete your quest may be destroyed before you can collect it. The remedy is to reload an earlier save and fight him using a less destructive method. **?**

# Skyrim:Shrouded Grove

## Overview

Shrouded Grove

**Shrouded Grove** is a grove with a small cave located in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale").

It is located due south of [Silverdrift Lair](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverdrift_Lair "Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair") and west of [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), and is inhabited by leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") and [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan").

### Shrouded Grove

The grove's only identifying features are a large stone statue head and a few stone columns. There is a leveled [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") camouflaged against a tree trunk to the left of the cave's entrance as well as a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") in the grove nearby. There is also a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") in the vicinity that may attack the animal.

### Shrouded Grove Cave

Interior of Shrouded Grove

The entrance leads into a short, ice-covered tunnel that leads into the cave itself. Upon entering, you will see two animals attacking each other; the winner will generally be quite injured by the encounter, making it an easy target. Camouflaged against a tree trunk to the left is another leveled [spriggan](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan"). Once the enemies are dealt with, you are free to explore the rest of the cave. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") against the east wall, by the back of the cave; to either side of it lie two dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers"), and an open sarcophagus lies behind it on the left. The sarcophagus contains a third draugr and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Ice and Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_and_Chitin "Skyrim:Ice and Chitin")*.

## Bugs

- Shrouded Grove isn't marked as a cave, so cave-based radiant quests won't target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Side Quests

## Overview

**Side quests** are standard-length quests that are not part of a questline and are not [Daedric quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Quests "Skyrim:Daedric Quests"). Completing side quests generally increases the "Side Quests Completed" statistic in your journal and counts toward the [Sideways](#Achievements) [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements").

Side quests are listed separately in your journal. Unlike [miscellaneous quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests"), they are not subcategorized, and are logged in your journal after completion. Side quests can be identified by the side quest knotwork (pictured above left) displayed next to the quest title in your journal and on each quest's page on this wiki.

Quests are sorted below by their usual starting location.

### Markarth

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!
- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

### Morthal

- **[Laid to Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Laid_to_Rest "Skyrim:Laid to Rest")**: Investigate a tragic house fire, and discover an insidious plot against the town.
- **[Rising at Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn")**: Track down [Falion](/wiki/Skyrim:Falion "Skyrim:Falion") to rid yourself of [vampirism](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism").

### Raven Rock ( DB )

- **[A New Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Help [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi") with his debt to [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)").
- **[Black Book: The Winds of Change](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Winds_of_Change_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Winds of Change (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Stop the [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attacks on [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Served Cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Save [Councilor Morvayn](/wiki/Skyrim:Lleril_Morvayn "Skyrim:Lleril Morvayn") from an assassination plot.
- **[The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find out what happened to the [great-grandfather](/wiki/Skyrim:Gratian_Caerellius "Skyrim:Gratian Caerellius") of [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius").

### Riften

- **[Promises to Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Promises_to_Keep "Skyrim:Promises to Keep")**: Help [Louis Letrush](/wiki/Skyrim:Louis_Letrush "Skyrim:Louis Letrush") get [Frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost "Skyrim:Frost") from [Sibbi Black-Briar](/wiki/Skyrim:Sibbi_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Sibbi Black-Briar").
- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

### Solitude

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.
- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.

### Whiterun

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").
- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").

### Windhelm

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

### Riverwood

- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").

### Skaal Village ( DB )

- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
- **[Filial Bonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Filial_Bonds "Skyrim:Filial Bonds")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood")'s brother, [Torkild](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild "Skyrim:Torkild"), who may have become a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear").
- **[Lost Legacy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legacy "Skyrim:Lost Legacy")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Travel to [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb") and defeat [Vahlok the Jailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok_the_Jailor "Skyrim:Vahlok the Jailor").

### Tel Mithryn ( DB )

- **[Azra's Staffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Azra%27s_Staffs "Skyrim:Azra's Staffs")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Retrieve a staff made by [Azra Nightwielder](/wiki/Lore:Azra_Nightwielder "Lore:Azra Nightwielder") for Master [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[Black Book: The Hidden Twilight](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Hidden_Twilight_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Hidden Twilight (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Briarheart Necropsy](/wiki/Skyrim:Briarheart_Necropsy "Skyrim:Briarheart Necropsy")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Examine a [Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[Experimental Subject (A)](/wiki/Skyrim:Experimental_Subject_(A) "Skyrim:Experimental Subject (A)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Help [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") by being a test subject in his experiment.
- **[From the Ashes](/wiki/Skyrim:From_the_Ashes "Skyrim:From the Ashes")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Help [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") by killing an [ash guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian").
- **[Healing a House](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_a_House "Skyrim:Healing a House")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Help [Elynea Mothren](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") repair the tower of [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").
- **[Heart Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stones "Skyrim:Heart Stones")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find a [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[Lost Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knowledge "Skyrim:Lost Knowledge")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Retrieve the [Black Books](/wiki/Lore:Black_Book "Lore:Black Book") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").
- **[Old Friends](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Friends "Skyrim:Old Friends")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find the source of attacks on [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)").
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Telvanni Research](/wiki/Skyrim:Telvanni_Research "Skyrim:Telvanni Research")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Extract a sample from an [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth")'s research.
- **[Wind and Sand](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_and_Sand_(quest) "Skyrim:Wind and Sand (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Retrieve a copy of *[Wind and Sand](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_and_Sand_(book) "Skyrim:Wind and Sand (book)")* for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth").

### Thirsk Mead Hall ( DB )

- **[Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Help [Bujold the Unworthy](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold_the_Unworthy "Skyrim:Bujold the Unworthy") retake [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").
- **[The Chief of Thirsk Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chief_of_Thirsk_Hall "Skyrim:The Chief of Thirsk Hall")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Help out a [Riekling Chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Chief "Skyrim:Riekling Chief") at [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").

### Other

- **[Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial")**: Convince an unwilling [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vantus_Loreius "Skyrim:Vantus Loreius") to help fix a stranded [jester's](/wiki/Skyrim:Cicero "Skyrim:Cicero") broken wagon wheel.
  - This quest is categorized as a Dark Brotherhood quest for most purposes; see details in the [achievements](#Achievements) section below.
- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

## Dungeons

These quests generally start when you approach or explore the associated dungeons and progress to completion within each dungeon. Only dungeon quests that are counted as side quests are listed here. The [Dungeon Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Quests "Skyrim:Dungeon Quests") page provides a list of all dungeon quests, including both the below side quests and several additional miscellaneous quests.

- **[A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska")**: Help [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") trace her roots in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins").
- **[Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship")**: Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his [aunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his [ancestral barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").
- **[Evil in Waiting](/wiki/Skyrim:Evil_in_Waiting "Skyrim:Evil in Waiting")**: Seal away an [ancient evil](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)").
- **[Infiltration](/wiki/Skyrim:Infiltration "Skyrim:Infiltration")**: Help [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") take back [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch").
- **[Repentance](/wiki/Skyrim:Repentance "Skyrim:Repentance")**: Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") prevent her mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") from transforming into a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").
- **[Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult")**: Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir").
- **[Silenced Tongues](/wiki/Skyrim:Silenced_Tongues "Skyrim:Silenced Tongues")**: Unlock the burial chamber of the Tongue Chieftain [Kvenel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kvenel_the_Tongue "Skyrim:Kvenel the Tongue").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
  - This quest is also listed as a Markarth [city quest](#Cities) as the associated dungeon is within Markarth.
- **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt").

## Other

- **[A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots")**: Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.
- **[Black Book: Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Black Book: The Sallow Regent](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_The_Sallow_Regent_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: The Sallow Regent (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Black Book: Untold Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Learn the [Black Book](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Untold_Legends_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Untold Legends (book)")'s hidden knowledge.
- **[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Find the treasure of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand").
- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
  - This quest is unique among side quests in that there are [multiple places](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend#A_Key_to_the_Past "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") from which it can be "normally started".
- **[Impatience of a Saint](/wiki/Skyrim:Impatience_of_a_Saint "Skyrim:Impatience of a Saint")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Collect the ten missing pages of [Saint Jiub](/wiki/Skyrim:Jiub "Skyrim:Jiub")'s Opus.
- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").
- **[The Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:The Ebony Warrior")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Locate and defeat the [Ebony Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Warrior "Skyrim:Ebony Warrior").
- **[Unearthed](/wiki/Skyrim:Unearthed "Skyrim:Unearthed")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Assist [Ralis Sedarys](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralis_Sedarys "Skyrim:Ralis Sedarys") in his search for the relics of [Ahzidal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal_(creature) "Skyrim:Ahzidal (creature)") in [Kolbjorn Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Kolbjorn_Barrow "Skyrim:Kolbjorn Barrow").

## Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is obtained by completing side quests:

-  **Sideways** (20 points/Bronze) — Complete 10 side quests
  - Completing any 10 qualifying side quests will unlock this achievement. Any quest that uses the side quest knotwork in your journal generally counts toward the achievement, but there are a few unusual cases:
    - The Black Book side quests, [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice"), and [Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages") do not count toward the achievement, but are listed on this page and are treated as side quests in your journal.
    - [The Affairs of Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Affairs_of_Hagravens "Skyrim:The Affairs of Hagravens") counts toward the achievement, but is not listed on this page and is treated as a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") in your journal.
    - [Delayed Burial](/wiki/Skyrim:Delayed_Burial "Skyrim:Delayed Burial") is listed on this page and counts toward the achievement, but is otherwise categorized as a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest and is marked in your journal with the Dark Brotherhood knotwork.
    - [Alteration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell") is not listed on this page and does not count toward the achievement, but is mistakenly marked in your journal with the side quest knotwork instead of the correct [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") knotwork.
  - In most cases where a quest has two possible conclusions, either ending will qualify toward the achievement. Exceptions include [A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska") and [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella"). See the individual quest pages for details.
  - You can track your progress toward the achievement using the "Side Quests Completed" statistic on the "Quest" page of your journal's "General Stats".

# Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir") |
| Location(s): | [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") |
| Reward: | [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(item) "Skyrim:Rahgot (item)"), [Dragon Priest Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Staff_(Rahgot) "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Staff (Rahgot)"), Word for the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") shout |
| ID: | dunForelhostQST |
| Suggested Level: | 24 |

Siege on the Dragon Cult

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir") to begin the quest.
2. Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost").
3. (Optional) Find the [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skorm_Snow-Strider%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skorm Snow-Strider's Journal") of Skorm Snow-Strider.
4. Make your way through the first zone into the Crypt.
5. Either pick the lock on the well or find the key, then move on to the Refectory.
6. Travel through the Refectory, find the glass claw and locate the [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Traps").
7. Use the claw to enter and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)").
8. Return to Valmir with the mask.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Valmir's camp sits in the ruins of Forelhost

When you enter the courtyard of Forelhost for the first time, [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir") will call to you. When the two of you get close enough, he'll initiate a conversation. He will claim he has been sent there by military forces in an attempt to recover a powerful artifact for the war effort. He asks for your help, since he cannot do it alone. According to him, this was the last stronghold of the Dragon Cult back in the First Era, and the commander's mask was allegedly an extremely powerful artifact. He requests that you enter the ruin and retrieve the item. He also mentions that the military general who stormed the fortress to wipe out the cult supposedly left his journal here, so finding it might provide some more information.

### Forelhost Stronghold

Shortly after entering the zone, you'll begin encountering ghosts of the cultists. They must be defeated or avoided to proceed. Work your way around to get behind the portcullis that is down, and you'll be able to enter the crypts. *[Skorm Snow-Strider's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Skorm_Snow-Strider%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Skorm Snow-Strider's Journal")* is found along this path. It recounts that when they took the fortress, the defenders had collapsed the entry and all killed themselves, leaving the ghosts to haunt the place. The well was locked and poisoned, and with the losses suffered from the poisoned water, Skorm decided not to search for the key in the crypts, simply choosing to leave the survivors sealed within.

### Forelhost Crypt

Once in the crypt, make your way to the well. If you can pick the lock, do so, and move on down; otherwise turn right instead and head through the crypt tunnels to the far end, where you'll find the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost_Well_Key "Skyrim:Forelhost Well Key"). Then head back to the well. After going down the well, follow the tunnels on to the Refectory. You will find a potion on top of a [stand](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate") with [dart](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") holes behind it - you can drop a wooden plate or something similar on the ground, pick up the potion, and use the plate/object to stop the darts.

### Forelhost Refectory

Once in the Refectory, move through and find the [glass dragon claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Claw "Skyrim:Glass Claw"), which you'll need to open the [puzzle door](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Door "Skyrim:Puzzle Door") later. Continue on to the door. From top (outer ring) to bottom (inner ring), the solution is: **Fox—Owl—Snake**.

You'll need to defeat the dragon priest [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") and four leveled draugr. Afterwards, loot Rahgot's body. He'll have the [mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(item) "Skyrim:Rahgot (item)"), a [dragon priest staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Staff_(Rahgot) "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Staff (Rahgot)"), and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost_Balcony_Key "Skyrim:Forelhost Balcony Key") to the battlements.

### Battlements

Head out onto the battlements to reach a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"), and learn a word for the [Storm Call](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Call "Skyrim:Storm Call") shout.

After visiting the word wall move near the inside of the battlements; you'll see Captain Valmir talking to an enemy soldier. The objective to return to Valmir remains, so drop down. You'll find that Valmir has now dressed in the armor of the opposing side, to convince this other soldier to do the same job he sent you to do! He's an impostor! Defeat both Valmir and the enemy soldier to conclude the quest. If you wish, loot *[Valmir's Orders](/wiki/Skyrim:Valmir%27s_Orders "Skyrim:Valmir's Orders")* to discover that he was actually an agent (strongly implied, but not explicitly stated, to be [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor")) who was sent to retrieve the mask and return to [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") with it (presumably to use the mask on the matching pedestal in [Bromjunaar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Bromjunaar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary")).

## Notes

- It is possible to ignore Valmir at the beginning of the quest (by ending conversation before agreeing to take the quest) and pickpocket the key to the ruins from him. You'll get an entry in your journal about his quest only when you reach the battlements and overhear his conversation with the second NPC.
- It is also possible to kill Valmir immediately after arriving at this location but before going into the ruins. You can then loot his body for the scrap of paper revealing his treachery.
- Version 1.3.3 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") delays the conversation between Valmir and the soldier until you're on the ground in the same area with them.

## Bugs

- If the puzzle door does not work, check [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Puzzle_Totems#Bugs "Skyrim:Puzzle Totems") for possible fixes.
- Captain Valmir may attack you on sight.
- If you pickpocket the key and proceed to get the mask, after stepping outside, the quest will initiate with the objective to kill Captain Valmir. The soldier attacks but Valmir does not; you will gain a bounty for killing him but the quest does not complete.
- If the claw is knocked off the pedestal before you pick it up, the metal gate may not lower.
  - Dragging an item back onto the pedestal and removing it again will trigger the gate.
- If you find the Refectory Library gate is raised you cannot proceed.
  - Leave the area and then return, the gates should be open.
- Multiple masks may be found on Rahgot's body.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Just before you enter the ruin, Valmir will mistakenly refer to finding a staff instead of the mask.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=14181))
- If you Switch sides during the civil War Valmir will wear the first selected faction uniform. And may not be able to talk to the player. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Siege on the Dragon Cult (dunForelhostQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I have been asked to defeat the Dragon Priest in Forelhost and to bring back his Mask. A journal left by Skorm Snow-Strider may reveal a way past the collapsed areas. *Objective 10:* (Optional) Find Skorm Snow-Strider's journal  *Objective 50:* Obtain Rahgot's mask |
| 20 |  | I have been asked to defeat the Dragon Priest in Forelhost and to bring back his Mask. I have found the journal of Skorm Snow-Strider, which may reveal how to bypass the collapsed areas. |
| 26 |  | *Objective 30:* (Optional) Find the key to the well in the Catacombs *(if Valmir not killed)* |
| 40 |  | I have been asked to defeat the Dragon Priest in Forelhost and to bring back his Mask. I can reach the blocked off areas of the stronghold through the well. |
| 50 |  | I have been asked to defeat the Dragon Priest in Forelhost and to bring back his Mask. |
| 60 |  | I have defeated the Dragon Priest, Rahgot, and taken his Mask. I should return with it to Valmir. *Objective 60:* Return to Valmir *(if Valmir not killed)* |
| 70 |  | Valmir has betrayed me and has been tricking soldiers into the ruins. He must die. *Objective 70:* Kill the imposter Valmir |
| 100 | ☑ |  |
| 110 | ☑ |  |
| *Unknown* |  | *Objective 20:* (Optional) Show Skorm Snow-Strider's journal to Valmir |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 3, 5, 15, 25, 30, 64, 65, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunForelhostQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunForelhostQST`.

# Skyrim:Sightless Pit

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Sightless Pit ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sightless+Pit)) | | |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [Skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), [Dwarven Automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"), [The Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Messenger "Skyrim:The Messenger")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") | |

Sightless Pit

**Sightless Pit** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains three zones: *[Sightless Pit](#Sightless_Pit)*, *[Temple of Xrib](#Temple_of_Xrib)*, and *[Abandoned Cave](#Abandoned_Cave)*. A fourth zone, *[Sightless Vault](#Sightless_Vault)*, is added by the [Sunder & Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").

Unlike most caves, you must drop down into this cave, making it impossible to leave the way you came in and forcing you to traverse the entire cave to return to the surface. There are many vertical elements in the cave, and the creatures are all leveled.

## Related Quests

- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.

### Exterior

The entrance is west of the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura"), and is marked by a single Falmer tent.

### Sightless Pit

Upon dropping into the hole in the ground, you will find yourself at the edge of a large pool of water surrounded by icy walls, with a tunnel leading to the north. A search of the deep pool of water reveals nothing of interest. Following the tunnel, it passes a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the right-hand wall, then turns to the east. A short way farther, it turns back to the north and opens into a cavern with a small camp. The camp consists of a campfire with three unowned bedrolls around it and three food barrels to the west, beside a flat-topped rock with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Aevar Stone-Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Aevar_Stone-Singer "Skyrim:Aevar Stone-Singer")*, and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") on top. On one of the barrels is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). The cavern continues to the north, where a ledge descends around the walls of the cavern. Immediately below the camp on a ledge is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") pierced by numerous [Falmer arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Arrow "Skyrim:Falmer Arrow"). If you drop down to this ledge, be sure not to land behind the chest, as you may get stuck and have to reload a previous save. The path descends to a level below this ledge, where another two bandits' corpses can be found, presumably of the people who set up the camp. There are a few glowing mushrooms found throughout the cave.

The path continues heading west and turns to the south after a short way. Take care along here, as there is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in the middle of the floor, on a darker patch, where it is harder to see. This triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that comes out of the ground in front. A few paces farther on, a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") is on the left-hand wall, with a leveled Falmer lurking inside. If the Falmer doesn't emerge (e.g., if you're sneaking), it is one of very few in the whole game that can be "extracted" by firing a ranged weapon into the hive.

The path turns to the west again, and the tunnel changes to Dwemer architecture. At the end of a short tunnel is a long dangerous drop, with a series of ledges you need to use to avoid severe damage or death. The final drop is onto a platform at the top of a curving ramp, where another pressure plate triggers a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to fire from the wall behind you. The ramp curves around the shaft to another ledge, where a second straight ramp leads down to a ledge with a stone pool containing shallow water, with another ramp curving down from this ledge. Below is a leveled Falmer and a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") on a ledge, with a Falmer hive concealing another Falmer on the wall. A final curved ramp leads down to the ground and a corridor heading west with a track for a [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") trap down the middle. This trap has no activation mechanism, so using a shout normally used to evade such a thing will only attract the attention of enemies lurking just ahead.

The corridor descends a short ramp to a crossroads, with two Falmer, one of which is leveled, standing in a dead end to the left, just out of sight. Using [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") or the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") may make it appear that only a single Falmer is standing there. There is an unlocked Dwarven chest ahead at the crossroads, and a corridor heading to the north from the chest, leading into another ice tunnel that turns to the west after a short distance. Ahead, it opens into a room of Dwemer construction, with a large staircase and a collapsed [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") that cannot be interacted with. Three more enemies guard the top of the stairs, consisting of a magic-using Falmer, frostbite spiders, [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and/or a leveled chaurus, depending on your level. The door at the top of the stairs leads to the second zone, the *Temple of Xrib*.

### Temple of Xrib

Temple of Xrib

The *Temple of Xrib* consists of a mixture of Dwarven ruins and frozen caves. Upon entering, a wide corridor rises to the west, turning north at the top before quickly turning west again. Through a short corridor lies a room guarded by a leveled chaurus, with a leveled Falmer patrolling a cylindrical tunnel in the room's southwestern corner. This tunnel, through which a Falmer tent is visible, leads into a large cavern. There is a hive on the wall to the left containing a Falmer, several more of which are farther into the cavern behind a rock wall to the tent's right and will be alerted by noise from fighting the first. The first tent, reachable by climbing an earthen ramp, has only a campfire inside, and a second empty tent lies to the right, along with a Falmer hive on the wall. Behind the first tent is an open pen with a few piles of [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") and a ledge (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

The path continues to the west, entering a tunnel that then turns to the south before opening into a massive mist-filled cavern, with wide stairs leading up to the south and a high ceiling that glitters like that of [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), which itself is rivaled by the huge Dwarven structure before you. You can spend a lot of time exploring different ledges and corners in this cavern, but there is nothing of interest away from the main path. From the cavern's entrance, you can see the top of a Falmer tent at the top of the first flight of stairs. A magic-using Falmer and a chaurus stand to the right of the tent, which has a fire inside. Behind, there are more levels, with a distant pair of pillars several levels above the entrance. From the top of the first flight of stairs, you can see more stairs off to the west, with two more Falmer patrolling the top. Climbing the second flight of stairs reveals a Falmer tent to the right, containing a fire and an unlocked chest. To the south, an unlocked chest sits in front of a second tent. At the other end of this level, a third Falmer tent contains yet another unlocked chest. Between the second and third tents is a flight of stairs crushed by falling masonry. To the west, a path climbs a curving ramp.

The curving ramp on the path to the west leads to a lit corridor, where a magic-using Falmer and a chaurus are patrolling. There is an unlocked Dwarven chest to the left of the second hanging light, and beyond this, another curving ramp to a tower above, guarded by another leveled Falmer. There is a short ramp down to the east on the other side leading to the level with the two pillars seen from below. There are many more enemies on this level, including a boss-leveled Falmer, chaurus, frostbite spiders, or skeevers, so a Detect Life spell or the Aura Whisper shout is recommended. Killing the creatures before the Falmer may cause a unique spell with a red blast effect to activate on their bodies, which teleports them between the two pillars and revives them. In the middle of this level, at the rear between two pillars lies a smaller pillar with a large unlocked boss chest in front. To the east is another lit tower with a lift to the third zone, the *Abandoned Cave*.

### Abandoned Cave

The *Abandoned Cave* is an unoccupied zone that serves as the exit for the cave. There is a short corridor to the south to a door that is barred from this side, preventing you from accessing the *Temple of Xrib* without first traversing the rest of the cave. The only items of interest in this area are a couple [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and a few glowing mushrooms which can be harvested along the path. Exiting to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") will bring you to a ledge overlooking the main entrance to the cave.

### Sightless Vault CC

Sightless Vault

The *Sightless Vault* is a zone added by the Sunder & Wraithguard Creation. It is a Dwemer repository holding [Sunder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder "Skyrim:Sunder") and [Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wraithguard "Skyrim:Wraithguard"), two of the three [Tools of Kagrenac](/wiki/Lore:Kagrenac%27s_Tools "Lore:Kagrenac's Tools"). To enter, you will need to obtain the [Attunement Crystal](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Attunement_Crystal&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Attunement Crystal (page does not exist)") during the quest [Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost").

At the end of the *Abandoned Cave*, place the Attunement Crystal on the Dwarven Pedestal to unseal the entrance to the *Sightless Vault*. The small corridor to the central room has a few glowing mushrooms, a white cap sample, and a bleeding crown sample. The vault consists of a large central room with two side areas. Sunder and Wraithguard are locked behind gates in the center of the room, and thus cannot be reached.

To begin unlocking the gates, you must first activate a Vault Release Valve at the back of the room. You must then solve two steam valve puzzles in the two side rooms, which will involve activating each valve several times until the steam travels in the right direction. Your goal is to direct the steam in the direction of the next valve, until you reach the end of the piping and your journal updates. You will need to fight two [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and two [Dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") respectively after you solve each room. With this done, the door near the original Vault Release Valve will open, and an extremely powerful ebony-colored Dwarven centurion named [the Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Messenger "Skyrim:The Messenger") will emerge.

Once you defeat this final guardian, the gates will swing open, and Sunder and Wraithguard will be yours to claim. Before you depart, make sure you loot the chest in the room from which the Messenger emerged.

## Notes

- There is an [unmarked stone altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Winterhold#Altar_of_Xrib "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Winterhold") on the mountain above the cave entrance with a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") lying on it next to a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill book *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")*. The skeleton on the altar can be [exploited](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches#Gold "Skyrim:Glitches") for unlimited gold. Touching anything will cause the skeleton to rise and two additional skeletons to reanimate from nearby bone piles. According to the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, this location is called the "Altar of Xrib". It is unknown who or what "Xrib" is, but it may be something the Falmer worship.
- There are multiple places within the cave where followers can get stuck.
  - At the large pool at the beginning, the follower might remain underwater indefinitely, and cannot be commanded to move out.
  - At some of the dropping edges, the follower might keep attempting to jump down, but stay at the same location.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.
- Sightless Pit appears in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")* as a [quest](/wiki/Legends:Sightless_Pit_(quest) "Legends:Sightless Pit (quest)") and a [card](/wiki/Legends:Sightless_Pit_(card) "Legends:Sightless Pit (card)").

## Bugs

- Behind one of the tents in the Falmer camp near the start of the *Temple of Xrib*, you can walk up onto a small ledge with a glitched wall texture, allowing you to step out of the playable area and see farther into the zone. You cannot proceed any farther, however, and can only step back onto the ledge.
- Placing the Attunement Crystal[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") on the pedestal and then leaving will cause you to lose both the crystal and access to the door it unlocks.

## Maps

- 

  Sightless Pit
- 

  Temple of Xrib
- 

  Abandoned Cave

# Skyrim:Sightless Pit

## Overview
