Sightless Pit

**Sightless Pit** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") south-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). It contains three zones: *[Sightless Pit](#Sightless_Pit)*, *[Temple of Xrib](#Temple_of_Xrib)*, and *[Abandoned Cave](#Abandoned_Cave)*. A fourth zone, *[Sightless Vault](#Sightless_Vault)*, is added by the [Sunder & Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club").

Unlike most caves, you must drop down into this cave, making it impossible to leave the way you came in and forcing you to traverse the entire cave to return to the surface. There are many vertical elements in the cave, and the creatures are all leveled.

## Related Quests

- **[Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard"): Track down Kagrenac's missing Tools.

### Exterior

The entrance is west of the [Shrine of Azura](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Azura "Skyrim:Shrine of Azura"), and is marked by a single Falmer tent.

### Sightless Pit

Upon dropping into the hole in the ground, you will find yourself at the edge of a large pool of water surrounded by icy walls, with a tunnel leading to the north. A search of the deep pool of water reveals nothing of interest. Following the tunnel, it passes a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the right-hand wall, then turns to the east. A short way farther, it turns back to the north and opens into a cavern with a small camp. The camp consists of a campfire with three unowned bedrolls around it and three food barrels to the west, beside a flat-topped rock with a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Aevar Stone-Singer](/wiki/Skyrim:Aevar_Stone-Singer "Skyrim:Aevar Stone-Singer")*, and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") on top. On one of the barrels is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). The cavern continues to the north, where a ledge descends around the walls of the cavern. Immediately below the camp on a ledge is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") pierced by numerous [Falmer arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Arrow "Skyrim:Falmer Arrow"). If you drop down to this ledge, be sure not to land behind the chest, as you may get stuck and have to reload a previous save. The path descends to a level below this ledge, where another two bandits' corpses can be found, presumably of the people who set up the camp. There are a few glowing mushrooms found throughout the cave.

The path continues heading west and turns to the south after a short way. Take care along here, as there is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in the middle of the floor, on a darker patch, where it is harder to see. This triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") that comes out of the ground in front. A few paces farther on, a [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") is on the left-hand wall, with a leveled Falmer lurking inside. If the Falmer doesn't emerge (e.g., if you're sneaking), it is one of very few in the whole game that can be "extracted" by firing a ranged weapon into the hive.

The path turns to the west again, and the tunnel changes to Dwemer architecture. At the end of a short tunnel is a long dangerous drop, with a series of ledges you need to use to avoid severe damage or death. The final drop is onto a platform at the top of a curving ramp, where another pressure plate triggers a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") to fire from the wall behind you. The ramp curves around the shaft to another ledge, where a second straight ramp leads down to a ledge with a stone pool containing shallow water, with another ramp curving down from this ledge. Below is a leveled Falmer and a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") on a ledge, with a Falmer hive concealing another Falmer on the wall. A final curved ramp leads down to the ground and a corridor heading west with a track for a [spinning blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades") trap down the middle. This trap has no activation mechanism, so using a shout normally used to evade such a thing will only attract the attention of enemies lurking just ahead.

The corridor descends a short ramp to a crossroads, with two Falmer, one of which is leveled, standing in a dead end to the left, just out of sight. Using [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") or the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") may make it appear that only a single Falmer is standing there. There is an unlocked Dwarven chest ahead at the crossroads, and a corridor heading to the north from the chest, leading into another ice tunnel that turns to the west after a short distance. Ahead, it opens into a room of Dwemer construction, with a large staircase and a collapsed [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") that cannot be interacted with. Three more enemies guard the top of the stairs, consisting of a magic-using Falmer, frostbite spiders, [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and/or a leveled chaurus, depending on your level. The door at the top of the stairs leads to the second zone, the *Temple of Xrib*.

### Temple of Xrib

Temple of Xrib

The *Temple of Xrib* consists of a mixture of Dwarven ruins and frozen caves. Upon entering, a wide corridor rises to the west, turning north at the top before quickly turning west again. Through a short corridor lies a room guarded by a leveled chaurus, with a leveled Falmer patrolling a cylindrical tunnel in the room's southwestern corner. This tunnel, through which a Falmer tent is visible, leads into a large cavern. There is a hive on the wall to the left containing a Falmer, several more of which are farther into the cavern behind a rock wall to the tent's right and will be alerted by noise from fighting the first. The first tent, reachable by climbing an earthen ramp, has only a campfire inside, and a second empty tent lies to the right, along with a Falmer hive on the wall. Behind the first tent is an open pen with a few piles of [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") and a ledge (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

The path continues to the west, entering a tunnel that then turns to the south before opening into a massive mist-filled cavern, with wide stairs leading up to the south and a high ceiling that glitters like that of [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), which itself is rivaled by the huge Dwarven structure before you. You can spend a lot of time exploring different ledges and corners in this cavern, but there is nothing of interest away from the main path. From the cavern's entrance, you can see the top of a Falmer tent at the top of the first flight of stairs. A magic-using Falmer and a chaurus stand to the right of the tent, which has a fire inside. Behind, there are more levels, with a distant pair of pillars several levels above the entrance. From the top of the first flight of stairs, you can see more stairs off to the west, with two more Falmer patrolling the top. Climbing the second flight of stairs reveals a Falmer tent to the right, containing a fire and an unlocked chest. To the south, an unlocked chest sits in front of a second tent. At the other end of this level, a third Falmer tent contains yet another unlocked chest. Between the second and third tents is a flight of stairs crushed by falling masonry. To the west, a path climbs a curving ramp.

The curving ramp on the path to the west leads to a lit corridor, where a magic-using Falmer and a chaurus are patrolling. There is an unlocked Dwarven chest to the left of the second hanging light, and beyond this, another curving ramp to a tower above, guarded by another leveled Falmer. There is a short ramp down to the east on the other side leading to the level with the two pillars seen from below. There are many more enemies on this level, including a boss-leveled Falmer, chaurus, frostbite spiders, or skeevers, so a Detect Life spell or the Aura Whisper shout is recommended. Killing the creatures before the Falmer may cause a unique spell with a red blast effect to activate on their bodies, which teleports them between the two pillars and revives them. In the middle of this level, at the rear between two pillars lies a smaller pillar with a large unlocked boss chest in front. To the east is another lit tower with a lift to the third zone, the *Abandoned Cave*.

### Abandoned Cave

The *Abandoned Cave* is an unoccupied zone that serves as the exit for the cave. There is a short corridor to the south to a door that is barred from this side, preventing you from accessing the *Temple of Xrib* without first traversing the rest of the cave. The only items of interest in this area are a couple [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes and a few glowing mushrooms which can be harvested along the path. Exiting to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") will bring you to a ledge overlooking the main entrance to the cave.

### Sightless Vault CC

Sightless Vault

The *Sightless Vault* is a zone added by the Sunder & Wraithguard Creation. It is a Dwemer repository holding [Sunder](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder "Skyrim:Sunder") and [Wraithguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Wraithguard "Skyrim:Wraithguard"), two of the three [Tools of Kagrenac](/wiki/Lore:Kagrenac%27s_Tools "Lore:Kagrenac's Tools"). To enter, you will need to obtain the [Attunement Crystal](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Attunement_Crystal&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Attunement Crystal (page does not exist)") during the quest [Legends Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Legends_Lost "Skyrim:Legends Lost").

At the end of the *Abandoned Cave*, place the Attunement Crystal on the Dwarven Pedestal to unseal the entrance to the *Sightless Vault*. The small corridor to the central room has a few glowing mushrooms, a white cap sample, and a bleeding crown sample. The vault consists of a large central room with two side areas. Sunder and Wraithguard are locked behind gates in the center of the room, and thus cannot be reached.

To begin unlocking the gates, you must first activate a Vault Release Valve at the back of the room. You must then solve two steam valve puzzles in the two side rooms, which will involve activating each valve several times until the steam travels in the right direction. Your goal is to direct the steam in the direction of the next valve, until you reach the end of the piping and your journal updates. You will need to fight two [Dwarven spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") and two [Dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") respectively after you solve each room. With this done, the door near the original Vault Release Valve will open, and an extremely powerful ebony-colored Dwarven centurion named [the Messenger](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Messenger "Skyrim:The Messenger") will emerge.

Once you defeat this final guardian, the gates will swing open, and Sunder and Wraithguard will be yours to claim. Before you depart, make sure you loot the chest in the room from which the Messenger emerged.

## Notes

- There is an [unmarked stone altar](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Winterhold#Altar_of_Xrib "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Winterhold") on the mountain above the cave entrance with a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") lying on it next to a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill book *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")*. The skeleton on the altar can be [exploited](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches#Gold "Skyrim:Glitches") for unlimited gold. Touching anything will cause the skeleton to rise and two additional skeletons to reanimate from nearby bone piles. According to the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, this location is called the "Altar of Xrib". It is unknown who or what "Xrib" is, but it may be something the Falmer worship.
- There are multiple places within the cave where followers can get stuck.
  - At the large pool at the beginning, the follower might remain underwater indefinitely, and cannot be commanded to move out.
  - At some of the dropping edges, the follower might keep attempting to jump down, but stay at the same location.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.
- Sightless Pit appears in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")* as a [quest](/wiki/Legends:Sightless_Pit_(quest) "Legends:Sightless Pit (quest)") and a [card](/wiki/Legends:Sightless_Pit_(card) "Legends:Sightless Pit (card)").

## Bugs

- Behind one of the tents in the Falmer camp near the start of the *Temple of Xrib*, you can walk up onto a small ledge with a glitched wall texture, allowing you to step out of the playable area and see farther into the zone. You cannot proceed any farther, however, and can only step back onto the ledge.
- Placing the Attunement Crystal[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunder_%26_Wraithguard "Skyrim:Sunder & Wraithguard") on the pedestal and then leaving will cause you to lose both the crystal and access to the door it unlocks.

## Maps

- 

  Sightless Pit
- 

  Temple of Xrib
- 

  Abandoned Cave

# Skyrim:Silenced Tongues

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). A puzzle door inside Volunruud

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud").
2. Read [Heddic's Volunruud Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Heddic%27s_Volunruud_Notes "Skyrim:Heddic's Volunruud Notes").
3. Locate the ceremonial weapons.
4. Open the Elder's Cairn.
5. Defeat [Kvenel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kvenel_the_Tongue "Skyrim:Kvenel the Tongue").

### Getting the Quest

Immediately inside the entrance to your left is a skeleton sitting on a throne that will come alive and attack you if given the chance. After killing him, look down to find [*Heddic's Volunruud Notes*](/wiki/Skyrim:Heddic%27s_Volunruud_Notes "Skyrim:Heddic's Volunruud Notes") and what appears to be Heddic's skeleton. Reading the book begins the quest, as does attempting to open the puzzle door further on.

### Finding the Weapons

The next room is a hub chamber with 4 passages radiating off in different directions. The northern passage, up a short flight of stairs, leads to the puzzle door and the final chamber. However, you will need to collect two ceremonial weapons, an axe and a sword, before heading for the puzzle door.

Head through the southwest passage to find a chest and some loot. There's nothing else here (unless you are on the quest [The Silence Has Been Broken](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silence_Has_Been_Broken "Skyrim:The Silence Has Been Broken")), so head back to the hub chamber.

Move through the northwest door. The first and second bends have undead sleeping in the walls, and there are two more waiting around the next corner. Continue down through the cave and through the next set of iron doors to find the next objective, guarded by an undead boss with one or two draugr to help him. Take them out while being careful of the floor traps scattered between them and you. The ceremonial axe you need is on a display plaque on the wall above and behind the throne. There is also the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") skill book *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")* to the right, on the arm of the throne. Now, head back to the hub chamber.

Go through the northeast passage. The first room has two levels and a high bridge above it all. There will be several more undead waiting for you on the balcony across from the one you are on when you enter the room. Kill the ones you can see across from you with a bow or ranged spells, then head down the log ramp and past the swinging spike trap. At the next fork, the northerly passage on your left leads to the balcony across from the one where you entered the last room, so if you wish to loot the draugr you range-killed as you entered, this is the best time to do so. Return to the fork and take the southeasterly branch, which spirals up to the high bridge you saw in the first room along this branch. Immediately after crossing the high bridge, you will arrive at a small chamber with a little altar amid numerous candles. Enter cautiously because there is an undead awaiting your arrival, out of your line of sight in a wall-crypt to your immediate right as you enter. Continue through the iron door and to your second objective, the ceremonial sword. As you approach the central coffin, two undeads will pop out of the wall-crypts flanking you and attack. After defeating them, take the ceremonial sword from the skeleton in the central coffin and head back the way you came, to the hub chamber.

Now, with both ceremonial weapons in your inventory, head up the short flight of stairs into the northern passage and activate the iron doors to Elder's Cairn. The two ceremonial weapons will be removed from your inventory and be placed into their respective receptacles in the doors. Activate the doors again to enter Elder's Cairn.

A short distance down this path is a small area with a burnt corpse and some minor loot. Just beyond that is a draugr guarding a large spider web, and then the final chamber, which contains The Tongue Chieftain [Kvenel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kvenel_the_Tongue "Skyrim:Kvenel the Tongue") himself, along with an undead conjurer.

### Fighting Kvenel

Kvenel is a bluish, ghostly form seated on a throne on the far side of the room, and his conjurer is a draugr to the right (southwest) of Kvenel.

The easiest way to defeat Kvenel and his minion (if you have decent Archery skills and enchantments, a powerful bow or crossbow and the Deadly Aim perk from the Sneak skill tree) is to sneak carefully into the room until you have a clear shot at Kvenel as he sits on his throne and shoot him dead with a triple-damage sneak shot with your bow. If your first shot doesn't kill him, you should have time for a second shot as he tries to rise from his throne. Meanwhile, instead of summoning an atronach or attacking you, his conjurer minion conveniently comes over to stand in front of the throne to see what is troubling the now-dead Kvenel, so you won't even have to re-aim your bow to take out the minion.

If you are not able, or inclined, to take out Kvenel and his minion from the entrance of the chamber, you will have a semi-difficult fight on your hands. Kvenel himself uses two ice-enchanted melee weapons, while his conjurer minion is a draugr who summons atronachs and casts ranged frost spells to slow you down.

Because he casts ranged ice and frost spells and summons atronachs, it is advisable to take out the conjurer first. Alternatively, you could try to draw Kvenel into another room to kill him first, then go back to the throne room to handle the conjurer.

The conjurer will summon a Frost Atronach when he sees you. He also uses ice magic to slow you down, making running away or closing the initial gap difficult for melee fighters. You can use the pillars on the northeastern side of the chamber (your left as you enter) to your advantage by using them to block the ice spells as well as blocking his line of sight and regaining stealth. For melee characters, [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") and plenty of stamina are helpful.

Once the conjurer is dead, Kvenel is relatively simple to defeat using any attacks you like and dodging to stay out of his melee range whenever possible. Blocking is also helpful here.

Among his ghostly remains is his enchanted sword, [Eduj](/wiki/Skyrim:Eduj "Skyrim:Eduj"). Due to a bug, you may have to activate his remains again to obtain [Okin](/wiki/Skyrim:Okin "Skyrim:Okin"), the enchanted axe. If it is not listed as loot on his corpse, you may also be able to find it on the ground near his remains.

To the right of the throne is a chest with leveled loot and around the stone platform are various potions. Exit the room through the southwest passage where you will find a word wall with a word of the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") shout. Up the stairs will be the bridge you passed under on your way into the boss chamber along with any draugr you didn't snipe on your way in. Across the bridge, you will find a final chest of leveled loot along with a [Dragon Priest Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Dagger "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Dagger") and a reference book about [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") on the floor.

As you return to the bridge, look to your hard right to find a chest on a ledge in the shadows. You can reach it by jumping to the tree roots and then jumping again over to the chest, or by using [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). Drop down and head south to find the exit.

## Bugs

- The swinging spiked door may be sprung by draugr and then not reset, making the rest of the northeast branch inaccessible. **?**
- Sometimes the ceremonial weapons are unable to be picked up. **?**
  - Reloading a past save should fix this.
  -  You can open the console, click the weapon, and then type `moveto player`. That should place the weapon at your feet and you should be able to pick it up.
- Putting in the sword first, then getting the axe and putting it in, may make the door inoperable.
- If you have the ceremonial weapons on you, the door might not take the weapons, making the rest of the quest and the word wall inaccessible. This may occur if you pick up one of the weapons before starting the quest. **?**
  - Drop the weapon(s) and then activate the door to start the quest and it should take the weapons.
- Sometimes, reading Heddic's Volunruud Notes will not give you the quest.
  - This may lead to the door not activating the quest either, making the quest inaccessible and the door unable to be opened, even with both ceremonial weapons in your inventory. One cause found for the quest not triggering is when Serana is your follower, as there is a skeleton that aggros as soon as you enter, she will reanimate the body you're supposed to explore to trigger the quest. Leave her outside to be sure it triggers, then proceed.
  - To activate the quest line, drop it and all ceremonial weapons from your inventory, then activate the sealed door.
  - To activate the quest line, drop both ceremonial weapons and the journal, exit Volunruud, re-enter then read the journal again.
  - If you have ANY vampire follower(s) -- not just Serana -- have them wait outside of Volunruud and you will experience no bugs. This is best done before entering the dungeon. The quest will trigger when you read the journal. Then bring your vampire follower(s) back and the quest will proceed as normal.
  -  Use the console command `coc Volunruud02` to get past the door.
  -  Alternatively, use the console command `tcl` to clip through the door and activate it from behind (it's a normal door), which moves you to Elder Cairn. Don't forget to switch tcl off afterwards.
- Don't kill Kvenel while he is sitting on his throne. You can get Eduj, but when you activate his remains again to obtain Okin, it won't be there. Reloading a previous save to re-kill Kvenel off his throne solves the problem. **?**
  - You can kill Kvenel while he is sitting and still get both weapons if you pickpocket Okin first. Eduj is still lootable from his remains.
  - do not pickup the weapons and leave for other quests the ceremonial weapons may glitch out of your inventory

## Quest Stages

| Silenced Tongues (dunVolunruudQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I may be able to recover two ceremonial weapons within Volunruud which will allow me to enter the Elder's Cairn. *Objective 10:* Locate The Ceremonial Weapons |
| 13 |  | I've found the ceremonial axe in Volunruud. |
| 14 |  | I've found the ceremonial Sword in Volunruud. |
| 20 |  | Now that I have both ceremonial weapons, I should be able to open the door to the Elder's Cairn. *Objective 20:* Open the Elder's Cairn |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Defeat Kvenel |
| 100 | ☑ | I defeated an ancient draugr named Kvenel within Volunruud. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunVolunruudQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunVolunruudQST`.

# Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Dwarven Ruin: Silent City Catacombs | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachSewer01 | |
| Region | |
| [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| Along the river east of Blackreach's city | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Geode_Ore "Skyrim:Geode Ore") | 2 |

The entrance to the Silent City Catacombs

The **Silent City Catacombs** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). The direct entrance to the catacombs is on the river in the center of the cavern, just east of Blackreach's city. The catacombs also connect to the [Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station") through a door at the west end.

### Exterior

East-southeast of the entrance on the other side of the river are two leveled [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") beside a stone wall, with several [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), a [geode vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Geode_Vein "Skyrim:Geode Vein"), and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") nearby. A second geode vein can be found to the northeast. The entrance looks like a sewer outlet, with a [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") growing beside the unlocked gate.

### Silent City Catacombs

Upon entering, you emerge in a partially flooded cave, with stone steps leading out of the water on your right. There are two [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the cave wall on your left, and beyond the mushrooms is a geode vein. A doorway to the west leads into a corridor, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") ahead. Moving around the corner to the north, you will encounter a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). It is standing by a T-junction, with a closed gate ahead to the north and another corridor to the west. Take care at the junction to avoid a pair of well-disguised [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that trigger a [slicer trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer"). The trap can be used to deal with a second Falmer that is lurking partway down the western corridor. Behind the unlocked gate to the north is a lever which will toggle part of the slicer trap, presumably so you can lure your enemies here and kill them. The second Falmer is standing by a caved-in corridor on the left with a single chaurus egg sac, while beyond the cave-in is a second pair of disguised pressure plates triggering a second slicer trap.

Inside the catacombs

The corridor then continues into the lower level of a two-level room. The upper level is not reachable from the lower level. There are two Falmer on the upper level that can snipe down on you if you are detected, one an archer and the other a magic user. The first Falmer lurks on a stone bridge that connects two sections of the room overhead, and the second is near the back of the room. This part of the corridor is full of shallow water, making [sneaking](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") even harder. The path turns to the north, and continues through a circular opening.

Beyond the opening is a room that doglegs to the left, then continues through another doorway into a room with metal grating for a floor and water beneath. A Falmer lurks just around the corner to the west. It is standing by a square hole in the grating where a sheet has fallen loose and dropped to the bottom of the water. To the south of the opening is a single chaurus egg sac. Jump into the water to find three unlocked chests hidden below. To find the first chest, swim east as far as you can go, then turn south. The other two are next to each other at the west end of the underwater area, on the left. Exiting the water is simple due to the grating to the north of the hole having dropped slightly, forming a ramp out. The path continues to the west on the far side of the gap before turning to the south.

After turning south, the corridor exits the grated area and climbs a ramp to another room containing a Falmer. A hole knocked through the eastern wall in the southeast corner leads to the upper level of the two-level room you passed through earlier, where the two Falmer were. The magic-using Falmer carries a [shaman's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Shaman%27s_Key "Skyrim:Shaman's Key"). On your left is a flight of stairs leading to a bridge over the lower corridor, with stairs back down on the other side. The far side has a geode vein on the ground beside the stairs, and another bridge leading to a closed door to the south. On your right is a culvert emerging from a caved-in tunnel in the west wall before dropping onto the lower path. Instead of crossing the two bridges, you can simply turn right from the previous room and cross the culvert to reach the southern door more directly.

Through the door is a large open room, with a raised section on your right. There can be up to three Falmer here: one on the raised section, who is a magic user and carries a shaman key, and two in the southwestern corner by some stairs leading up to the raised section. A door in the northwestern corner leads to the [Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station").

## Bugs

- Silent City Catacombs has numerous issues with its navmesh, including broken links, missing sections, inaccessible islands, and verts at too steep an angle to navigate.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3, addresses this issue. The entire cell had to be cleaned up and readjusted to resolve this.

## Maps

Map of the Silent City Catacombs

# Skyrim:Silent Moons Camp

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Silent Moons Camp ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silent+Moons+Camp)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Silent_Moons_Camp "Lore:Silent Moons Camp")) | | |

Silent Moons Camp

**Silent Moons Camp** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[Silent Moons Camp](#Silent_Moons_Camp)*.

## Related Quests

- **[In the Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:In_the_Shadows "Skyrim:In the Shadows")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow_of_Shadows "Skyrim:Bow of Shadows"): Save the Jarl of Whiterun from an assassination plot.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Lunar Forge

The main part of the ruins are built on a hill and consists of a thick semi-circular wall with a walkway along the top around an open-topped dome-like barrow with an enclosed outer walkway around the central area which contains the unique [Lunar Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Forge "Skyrim:Lunar Forge"). The normal approach is from the southwest, where a stone hut on the left can be found as you approach, similar to several huts found at [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian"). It contains two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels and two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). Past this, by the bottom of a series of flights of wide stairs, on the left is a campfire, with a long wooden table holding two portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), four [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), and a wedge of cheese. There is also a rack with three whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hanging from it and four food barrels nearby, while on the right is a wooden door leading into the interior. There is also a doorway blocked by a lowered gate in the bottom of the thick wall to the south. There are a number of leveled [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") guarding both the approach and working [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") at the top. There is a broken stone table in the outer walkway around the forge with three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") on top.

The Lunar Forge includes a complete blacksmith's forge, an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). On the workbench is a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Light Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Light Armor Forging")*, a book *[Notes On The Lunar Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_On_The_Lunar_Forge "Skyrim:Notes On The Lunar Forge")* which describes the forge, and a random leveled one-handed weapon enchanted with a unique enchantment which will burn the target when the moons are out. This and other enchanted "[lunar weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Items#Lunar_Weapons "Skyrim:Leveled Items")" found in the camp may take one of the following forms: [lunar iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Lunar Iron Mace"), [lunar iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Lunar Iron Sword"), [lunar iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Lunar Iron War Axe"), [lunar steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Lunar Steel Mace"), [lunar steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Lunar Steel Sword"), or [lunar steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Lunar_Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Lunar Steel War Axe"). On top of the grindstone is a second random leveled one-handed lunar weapon. There is also an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the right of the workbench.

### Silent Moons Camp

Immediately through the door is an area with distinctly Nordic architecture, with a campfire surrounded by four unowned bedrolls. There is a long wooden table and chairs on your left and a set of shelves in the back corner of the room holding four bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the right of the fire is a tunnel, with a small table, three food barrels, and an empty cart on either side of it. The tunnel descends a short distance to the east, before turning south and opening out into a storage area, where you are likely to find the bandit leader and up to two bandits. In the storage area are four barrels of food, an unlocked chest, as well as clusters of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), and [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungi. There is also a tunnel to the east, which turns immediately south and descends to a pair of adept-locked iron double doors. A bandit will be guarding these and will be alerted to any fighting above. There are two food barrels and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") to the left of the door.

Through the doors is a room with a ladder in the middle, with an unlocked chest to the right. Around the walls are three sets of shelves holding a [solution of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Health "Skyrim:Solution of Health"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [philter of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Philter of Regeneration"), three [potions of extra magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), a [potion of plentiful stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina"), a random leveled one-handed lunar weapon, three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a bottle of [lingering stamina poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Lingering_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Lingering Stamina Poison"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), and some bread. Hanging from the ceiling is a rack holding two bunches of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). There is also a lever behind the door to the left, when entering the room, which operates the door you entered through.

The ladder exits inside a tower containing an unlocked chest and a chain to the right of the doorway, which raises the gate blocking access. There is an upper floor within the tower; however, this can only be reached by climbing partway up the hill and dropping down to it from the outer wall. On the upper level is a long wooden table holding a random leveled one-handed lunar weapon, a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"), and a potion of regeneration, with a potion of enhanced stamina on the floor under the table. To the right of the table is a food barrel, and against the west wall is a set of shelves holding two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of healing, magicka, or stamina and an [iron cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor").

## Notes

- Humorously, the bandits occupying the camp may inadvertently draw the ire of the [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") from the nearby stream; the mudcrabs will then launch an assault on the camp and may succeed in clearing the bandits from the camp exterior at lower levels. Similarly, if you are having trouble with the bandits in the camp exterior, you can lead them to the two peaceful [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth") that patrol the plains near the ruin; these creatures should handily defeat the bandits. You can assist the mammoths, but beware of friendly fire, or you'll have to deal with both the bandits and the mammoths.
- You can not actually use the Lunar Forge to create lunar enchanted [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), although you can disenchant one of the weapons then create your own using any [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter").
- The best possible lunar weapons will spawn here if you are at least level 8.
- The gate to the tower stays open and doesn't reset when the location respawns.
- Nothing respawns in the tower except one of the random potions on the set of shelves on the upper floor.
- Two [silver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") are on the east side of a dry stream bed south of the camp.
- Two [moonstone ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") are north of the camp.
- One [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") is on a small hill northeast of the camp in the direction of [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp").
- *Notes On The Lunar Forge* incorrectly states that the Lunar weapons here give you a [vampire-like](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism") effect that transfers health from the victim to the user like [absorb health](/wiki/Skyrim:Absorb_Health "Skyrim:Absorb Health"), when their [real enchantment](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Damage "Skyrim:Light Damage") doesn't absorb health at all.

## Bugs

- A permanently disabled copy of the skill book *[Heavy Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Heavy Armor Forging")* is placed here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The enchanted weapons may not be here if your level is too low. **?**

## Overview

Silent Ruin

**Silent Ruin** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"). It is north of the Dwarven city. The building is devoid of any [creatures](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") or [automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"); however, you do need to keep an eye out for traps.

### Exterior

Outside the building against the northeast corner is a large brass pipe with a [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") growing beside it. A path north of the building leads down to a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") camp with two tents and two Falmer. Four [dead salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hang from a rack next to the tents, and there is a [geode vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Geode_Vein "Skyrim:Geode Vein") just northeast of the two tents.

### Silent Ruin

Interior view

The entrance is on the southwest side of the building, and is unlocked. It leads into a single room, with a short flight of stairs leading down to the main floor. Two huge stone pillars to the northeast and southwest support a very high roof. Opposite the entrance is a throne on a slightly raised platform. On the seat of the throne is a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(book) "Skyrim:Warrior (book)")*; however, care is needed, as there is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") in front of the throne that triggers a [spinning blade trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Blades "Skyrim:Spinning Blades"). To the right of the throne is a crimson nirnroot growing in a large metal urn. Finally, in the northwest corner, there is a set of Dwemer shelves against the west wall holding various small Dwemer items, and to the right, against the north wall, is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

## Bugs

- Followers will not follow you into the building, and instead will run north, possibly attempting to leave Blackreach to find you.

## Maps

- 

  Silent Ruin

# Skyrim:Silus Vesuius's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Silus Vesuius's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Silus+Vesuius%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DawnstarSilussHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| North side of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Silus Vesuius's House

**Silus Vesuius's House** is the home of [Silus Vesuius](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius"), and a museum dedicated to the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn").

The house is located on the north side of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), close to the coastline. It is the last house in the row to the left of [Beitild's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild%27s_House "Skyrim:Beitild's House"). It is inaccessible until you reach level 20. It consists of one area, *[Silus Vesuius's House](#Silus_Vesuius.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Silus Vesuius](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius") |

## Related Quests

- **[Visit the museum in Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Visit_the_museum_in_Dawnstar "Skyrim:Visit the museum in Dawnstar")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.
- **[Pieces of the Past](/wiki/Skyrim:Pieces_of_the_Past "Skyrim:Pieces of the Past")**: Retrieve the scattered pieces of [Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Mehrunes' Razor") and reforge this deadly blade.

## Silus Vesuius's House

Silus Vesuius's House is a single-room house. Half the house has been converted into a museum for the [Mythic Dawn](/wiki/Lore:Mythic_Dawn "Lore:Mythic Dawn"), while the other half is Silus Vesuius' living area. There are four display cabinets around the northwestern half of the house, with a Mythic Dawn banner behind each. The first three of these are adept-locked, while the fourth cannot be interacted with. The first display cabinet to your left as you enter contains two [Mythic Dawn robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Robes "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Robes") (one hooded and one not), a pair of [Mythic Dawn boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Boots "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Boots"), and a pair of [Mythic Dawn gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Gloves "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Gloves"). The second display cabinet contains a tattered page of the *[Mysterium Xarxes](/wiki/Lore:Mysterium_Xarxes "Lore:Mysterium Xarxes")*. The third display cabinet contains copies of all four of the *[Mythic Dawn Commentaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mythic_Dawn_Commentaries "Skyrim:Mythic Dawn Commentaries")*. The fourth display cabinet contains the [Scabbard of Mehrunes' Razor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scabbard_of_Mehrunes%27_Razor "Skyrim:Scabbard of Mehrunes' Razor"), until removed by Silus during the related quest.

The southeastern end of the house is Silus' living area, and contains a stone fireplace opposite the door, with a cooking pot to the right on the hearth, and a hanging rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") above. There are several pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") to the left on the hearth. A wardrobe stands in the eastern corner of the room. There is a double owned bed against the southeast wall, and two barrels in the southern corner. There is a small table and chair holding a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg").

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"Also known as the Museum of the Mythic Dawn, the building is dedicated to the cult in Dawnstar. This is Silus's vain attempt to capture some attention and infamy for his family's past deeds. The pride of the collection is his impressive assortment of Mythic Dawn memorabilia, as well as a piece of Mehrunes' Razor that is kept in a secured display case."*

- If you visit Silus Vesuius's House before receiving the [museum pamphlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Museum_Pamphlet "Skyrim:Museum Pamphlet"), the Mythic Dawn banners are not yet present. They only appear after the museum has opened.
- All the locked display cases can be freely lockpicked, but the items on the inside of two of them (the one containing the uniforms and the one with the books) have to be stolen. Additionally, the books and the robes, shoes and gloves respawn, along with the rest of his house after ten days.

## Bugs

- Version 1.6.342.0.8 of the [Anniversary Edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Anniversary_Edition "Skyrim:Anniversary Edition") causes a crash-to-desktop when entering the house. This is caused by a corruption to a texture.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version Version 1.6.353, fixes this bug.
- If you use any form of weapon or Destruction-type spell on the tattered page of the *[Mysterium Xarxes](/wiki/Lore:Mysterium_Xarxes "Lore:Mysterium Xarxes")*, it will transform into an immobile bucket. This transformation is permanent.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12015)) The attached destruction data is removed.
- After killing him in the Pieces of the Past quest, Silus's bed can be slept in despite the "Owned" marker. **?**

# Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

Silver-Blood Inn

**Silver-Blood Inn** is an [inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Skyrim:Inns") located in the city of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

The inn is owned by Markarth's prominent [Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thonar_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thonar Silver-Blood") clan, even though the members of the family are never seen in the building. They leave the business of running the inn to [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr"), who rents rooms and sells food and drink. His wife, [Frabbi](/wiki/Skyrim:Frabbi "Skyrim:Frabbi"), works at the inn, at least when she is not busy arguing with her husband. If Kleppr dies she takes over running the business, with nearly as many complaints about her husband as when he was alive. Their two children, [Hreinn](/wiki/Skyrim:Hreinn "Skyrim:Hreinn") and [Hroki](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroki "Skyrim:Hroki"), are also kept busy with jobs around the inn.

- **[Fortunate Son](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortunate_Son "Skyrim:Fortunate Son")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Claim a fortune.[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club")

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Silver-Blood Inn

Inside the inn

The Silver-Blood Inn is one of the largest inns in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), and many other townspeople can frequently be found at the inn. Entry is directly into the common room with a central bar facing you and a fireplace behind against the southwest wall. There are two corridors off this room one to the southeast and one to the northwest, with two flights of stairs up to closed doors also one to each side. [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr"), the innkeeper, is always standing behind the counter ready to welcome all-comers. There are many [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks around the establishment and all the beds and tables are made of stone. In the northern and eastern corners are sets of shelves, the first holds a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and the second just clutter. To the right of the eastern shelves is a shelf with five [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a cast iron pot containing a potato and [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), with a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") to the right and having two pieces of cheese on top. A matching ledge opposite to the north holds a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), with an unusable barrel beside it with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top.

The counter is a square U-shape, facing the entrance. On the counter there is a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), with six wooden bar stools arranged in twos on each side. Under the counter are two small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a loaf of bread and a [key to Margret's room](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Margret%27s_Room "Skyrim:Key to Margret's Room"), that is useful during [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") quest, however you can gain it purely by asking Kleppr. Between the corridor and stairs to the southeast is a small set of shelves with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a wooden bowl containing two [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") on top. To the left of the fireplace against the southwest wall is a basket containing a cabbage and [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). There is nothing of interest on the right side of the fireplace. Nor is there anything of interest on a set of shelves between the corridor and stairs to the northwest.

Your room in the inn

The corridor to the southeast has a door a few paces along on the left, which is the room you can rent. It enters into a bedroom with a single owned bed against the northeast wall, with a table to the southeast. There is only clutter in this room. Further along this corridor is a flight of stairs leading up to Margret's room, if you managed to save her during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") she will either be in here eating or in the common room sat by the fireplace. The room has a single owned bed against the southeast wall, with a wall shelf above holding a copy of *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Skyrim:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")* and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). To the northeast is a table and chair with a bottle of wine, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and a goat cheese wedge on top with a [plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate") and [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"). At the other end of the room is a shelf with a few loaves of bread and three apples on top of it. In front of the shelf is an end table with a plate holding a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), a medium coin purse and three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") all on top. The end table also contains [Margret's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Margret%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Margret's Journal") (see [notes](#Notes)).

The closed door to the southeast opens directly into Kleppr and [Frabbi's](/wiki/Skyrim:Frabbi "Skyrim:Frabbi") quarters. They consist of a double owned bed against the northeast wall with an end table on either side of the bed. Between the end table and bed on the left, is a shelf with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and small coin purse on it. The end table to the right has a bottle of wine on top. To the right is a shelf on the southeast wall with an apprentice [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") next to a dresser with a [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger"), a medium coin purse and a wooden bowl containing a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") on top. Above the dresser is a shelf with a barrel containing ingredients, while to the right is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") and a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). In the southern corner of the room is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and pot hanging in front of it. The pot contains a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") and portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"). To the right of the fireplace is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a table and two chairs to the right. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a salmon steak, a [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a portion of grilled leeks, a [tomato](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), two loaves of bread and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge").

The door to the northwest opens into a twin bedroom with two single owned beds. They are both facing the same way, against the northeast wall with an end table between them with a bunch of tundra cotton and two loose septims on top. By the first bed, on the northeast wall is a shelf is a small coin purse and copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")*, which if you haven't already started the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)") reading it will cause the quest to start. Above the head of the bed, on a shelf is a bottle of alto wine and a loaf of bread. The shelf by the second bed has a loaf of bread on it. The shelf on the northwest wall, by the foot of the second bed has on it a couple of apples and a bunch of lavender in a cast iron pot. To the left of this is a tall wardrobe. There is a fireplace in the western corner with a cooking pot on a stand in front and a rack hanging from the ceiling to the right, holding a bunch of dried elves ear and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), with a seared slaughterfish on a block of wood beneath it. To the left of the fireplace is a pile of firewood with a shelf above it holding a copy of *[Herbane's Bestiary: Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Herbane%27s_Bestiary:_Hagravens "Skyrim:Herbane's Bestiary: Hagravens")* and to the left of the firewood is a barrel containing ingredients with a loaf of bread and [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on top. In the southern corner is a table and two chairs, with a bottle of wine, a baked potato, a red apple, a loaf of bread and a goat cheese wedge on top.

The corridor to the northwest has a door on the right similar to the one you rent, with an owned single bed against the southeast wall, with a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") and a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the floor above the head of the bed and a loaf of bread on a shelf beside them. Above the bed is another wall shelf holding a bottle of alto wine and a basket containing a few loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"). Against the northwest wall is a table with a bottle of alto wine, a potato, a couple of pieces of eidar cheese and a basket containing two gourd on top. To the left of the table on a shelf is a small coin purse. Like the other corridor past this room there are stairs leading up to another bedroom, used by [Hogni Red-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hogni_Red-Arm "Skyrim:Hogni Red-Arm") when he isn't working, selling raw meat from his stall on the market. It has a single owned bed against the northwest wall, with a shelf above holding a bottle of wine and a bucket containing three potatoes by the foot of the bed. On the shelf to the southwest is an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a [Dwemer Pan](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Pan "Skyrim:Dwemer Pan"), two bottles of alto wine, a pair of cabbages, a red apple and a leather strip. Against the northeast wall is a table and chair, with an iron dagger, a bottle of wine, a joint of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") and a tomato on top.

There are several people who spend either all or a significant amount of their time at the inn. [Ogmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund "Skyrim:Ogmund") is the local bard and spends most of his time here, although he sleeps at his [own house](/wiki/Skyrim:Ogmund%27s_House "Skyrim:Ogmund's House"). [Cosnach](/wiki/Skyrim:Cosnach "Skyrim:Cosnach"), [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine"), and [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") are some of the regulars at the bar in the evening, but they do not live in the inn.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in the inn's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Notes

- There is a  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the top right of the entrance door.
- Editor ids suggest that this inn was originally named the Silver-Fish Inn, and that the Silver-Blood clan also originally had that name.
- If Margret dies at the start of the relevant quest picking up her journal will cause it to become stuck as a quest item permanently.--(see the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy") for more details).

# Skyrim:Silver Lining

## Overview

Rigel Strong-Arm's treasure

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Talk to [Endon](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") for the details.
3. Travel to [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch") and enter the caves from the basement.
4. Make your way to the Bandit's Sanctuary and take the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch_Key "Skyrim:Pinewatch Key") from [Rigel Strong-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Rigel_Strong-Arm "Skyrim:Rigel Strong-Arm").
5. Open the room and take the [silver mold](/wiki/Skyrim:Curious_Silver_Mold "Skyrim:Curious Silver Mold").
6. Return the mold to Endon.

### A Special Job

Once you've completed five additional jobs in the city of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), speak to [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") at the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") to receive a 'special job'. Delvin explains that he has received word from [Endon](/wiki/Skyrim:Endon "Skyrim:Endon") in Markarth of a special request. Travel to Markarth and speak to Endon, who will be in the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") for this quest. He will explain that he wants you to recover a silver mold he ordered, which was stolen by bandits in transit. *"The only thing I can tell you is that the mold was taken to the bandit's hideout... a small cottage called [Pinewatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch "Skyrim:Pinewatch")."*

- If you've already been to Pinewatch and have the mold, he will take it and the quest will be completed.

### A Hidden Entrance

When you enter Pinewatch, a man named [Rhorlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Rhorlak "Skyrim:Rhorlak") may engage you in conversation. You can bribe him into revealing the location of the bandit's hideout, which is opened by a button next to the bookcase in the basement.

The button opens a hidden entrance that leads down to some caves. There are three bandits here who can all be avoided by dropping to the lower area and carefully making your way around the back and back up the planks. The exit will be on your left if you fight across the bridge (and therefore on your right if you sneak up from behind via the lower level).

The three bandits in the next room are harder to avoid, but this can be done with some careful timing. There is one more bandit in front of the door to Pinewatch Bandit's Sanctuary; this last one is nearly impossible to avoid because of the light sources in the tunnel. If you prefer to fight through this whole section, there is no reason to leave any of the bandits alive.

After entering the next section, you'll find several bandits conversing around a table, but they can be avoided by sneaking around the clutter to the left and carefully making your way up the path to the right. The next bandit can be avoided by staying in the shadows. Soon you will come to a dark room with several dead draugr, patrolled by another lone bandit. There is a treasure room to the right which contains an [unusual gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") and various other valuables, along with a booby-trapped novice-level chest.

Past the draugr room is a living area, with a shared bedroom separated by a wooden partition from a bar, where several bandits will discuss their leader's obsession with protecting her treasure. It is very difficult to sneak past all of these bandits, due mainly to the firelight and the directions the bandits face. With a high Sneak skill you can sneak past by hugging the left wall, or you can use a short duration invisibility effect and sneak straight through the middle of the room (even eating vampire dust may work with the right timing).

### Every Cloud...

Next is [Rigel Strong-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Rigel_Strong-Arm "Skyrim:Rigel Strong-Arm")'s room. She alternates between sitting at the table, patrolling the next tunnel, and sleeping. The first part contains six bone rattles, a workbench, and a potion on the shelves. Her bedroom contains a potion on the dresser, a leveled weapon propped against an apprentice-locked chest, and a leveled soul gem on the bedside table. Rigel carries the [Pinewatch Treasure Room Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinewatch_Treasure_Room_Key "Skyrim:Pinewatch Treasure Room Key"), and you do not need to kill her to complete the quest.

Rigel has taken a few precautions and set up some traps to stop anyone from getting to her treasure. The room after the next tunnel contains a bone rattle and a master-locked door, which can also be unlocked by the treasure room key. There is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") before the bridge, which activates [darts](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from both sides. At the start of the next tunnel is another pressure plate that activates [blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") in front of you, and another plate at the far end that activates a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from the right. After that is a metal pressure plate that activates a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") from the right. Opening the final door before the treasure room activates another mace, while the final trap is a metal pressure plate which activates darts from the walls and ceiling.

Your patience and fortitude is rewarded by a random and leveled assortment of potions, ore, ingots, coin purses, loose coins, and enchanted armor, and of course the silver mold. There is also a leveled chest beside the exit door, which opens to behind the barred door in the first section of the caves. If you left the bandits alive, you can again drop to the lower level and sneak back to the house area of Pinewatch.

### ...has a Silver Lining

Return to Endon and give him the mold, and he will reward you with an enchanted piece of armor, and offer his services as a fence.

Report back to Delvin. He'll compliment you on your success, *"I hear Endon's quite pleased to have his merchandise back. He's a powerful ally in Markarth. Should help the Guild regain a foothold in the west."* He will also inform you of a new merchant setting up shop in the Ragged Flagon.

## Notes

- If you press the button in Rhorlak's basement without hearing about it from him first, he will turn hostile towards you.
- After completing this quest, three [Thief Cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") barrels will appear around Markarth.

## Quest Stages

| Silver Lining (TGTQ01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Endon, a silversmith residing in Markarth, has requested assistance from the Thieves Guild. *Objective 10:* Speak to Endon the Silversmith |
| 20 |  | Endon had a silver mold stolen while it was en route to Markarth. The item in question was taken by a group of bandits led by Rigel Strong-Arm and brought to their hideout at Pinewatch. *Objective 20:* Enter Pinewatch |
| 30 |  | *Objective 30:* Recover Endon's Silver Mold |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* Return to Endon |
| 200 | ☑ | The silver mold has been returned to Endon, and the Thieves Guild can now count on him as an influential ally in Markarth. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage TGTQ01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest TGTQ01`.

# Skyrim:Silverdrift Lair

## Overview
