Silverdrift Lair

**Silverdrift Lair** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south-southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). It contains only one zone, *[Silverdrift Lair](#Silverdrift_Lair)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Disarm](/wiki/Skyrim:Disarm "Skyrim:Disarm") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Two [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") guard the entrance of the ruin.

### Silverdrift Lair

Interior

Two dead bandits flank a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") in the first room. There is a large urn and a set of shelves holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") against the south wall. There are [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle") and tankards throughout this ruin. A passage heads east, with a dead bandit by a T-junction and a hanging rack holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") above. The passage to the east is blocked by a barred door. On the left, among some rubble, is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and some random [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). The passage to the north is patrolled by a draugr, and leads to an iron door.

A draugr will greet you on the other side of the door. There are sets of shelves to the north and two to the south holding mainly clutter, except for a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on the upright shelves to the south. There are two sideboards by pillars near the middle of the room, with a dead bandit on the floor between them. The right-hand sideboard holds an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") leans against it. An embalming table opposite the door adorned with candles holds another random potion of healing, a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*.

The next room has multiple levels, and is accessed by a raised walkway starting to the left of the embalming table. This walkway links with others that lead to the far side of the room and with spiraled wooden ramps that descend to the lower level. A matching walkway to the right of the table has collapsed. There is a caged walkway far above running east-west. A draugr magic-user patrols the lower level near a campfire and a throne. There is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") beside the campfire, with a rack with two more rabbits and another pheasant to the left. There is another dead bandit beside the fire. If you look west from the fire, under the balcony you came down from, you'll see a wooden wall on a slightly raised platform. Behind this wall is a bedroll and an unlocked chest. Northeast of the fire, you'll find two [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and another barred wooden door. From here, you can either take the detour for more loot through a concealed door on the ground floor to the west, or head directly for the word wall via the second-level walkway to the east.

In the middle of the west wall is a short passage with an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") and an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging above. There are two rune totems, one showing a snake, and the other a whale; each has a handle near the top. The answer is high on the wall concealed by the oil lantern. Pulling the whale opens a concealed door, while pulling the snake releases the lantern which ignites the oil slick. You can also disarm this trap by igniting the oil before stepping into the area. Behind the concealed door is a tunnel that twists and turns.

The tunnel is covered in light cobwebs that can be walked through, and ends in a room containing two upright sarcophagi in the middle that release draugr when approached. There are three further upright sarcophagi around the walls, none of which contain draugr. On the floor in front of the sarcophagus to the north are three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). A sideboard in the northwestern corner has a random [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka") on top. A doorway to the east leads to typical brightly lit catacombs, with two upright sarcophagi on either side of a central pillar patrolled by two leveled draugr. A table to the southeast holds an expert-locked chest, a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and a random [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor").

A northeastern doorway leads to the next room, which has three two-room sections. One room of each section has a handle that opens a rotating door into the other room. The northern handle reveals a small room with a chest with some minor loot, as well as a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), three coin purses, and/or the [Ancestral Sword of Clan Ice-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Sword_of_Clan_Ice-Blade "Skyrim:Ancestral Sword of Clan Ice-Blade") if [The Gray Cowl Returns!](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed. The middle handle opens the way to a draugr. The southern handle leads to a hallway that turns south and ends at a door with a bar blocking it. Raising the bar and opening the door leads back to the multi-level room with the campfire.

Crossing the walkways to the east leads to a second balcony. Take care, as there are two [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that trigger [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") traps. There are also two draugr just past the traps, one of whom is leveled and equipped with a leveled [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and may also possess a melee weapon. With correct timing and planning, the spike walls can be used to help take down both of the draugr. In the center of the east wall is a doorway blocked by spears; the handle to lower these is on a stone post on your right as you approach. Before passing through the doorway, to the south is a pedestal with an enchanted [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"). Taking the helmet triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the floor. To avoid damage, either knock the helmet off with a bow or ranged magic or use [Telekinesis](/wiki/Skyrim:Telekinesis "Skyrim:Telekinesis") to retrieve it.

Through the doorway to the east is a short passage leading to an iron door. Through the door is a room guarded by a draugr. There is an unlocked chest and a random potion of healing on a stone table, with a dead bandit lying on a bedroll to the right. There is an iron shield on the floor beside the bandit. To the left of the table is a small empty alcove blocked by an adept-locked gate. To the south is a gate that is raised by pulling a chain to the left. Stand to the side when pulling the chain, as opening the gate will trigger a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from behind the gate.

*Thief*

Through the gate, the passage turns first west then north, while ascending several flights of stairs. At the top is a room with a long dining table with benches along both sides and a couple leveled draugr. There is a leveled [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") (which may be enchanted) and a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") on the table, with a dead bandit to the right of it. To the north is another passage which takes a couple turns as it climbs more stairs. A draugr is guarding the room at the top, which contains a wooden table with a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a random shield on top and a sideboard holding an unlocked chest. To the right of this is a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill book *[Thief](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_(book) "Skyrim:Thief (book)")* on the ground, between two skeletal hands with a skull above. There are two bedrolls in the room: one on your right as you enter, the other under a dead bandit between the table and chest. The exit is in the southwestern corner.

The passage descends several flights of stairs to an unlocked gate at the bottom. Through the gate is a caged walkway high above the main chamber. A leveled draugr possessing a leveled bow and a melee weapon will be waiting on the far side of the bridge. On the far side, the passage turns south, and heads up more stairs. The iron door at the top leads to the room containing the word wall.

The room is guarded by two draugr; one is a leveled draugr, while the other is a leveled boss draugr or [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest"). The boss draugr will almost always be in front of the word wall. There are two [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") and two dead bandits on the floor between you and the wall. The second draugr is on a raised platform to the left as you enter. To reach it, you must climb stairs on the right, passing two opened upright sarcophagi and crossing a bridge. There is a third open sarcophagus by the second draugr containing a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and a random helmet. The boss draugr may raise the bandits to assist in the fight. There are several plinths around the room, but they only hold [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book").

Once you manage to defeat the draugr, the word wall teaches a word for the Disarm shout. There is an iron door to the west leading to a passage to a small room containing two large urns and an unlocked boss chest. A gate on your right is opened by a chain to the left of the chest. Stairs lead down from here and around the corner to the other barred door found previously, which opens into the first hallway you entered.

## Notes

- The two "Loot" [shadowmarks](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") only appear if [The Gray Cowl Returns!](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed.
- Two [quicksilver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") are on a cliff 200 feet northwest of the lair. The veins may be reached by heading to the right when exiting the lair and following the rocks to your right until you see a path up to the small plateau. Alternatively, go east on the mountain from [Duskglow Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Duskglow_Crevice "Skyrim:Duskglow Crevice") until you reach the ridge overlooking the entrance to the lair.

## Bugs

- In the large multi-level chamber near the start, there's a lit brazier in an alcove on the eastern wall of the ground floor. It is possible to jump behind this brazier and get stuck, with no legitimate way to escape.
  - Summoning an atronach beneath your feet, should you become trapped in this space, may slowly push you out with creative jumping and a little luck, allowing you to escape.
  -  You can use the `tcl` [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command to extricate yourself.
- The barred door will open from the wrong side, but, as the bar will still be in place, there is no way to raise the bar to go backwards through the ruin.
- The wall might not teach you a Word. This can prevent further information about Words of Power via the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards"), or [Letters from a Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_a_Friend "Skyrim:Letter from a Friend").
  -  The wall should teach a word for the Disarm shout. Check your shouts to confirm whether you knew the shout already, and if so, which word(s). Use the console command `teachword 0005fb95` to acquire the first word, or the command `teachword 0005fb96` to acquire the second word, or the command `teachword 0005fb97` to acquire the third word, as needed.
  -  You can clear the quest [The Words of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power") if received from the Greybeards by using the console command `SetStage FreeFormHighHrothgarA 20`.
  -  You can clear the quest [Shout - learn about word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Shout_-_learn_about_word_wall "Skyrim:Shout - learn about word wall") if received from a friend by using the console command `SetStage WICastMagic04 200`.
- After exiting the ruins through the shortcut, you may fall into a crevice with no way out. **?**
  - Fast travel to another location to escape.
- The interior orientation of the ruin does not match the exterior; the compass directions are rotated by 90 degrees. Exiting the main door shows you facing west, but after exiting you are facing south.

Sinderion's Field Laboratory

**Sinderion's Field Laboratory** is a small [Dwarven building](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") serving as [Sinderion's](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") alchemical foothold in the cavern. The laboratory can be found closest to the entrance to Blackreach from [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"). After descending the steps, you should be able to see the laboratory on the right.

## Related Quests

- **[A Return To Your Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots")**: Go where a [famous alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion "Skyrim:Sinderion") could not in order to aid ground-breaking research.

## Interior

Sinderion's remains can be found in the room, still clutching his [field journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Journal "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Journal"), his body riddled with dwarven arrows. This is where Sinderion eventually found himself after having been shown a sample of [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") by a passing adventurer during his time in [Skingrad](/wiki/Lore:Skingrad "Lore:Skingrad"), as his journal reveals. Reading the journal (or collecting crimson nirnroot from the plant in the room) will trigger a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Return_To_Your_Roots "Skyrim:A Return To Your Roots") to finish Sinderion's research.

Sinderion had set up a full research station in the laboratory, including an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), a rare-type [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[De Rerum Dirennis](/wiki/Skyrim:De_Rerum_Dirennis "Skyrim:De Rerum Dirennis")*, and thirty different [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), which are listed in the table below.

Other items of particular interest are a pair of [Leather Boots of Hauling](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots_of_Hauling "Skyrim:Leather Boots of Hauling") and an [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere"). There is also a knapsack, two chests, a [dwarven dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), three [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (one filled lesser soul gem, one empty greater soul gem, and one random soul gem), and three potions, in addition to a typical range of Dwemer household items and scrap metal.

| No. | Ingredient | No. | Ingredient | No. | Ingredient |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 3 | [Blue Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") | 1 | [Butterfly Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing") | 1 | [Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") |
| 3 | [Purple Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") | 1 | [Canis Root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") | 1 | [Honeycomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeycomb "Skyrim:Honeycomb") |
| 3 | [Red Mountain Flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 1 | [Charred Skeever Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") | 1 | [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") |
| 2 | [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") | 1 | [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") | 1 | [Luna Moth Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing") |
| 2 | [Falmer Ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear") | 1 | [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") | 1 | [Moon Sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar") |
| 2 | [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") | 1 | [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") | 1 | [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") |
| 1 | [Bear Claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Claws "Skyrim:Bear Claws") | 1 | [Ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm") | 1 | [Mudcrab Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin") |
| 1 | [Blue Dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing") | 1 | [Eye of Sabre Cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Eye_of_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Eye of Sabre Cat") | 1 | [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") |
| 1 | [Bone Meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") | 1 | [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") | 1 | [Sabre Cat Tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Tooth "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Tooth") |
| 1 | [Briar Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart") | 1 | [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") | 1 | [Torchbug Thorax](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") |

## Notes

- This can be an especially valuable location in [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode") while exploring [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") since there is a usable bed, cooking station, and safe storage.

## Bugs

- Taking the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") from this lab may render it permanently stuck in your inventory if the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane") has been started.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. Once the quest is complete, all related items can be discarded normally.
- If you have [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") as a follower, after leaving the laboratory, she will not follow you anymore and will instead just stand in front of the laboratory. Waiting or speaking to her will not help, but if you use one of the lifts, she will be teleported back to you and follow you as normal.
  -  Use `moveto player` when at least a few steps away from the laboratory's entrance.

## Maps

- 

  Sinderion's Field Laboratory

source_url: "https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim:Sivdur's_Respite"
title: "Skyrim:Sivdur's Respite"

Sivdur's Respite

**Sivdur's Respite** is a Nordic ruin located north of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). It is the final resting place of the Nord warrior [Sivdur](/wiki/Lore:Sivdur "Lore:Sivdur"). The ruins are currently inhabited by [Boethiah cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah_Cultist "Skyrim:Boethiah Cultist"). To fully enter the ruins you will need to have Sivdur's Amulet and Magrathi's Skull.

## Related Quests

- **[A Matter of Pride](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Matter_of_Pride "Skyrim:A Matter of Pride")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand "Skyrim:Goldbrand"): Obtain the legendary katana [Goldbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldbrand_(item) "Skyrim:Goldbrand (item)").

## Interior

The two tablets and holders.

The entrance of this area is a cave, with a Nordic ruin entrance being found further in. This Nordic entrance has three Boethiah cultists guarding it, once they are dispatched with, you can read the two etched tablets, with the left etched tablet stating:

:   *"I, Sivdur, warrior and defender of dragons, lie in rest here
    My amulet, the symbol of my valor
    Place it here so that I may have proof of my deeds in Sovngarde"*

The right etched tablet states:

:   *"Forever my nemesis, Magrathi, high priest and slayer of my brother
    His skull, the symbol of his betrayal
    Place it here, away from his kinsman, so that he may never find peace"*

Place Sivdur's amulet on the pedestal to the left of the door and Magrathi's skull on the pedestal to the right of the door in order to proceed. Before leaving the room look to the right of the pedestals for a knapsack and apothecary's satchel to loot.

Head down the stairs to a small room with a set of double doors, two unopened sarcophagi, and some draugr in it. Once they are defeated ignore the double doors for now and pull the chain to open the portcullis on the left side of the room. Directly across from the hall there is a burial urn. Take the hall to the left and you'll find an alcove with an ancient Nord bow and some arrows, another alcove with some potions, gems, a soul gem, and alchemical ingredients and at the end of the hall you'll find an expert-locked chest; the hall to the right leads to another small room with some more draugr in it. You'll find an urn and a random Spell Tome. Go back up to the previous room and beware the firetrap as you go through the set of double doors. Head down a short flight of stairs and go until you reach a dead end. Pull the chain to open the portcullis on your right to enter a room with a draugr to defeat. You'll find a soul gem and potion and another urn to loot. Head back across the hall and descend a spiral stairway until you reach a set of iron doors. Don't forget to check the alcoves for a potion and burial urn to loot along the way. The iron doors lead to Sivdur's Tomb.

Sivdur's honor guards

Enter the room and take the Goldbrand Katana from the table. Doing this will cause two of Sivdur's honor guards to attack you. Once they are defeated the sword is yours. Loot the boss level chest and urns in the room. There is no shortcut out of the cave so you will need to retrace your steps to leave. Be aware as you leave that when you reach the room with the two unopened sarcophagi they will open and you will need to fight a final two draugr in order to escape the tomb.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Sivdur%27s_Respite&action=edit).*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Morwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen "Skyrim:Morwen") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
2. Take [her mother's necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Bera%27s_Necklace "Skyrim:Bera's Necklace") to [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil") in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath").
3. Return to Morwen.

## Detailed Walkthrough

If you return to [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") after the quest [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal"), you may find [Morwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Morwen "Skyrim:Morwen") working near the forge. She may tell you, *"My mother was Skaal, but she left the village and I was born in Skyrim."* If you ask her why her mother left the village, she will tell you the whole story of her family. A trade ship from Skyrim struck ice off the coast near the village, and the Skaal took in the surviving sailors. Her mother, Bera, fell in love with one of the sailors—her father, Ulfarr—and eventually returned with him to Skyrim. However, Bera never returned to the village and died in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), where little Morwen was born.

If you are willing to give Morwen a hand, she will tell you that she came across a few of her mother's old things not long ago and among them was a necklace that her father gave to her mother when they were married. She believes it would be meaningful to place it upon her tombstone in Falkreath, as a symbol of her undying love and the great sacrifice she made for it. She wants you to deliver [her mother's necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Bera%27s_Necklace "Skyrim:Bera's Necklace") to the priest [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil"). After the conversation, Bera's necklace will be added into your inventory. If you haven't talked to [Gjalund Salt-Sage](/wiki/Skyrim:Gjalund_Salt-Sage "Skyrim:Gjalund Salt-Sage") about the passage back to Skyrim, a quest marker will appear at his location.

Travel to Falkreath and you may find Runil in Falkreath's [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)"). Talk to him about the request of Morwen of Skaal Village; he will recall the name. *"I knew her parents quite well, you know. Bera and Ulfarr were good people, very much in love."* Then he will be willing to grant her request. *"Bera's silver necklace. It was a wedding gift and she rarely took it off. I'll be glad to oblige. What a touching gesture, to display the symbol of her devotion in such a way."* He is sure it will bring joy to her parents as they walk in [Aetherius](/wiki/Lore:Aetherius "Lore:Aetherius"). Then he will take the necklace from your inventory.

Return to Morwen in Skaal Village, and she will be grateful. *"You've brought warmth to my heart, outsider, and I'm in your debt."* Then she will reward you with a [Nordic carved helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Helmet "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Helmet") and regard you as an ally to the Skaal. She will also become a potential [spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Notes

- You can steal the necklace back from Runil after giving it to him.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2SkaalVillageFreeform1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2SkaalVillageFreeform1`.

Skaal Village

**Skaal Village** is a [village](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim").

The village is home to the [Skaal tribe](/wiki/Lore:Skaal "Lore:Skaal"), who strive to live in harmony with nature in accordance with their worship of the [All-Maker](/wiki/Lore:All-Maker "Lore:All-Maker"). They live a simple existence in the frozen north of Solstheim, subsisting on hunting and minor agriculture, but are also familiar with the secrets of forging [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim").

The village's eight buildings circle the central well, with a communal [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and a meat preparation shed sheltering a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on either side of the well. All other crafting stations are found outside the houses of [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper"), [Deor Woodcutter](/wiki/Skyrim:Deor_Woodcutter "Skyrim:Deor Woodcutter"), and [Edla](/wiki/Skyrim:Edla "Skyrim:Edla"). Chief [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice")'s imposing greathall and shaman [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider")'s more modest hut are at the east end of the village, while the remaining residents' homes are to the west and north.

#### Dragonborn

- **[The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal")**: Find a way to free the citizens of Skaal Village.
- **[Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones")**: Use the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to cleanse each of the remaining [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones").

#### Side Quests

- **[Filial Bonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Filial_Bonds "Skyrim:Filial Bonds")**: Find [Wulf Wild-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Wulf_Wild-Blood "Skyrim:Wulf Wild-Blood")'s brother, [Torkild](/wiki/Skyrim:Torkild "Skyrim:Torkild"), who may have become a [werebear](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear").
- **[Lost Legacy](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legacy "Skyrim:Lost Legacy")**: Travel to [Vahlok's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Vahlok's Tomb") and defeat [Vahlok the Jailor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vahlok_the_Jailor "Skyrim:Vahlok the Jailor").
- **[A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim")**: Find a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") missing from Skaal Village.

[†](#note_Stalhrim)Only the first part of this quest is classed as miscellaneous, but both are documented on the same page.

## Notes

- Next to the village cooking pot hangs a unique [dead horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_(dead) "Skyrim:Horker (dead)").
- Next to the village cooking pot is an unusable bedroll. The closest places to sleep are [Haknir's Shoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Shoal "Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal") to the north-northwest, [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat") to the south-southeast, or [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall") to the south-southwest, depending on your progress in the quests [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") or [The Chief of Thirsk Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Chief_of_Thirsk_Hall "Skyrim:The Chief of Thirsk Hall").
- Skaal Village also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Skaal_Village "Bloodmoon:Skaal Village") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*. In *Bloodmoon*, the village has a unique architectural style similar to Thirsk. However, in *Dragonborn*, Thirsk still looks visually distinct, while the buildings in Skaal Village are repurposed from [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), albeit with an added layer of snow on the roofs.
- This wiki's current Skyrim satellite map displays Skaal Village in regular its state; the previous Solstheim satellite map displayed Skaal Village the way it did at the beginning of the *Dragonborn* storyline.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch") marks the charcoal pieces, dead salmon, and ice wolf pelt as owned by the village.

## Bugs

- The village residents will never sleep, as all beds in the village are incorrectly owned by [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- The village residents have crime detection and will call for guards if they witness a crime. However, they do not actually have guards or a jail and have no way of arresting you.

# Skyrim:Skaggi's House

## Overview

Skaggi's House

**Skaggi's House** is the home of [Skaggi Scar-Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi_Scar-Face "Skyrim:Skaggi Scar-Face") and [Sosia Tremellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Sosia_Tremellia "Skyrim:Sosia Tremellia").

It is the last house on the left on the approach to [Left Hand Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Left_Hand_Mine "Skyrim:Left Hand Mine"), next door to [Daighre's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Daighre%27s_House "Skyrim:Daighre's House").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Skaggi Scar-Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaggi_Scar-Face "Skyrim:Skaggi Scar-Face")  [Sosia Tremellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Sosia_Tremellia "Skyrim:Sosia Tremellia") |

### Exterior

It is a single story Dwemer style dwelling, with a novice-locked door. It is opposite the smelter outside of the mine. A [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") can be found wandering around outside.

### Skaggi's House

Skaggi's house interior

The house consists of a single room with a large fireplace on the east wall with two [cooking pots](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a third pot containing a [rabbit haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_Haunch "Skyrim:Rabbit Haunch") and [carrot](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). To the left of the fireplace, on the floor is a mead barrel and basket containing two sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), while to the right is a pile of firewood. Opposite the fireplace, coming out from the west wall is a large double bed with an end table to the right holding a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") and two bunches of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), one in a wooden bowl. To the left of the bed, on a ledge is a copy of *[Killing - Before You're Killed](/wiki/Skyrim:Killing_-_Before_You%27re_Killed "Skyrim:Killing - Before You're Killed")* and on the floor, in a bucket are copies of *[The Holds of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Holds_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:The Holds of Skyrim")* and *[The City of Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_City_of_Stone "Skyrim:The City of Stone")*. Against the south wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), while against the north wall is square wooden table and two chairs, with a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") on the table.

# Skyrim:Skilled Apprenticeship

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Retrieve a [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash") for [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") |
| Location(s): | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"): Blacksmith shop near the waterwheel south of [The Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure"), [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard") |
| Reward: | Free [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") Lesson, [Blood-Kin](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin "Skyrim:Blood-Kin") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol")) |
| ID: | FreeformMarkarthL |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |

Ghorza gra-Bagol needs your help with her apprentice

## Quick Walkthrough

The skill book in Fort Sungard Muster

1. Visit [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") at her blacksmith shop during business hours.
2. Retrieve the skill book *[Last Scabbard of Akrash](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash")*.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When visiting her shop during business hours, you can hear [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") berating the smithing skills of her hapless apprentice, [Tacitus Sallustius](/wiki/Skyrim:Tacitus_Sallustius "Skyrim:Tacitus Sallustius"). She mentions a skill book, *[Last Scabbard of Akrash](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash")*, that might teach him something.

The marker points to [Fort Sungard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard "Skyrim:Fort Sungard"), which is south of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). The fort is well guarded by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and the book is in [Fort Sungard Muster](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard_Muster "Skyrim:Fort Sungard Muster"). However, you do not need to retrieve this exact copy of the book; any copy will do. The other two locations are [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") and an unmarked area south-southeast of [Black-Briar Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Lodge "Skyrim:Black-Briar Lodge"). With the [Bloodchill Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, a copy can also be found on a shelf to the right of the [Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern")'s smithing area.

For retrieving the book, she will reward you with a free smithing lesson and will tell you that she is advising the [Orc Strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") that you can be trusted and that you should now be welcome in them.

## Quest Stages

| Skilled Apprenticeship (FreeformMarkarthL) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring The Last Scabbard of Akrash to Ghorza |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 20, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformMarkarthL stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformMarkarthL`.
